## Topic 4: Basic Algebra & Manipulation
*Algebraic expressions, like terms, expansion, factorisation* — 153 questions

### LIKE TERMS (Q1–35)

1. Simplify 7x + 3x.
   - **A) 10x** | B) 10x² | C) 21x | D) 4x
   - *7x and 3x are like terms. 7 + 3 = 10, so the answer is 10x.*

2. Simplify 9a − 4a.
   - **A) 5a** | B) 13a | C) 5 | D) 36a
   - *9a − 4a: subtract coefficients → 9 − 4 = 5, giving 5a.*

3. Simplify 4x + 3y − x + 2y.
   - **A) 3x + 5y** | B) 7x + 5y | C) 3x + y | D) 5x + 5y
   - *x terms: 4x − x = 3x. y terms: 3y + 2y = 5y. Answer: 3x + 5y.*

4. Simplify 6a − 2b + a − 3b.
   - **A) 7a − 5b** | B) 5a − 5b | C) 7a + b | D) 5a + b
   - *6a + a = 7a; −2b − 3b = −5b. Answer: 7a − 5b.*

5. Simplify 5m + 2n − 3m + n.
   - **A) 2m + 3n** | B) 8m + 3n | C) 2m + n | D) 2m − 3n
   - *5m − 3m = 2m; 2n + n = 3n. Answer: 2m + 3n.*

6. Simplify 8p − 3p + p.
   - **A) 6p** | B) 12p | C) 4p | D) 11p
   - *8p − 3p + p = (8 − 3 + 1)p = 6p.*

7. Simplify 2a + 5b + 3a − b.
   - **A) 5a + 4b** | B) 5a − 4b | C) 5a + 6b | D) 2a + 4b
   - *2a + 3a = 5a; 5b − b = 4b. Answer: 5a + 4b.*

8. Simplify 10x − 4x − 2x.
   - **A) 4x** | B) 8x | C) 6x | D) 16x
   - *10x − 4x − 2x = (10 − 4 − 2)x = 4x.*

9. Simplify 3ab + 2ab − ab.
   - **A) 4ab** | B) 6ab | C) 3ab | D) 2ab
   - *3 + 2 − 1 = 4, so 4ab.*

10. Simplify 7x² + 3x − 2x² + x.
   - **A) 5x² + 4x** | B) 10x² + 4x | C) 5x² + 2x | D) 9x² + 4x
   - *x² terms: 7 − 2 = 5, giving 5x². x terms: 3 + 1 = 4, giving 4x. Answer: 5x² + 4x.*

11. Which of the following are like terms?
   - A) 3x and 3y | B) 5a and 5a² | C) 4xy and 4x | **D) 6p and 2p**
   - *Like terms must have exactly the same variable(s) and power(s). 6p and 2p both have variable p to power 1.*

12. Simplify 4x + 2 − x − 5.
   - **A) 3x − 3** | B) 5x − 3 | C) 3x + 7 | D) 3x − 7
   - *x terms: 4x − x = 3x. Constants: 2 − 5 = −3. Answer: 3x − 3.*

13. Simplify 6y − 3 + 2y + 7.
   - **A) 8y + 4** | B) 8y − 4 | C) 4y + 4 | D) 8y + 10
   - *y terms: 6y + 2y = 8y. Constants: −3 + 7 = 4. Answer: 8y + 4.*

14. Simplify 9k − 6k + 2.
   - **A) 3k + 2** | B) 5k + 2 | C) 3k − 2 | D) 15k + 2
   - *9k − 6k = 3k. The constant 2 stays. Answer: 3k + 2.*

15. Simplify 5a + 3b − 5a + b.
   - **A) 4b** | B) 6b | C) 10a + 4b | D) 0 + 4b
   - *5a − 5a = 0. 3b + b = 4b. Answer: 4b.*

16. Simplify 2x + 3y + 4z − x − y.
   - **A) x + 2y + 4z** | B) x + 4y + 4z | C) 3x + 2y + 4z | D) x + 2y − 4z
   - *x: 2x − x = x. y: 3y − y = 2y. z: 4z unchanged. Answer: x + 2y + 4z.*

17. Simplify 12m − 7m.
   - **A) 5m** | B) 19m | C) 5 | D) 84m
   - *12m − 7m = (12 − 7)m = 5m.*

18. Simplify −3x + 8x.
   - **A) 5x** | B) 11x | C) −5x | D) −24x
   - *−3x + 8x = (−3 + 8)x = 5x.*

19. Simplify 4p − 7p.
   - **A) −3p** | B) 3p | C) −11p | D) 11p
   - *4p − 7p = (4 − 7)p = −3p.*

20. Simplify 3a² + 5a².
   - **A) 8a²** | B) 8a⁴ | C) 15a² | D) 8a
   - *3a² + 5a² = 8a². The variable and power don't change when combining like terms.*

21. Simplify 6x² − 4x².
   - **A) 2x²** | B) 10x² | C) 2x | D) 6x²
   - *6x² − 4x² = (6 − 4)x² = 2x².*

22. Simplify 5xy − 2xy + xy.
   - **A) 4xy** | B) 7xy | C) 3xy | D) 8xy
   - *5 − 2 + 1 = 4, so 4xy.*

23. Simplify 3a + 4b + 2a − 6b + 1.
   - **A) 5a − 2b + 1** | B) 5a + 10b + 1 | C) a − 2b + 1 | D) 5a − 2b − 1
   - *a terms: 3a + 2a = 5a. b terms: 4b − 6b = −2b. Constant: 1. Answer: 5a − 2b + 1.*

24. Simplify 7 − 3x + 2x − 1.
   - **A) −x + 6** | B) −5x + 6 | C) x + 6 | D) x + 8
   - *x terms: −3x + 2x = −x. Constants: 7 − 1 = 6. Answer: −x + 6.*

25. Simplify 2(x) + 3(x) without expanding fully — treat as like terms.
   - **A) 5x** | B) 6x | C) 5x² | D) 2x + 3x
   - *2x and 3x are like terms: 2x + 3x = 5x.*

26. Simplify 4ab − ab + 3ab.
   - **A) 6ab** | B) 8ab | C) 7ab | D) 3ab
   - *4 − 1 + 3 = 6, so 6ab.*

27. Simplify 10x − 3 − 4x + 8.
   - **A) 6x + 5** | B) 6x − 5 | C) 14x + 5 | D) 6x + 11
   - *x terms: 10x − 4x = 6x. Constants: −3 + 8 = 5. Answer: 6x + 5.*

28. Simplify 3p + 4q − 2p + q − 5.
   - **A) p + 5q − 5** | B) p + 3q − 5 | C) 5p + 5q − 5 | D) p + 5q + 5
   - *p: 3p − 2p = p. q: 4q + q = 5q. Constant: −5. Answer: p + 5q − 5.*

29. Simplify 8k + 3j − 5k − 3j.
   - **A) 3k** | B) 3k + 6j | C) 13k | D) 3k − 6j
   - *k terms: 8k − 5k = 3k. j terms: 3j − 3j = 0. Answer: 3k.*

30. Simplify 6n − n.
   - **A) 5n** | B) 6 | C) 6n | D) −n
   - *6n − n = (6 − 1)n = 5n. Remember: n = 1n.*

31. Simplify a + a + a + a.
   - **A) 4a** | B) a⁴ | C) 4 | D) a + 4
   - *a + a + a + a = 4 × a = 4a.*

32. Simplify 5x² + 3x + 2x² − x.
   - **A) 7x² + 2x** | B) 8x² + 2x | C) 7x² + 4x | D) 7x + 2x²
   - *x² terms: 5 + 2 = 7, giving 7x². x terms: 3 − 1 = 2, giving 2x. Answer: 7x² + 2x.*

33. Simplify 4mn + 3m − mn + 2m.
   - **A) 3mn + 5m** | B) 5mn + 5m | C) 3mn + m | D) 7mn + 5m
   - *mn terms: 4mn − mn = 3mn. m terms: 3m + 2m = 5m. Answer: 3mn + 5m.*

34. Simplify −2x − 3x + 10.
   - **A) −5x + 10** | B) 5x + 10 | C) −5x − 10 | D) −x + 10
   - *−2x − 3x = −5x. Constant 10 unchanged. Answer: −5x + 10.*

35. Simplify 3a − (−2a).
   - **A) 5a** | B) a | C) −5a | D) a²
   - *Subtracting a negative is addition: 3a − (−2a) = 3a + 2a = 5a.*

### EXPANSION — single bracket (Q36–65)

36. Expand 3(x + 4).
   - A) 3x + 4 | B) 3x + 7 | **C) 3x + 12** | D) x + 12
   - *3 × x = 3x; 3 × 4 = 12. Answer: 3x + 12.*

37. Expand −2(y − 5).
   - A) −2y − 10 | **B) −2y + 10** | C) 2y − 10 | D) 2y + 5
   - *−2 × y = −2y; −2 × −5 = +10. Answer: −2y + 10.*

38. Expand 5(2a + 3).
   - A) 10a + 3 | B) 10a + 8 | **C) 10a + 15** | D) 7a + 15
   - *5 × 2a = 10a; 5 × 3 = 15. Answer: 10a + 15.*

39. Expand 4(3x − 2).
   - A) 12x − 2 | **B) 12x − 8** | C) 7x − 8 | D) 12x + 8
   - *4 × 3x = 12x; 4 × −2 = −8. Answer: 12x − 8.*

40. Expand x(x + 5).
   - A) x + 5 | B) x² + 5 | **C) x² + 5x** | D) 2x + 5
   - *x × x = x²; x × 5 = 5x. Answer: x² + 5x.*

41. Expand 2x(3x − 4).
   - A) 6x² − 4 | **B) 6x² − 8x** | C) 5x − 8x | D) 6x − 8
   - *2x × 3x = 6x²; 2x × −4 = −8x. Answer: 6x² − 8x.*

42. Expand −3(2x + 1).
   - A) −6x + 1 | B) −6x − 1 | **C) −6x − 3** | D) 6x − 3
   - *−3 × 2x = −6x; −3 × 1 = −3. Answer: −6x − 3.*

43. Expand 7(a − b).
   - A) 7a − b | B) a − 7b | **C) 7a − 7b** | D) 7a + 7b
   - *7 × a = 7a; 7 × −b = −7b. Answer: 7a − 7b.*

44. Expand −(3x − 4).
   - A) −3x − 4 | B) 3x − 4 | **C) −3x + 4** | D) 3x + 4
   - *−1 × 3x = −3x; −1 × −4 = +4. Answer: −3x + 4.*

45. Expand 6(2 − x).
   - A) 12 − x | **B) 12 − 6x** | C) 2 − 6x | D) 12 + 6x
   - *6 × 2 = 12; 6 × −x = −6x. Answer: 12 − 6x.*

46. Expand a(a + 1).
   - A) a + 1 | B) a² + 1 | **C) a² + a** | D) 2a + 1
   - *a × a = a²; a × 1 = a. Answer: a² + a.*

47. Expand 3x(x − 2).
   - A) 3x − 6 | B) 3x² − 6 | **C) 3x² − 6x** | D) 3x² + 6x
   - *3x × x = 3x²; 3x × −2 = −6x. Answer: 3x² − 6x.*

48. Expand 2(3 + 4y).
   - A) 5 + 4y | B) 6 + 4y | **C) 6 + 8y** | D) 10y
   - *2 × 3 = 6; 2 × 4y = 8y. Answer: 6 + 8y.*

49. Expand 5a(a + 3).
   - A) 5a + 3 | B) 5a² + 3 | **C) 5a² + 15a** | D) 5a² + 15
   - *5a × a = 5a²; 5a × 3 = 15a. Answer: 5a² + 15a.*

50. Expand −4(x − 3).
   - A) −4x − 12 | **B) −4x + 12** | C) 4x − 12 | D) 4x + 12
   - *−4 × x = −4x; −4 × −3 = +12. Answer: −4x + 12.*

51. Expand 3(2p + 5q).
   - A) 6p + 5q | B) 5p + 8q | **C) 6p + 15q** | D) 6p + 15
   - *3 × 2p = 6p; 3 × 5q = 15q. Answer: 6p + 15q.*

52. Expand 2y(y − 4).
   - A) 2y − 8 | B) 2y² − 4 | **C) 2y² − 8y** | D) 2y² + 8y
   - *2y × y = 2y²; 2y × −4 = −8y. Answer: 2y² − 8y.*

53. Expand −5(−2x + 1).
   - **A) 10x − 5** | B) −10x + 5 | C) 10x + 5 | D) −10x − 5
   - *−5 × −2x = +10x; −5 × 1 = −5. Answer: 10x − 5.*

54. Expand 4(x² + 3x − 1).
   - A) 4x² + 3x − 4 | B) 4x² + 12x − 1 | **C) 4x² + 12x − 4** | D) x² + 12x − 4
   - *4 × x² = 4x²; 4 × 3x = 12x; 4 × −1 = −4. Answer: 4x² + 12x − 4.*

55. Expand 3m(2m + n).
   - A) 6m + 3mn | **B) 6m² + 3mn** | C) 6m² + mn | D) 6m² + 3n
   - *3m × 2m = 6m²; 3m × n = 3mn. Answer: 6m² + 3mn.*

56. Expand 2(5 − 3k).
   - A) 10 − 3k | **B) 10 − 6k** | C) 7 − 6k | D) 10 + 6k
   - *2 × 5 = 10; 2 × −3k = −6k. Answer: 10 − 6k.*

57. Expand x(2x − y).
   - A) 2x − xy | **B) 2x² − xy** | C) 2x² − y | D) x² − xy
   - *x × 2x = 2x²; x × −y = −xy. Answer: 2x² − xy.*

58. Expand −2a(3a − 5).
   - A) −6a² − 10a | **B) −6a² + 10a** | C) 6a² − 10a | D) 6a² + 10a
   - *−2a × 3a = −6a²; −2a × −5 = +10a. Answer: −6a² + 10a.*

59. Expand 9(x + y − 2).
   - A) 9x + 9y − 2 | B) 9x + y − 18 | **C) 9x + 9y − 18** | D) x + 9y − 18
   - *9 × x = 9x; 9 × y = 9y; 9 × −2 = −18. Answer: 9x + 9y − 18.*

60. Expand 3b(b + 4).
   - A) 3b + 4 | B) 3b² + 4 | **C) 3b² + 12b** | D) 3b² + 12
   - *3b × b = 3b²; 3b × 4 = 12b. Answer: 3b² + 12b.*

61. Expand −(5a + 3b).
   - A) 5a + 3b | **B) −5a − 3b** | C) −5a + 3b | D) 5a − 3b
   - *Multiply each term by −1: −1 × 5a = −5a; −1 × 3b = −3b. Answer: −5a − 3b.*

62. Expand 4k(k − 1).
   - A) 4k − 4 | B) 4k² − 1 | **C) 4k² − 4k** | D) 4k² + 4k
   - *4k × k = 4k²; 4k × −1 = −4k. Answer: 4k² − 4k.*

63. Expand 6(4a − 3b + 2).
   - A) 24a − 3b + 2 | **B) 24a − 18b + 12** | C) 24a − 18b + 2 | D) 10a − 3b + 8
   - *6 × 4a = 24a; 6 × −3b = −18b; 6 × 2 = 12. Answer: 24a − 18b + 12.*

64. Expand 2n(3 − n).
   - A) 6n − n² | **B) 6n − 2n²** | C) 6 − 2n² | D) 6n − 2n
   - *2n × 3 = 6n; 2n × −n = −2n². Answer: 6n − 2n².*

65. Expand −3x(x + 4).
   - A) −3x² + 12 | **B) −3x² − 12x** | C) 3x² − 12x | D) −3x² + 12x
   - *−3x × x = −3x²; −3x × 4 = −12x. Answer: −3x² − 12x.*

### EXPAND AND SIMPLIFY (Q66–95)

66. Expand 5(3 − 2x + x²).
   - **A) 15 − 10x + 5x²** | B) 15 − 2x + x² | C) 15 − 10x + x² | D) 5 − 10x + 5x²
   - *5 × 3 = 15; 5 × −2x = −10x; 5 × x² = 5x². Answer: 15 − 10x + 5x².*

67. Expand and simplify 2(3a + 1) + 4(a − 2).
   - **A) 10a − 6** | B) 10a + 6 | C) 10a − 2 | D) 14a − 6
   - *2(3a+1) = 6a+2; 4(a−2) = 4a−8. Combine: 10a − 6.*

68. Expand and simplify 3(x + 2) + 2(x + 5).
   - **A) 5x + 16** | B) 5x + 7 | C) 6x + 16 | D) 5x + 14
   - *3(x+2) = 3x+6; 2(x+5) = 2x+10. Combine: 5x + 16.*

69. Expand and simplify 4(2x − 1) − 3(x + 2).
   - **A) 5x − 10** | B) 5x − 2 | C) 5x + 10 | D) 8x − 10
   - *4(2x−1) = 8x−4; 3(x+2) = 3x+6. 8x−4 − (3x+6) = 5x − 10.*

70. Expand and simplify 2(a + 3) + 3(a − 1).
   - **A) 5a + 3** | B) 5a + 6 | C) 5a − 3 | D) 2a + 3
   - *2(a+3) = 2a+6; 3(a−1) = 3a−3. Combine: 5a + 3.*

71. Expand and simplify 5(x − 2) − 2(x − 4).
   - **A) 3x − 2** | B) 3x − 18 | C) 7x − 2 | D) 3x + 2
   - *5(x−2) = 5x−10; 2(x−4) = 2x−8. 5x−10 − 2x+8 = 3x − 2.*

72. Expand and simplify 3(2b + 4) − 4(b − 1).
   - **A) 2b + 16** | B) 2b + 12 | C) 2b + 8 | D) 6b + 16
   - *3(2b+4) = 6b+12; 4(b−1) = 4b−4. 6b+12 − 4b+4 = 2b + 16.*

73. Expand and simplify 2(3x + 1) − (x + 5).
   - **A) 5x − 3** | B) 5x + 3 | C) 7x − 3 | D) 7x + 3
   - *2(3x+1) = 6x+2; −(x+5) = −x−5. 6x+2 − x−5 = 5x − 3.*

74. Expand and simplify 4(p + q) + 2(p − q).
   - **A) 6p + 2q** | B) 6p − 2q | C) 6p + 6q | D) 2p + 6q
   - *4(p+q) = 4p+4q; 2(p−q) = 2p−2q. Combine: 6p + 2q.*

75. Expand and simplify 3(2x − y) − 2(x − 3y).
   - **A) 4x + 3y** | B) 4x − 7y | C) 8x + 3y | D) 4x + 7y
   - *3(2x−y) = 6x−3y; −2(x−3y) = −2x+6y. Add: 6x−3y − 2x+6y = 4x + 3y.*

76. Expand and simplify 5(a − 3) + 3(a + 5).
   - **A) 8a** | B) 8a + 15 | C) 8a − 15 | D) 8a + 30
   - *5(a−3) = 5a−15; 3(a+5) = 3a+15. Combine: 8a + 0 = 8a.*

77. Expand and simplify 2(x + y) − 3(x − y).
   - **A) −x + 5y** | B) −x − 5y | C) 5x + y | D) x + 5y
   - *2(x+y) = 2x+2y; −3(x−y) = −3x+3y. Combine: −x + 5y.*

78. Expand and simplify 4(3x + 2) + 2(x − 6).
   - **A) 14x − 4** | B) 14x + 4 | C) 12x − 4 | D) 14x + 20
   - *4(3x+2) = 12x+8; 2(x−6) = 2x−12. Combine: 14x − 4.*

79. Expand and simplify 3(k − 4) − 2(k − 6).
   - **A) k** | B) k − 24 | C) k + 24 | D) 5k + 24
   - *3(k−4) = 3k−12; −2(k−6) = −2k+12. Combine: k + 0 = k.*

80. Expand and simplify 2(5m + 3) − 4(2m − 1).
   - **A) 2m + 10** | B) 2m − 10 | C) 2m + 2 | D) 10m + 10
   - *2(5m+3) = 10m+6; 4(2m−1) = 8m−4. 10m+6 − 8m+4 = 2m + 10.*

81. Expand and simplify 3(2x + 1) + 2(4x − 3).
   - **A) 14x − 3** | B) 14x + 3 | C) 14x − 9 | D) 10x + 3
   - *3(2x+1) = 6x+3; 2(4x−3) = 8x−6. Combine: 14x − 3.*

82. Expand and simplify −2(3a − 4) + 5(a + 2).
   - **A) −a + 18** | B) −a − 18 | C) −a + 2 | D) a + 18
   - *−2(3a−4) = −6a+8; 5(a+2) = 5a+10. Combine: −a + 18.*

83. Expand and simplify 6(x + 1) − 3(2x + 1).
   - **A) 3** | B) 0 + 3 | C) −6x + 3 | D) 6x + 3
   - *6(x+1) = 6x+6; 3(2x+1) = 6x+3. 6x+6 − 6x−3 = 3.*

84. Expand and simplify 4(2a + 3b) − 2(a + b).
   - **A) 6a + 10b** | B) 6a − 10b | C) 8a + 10b | D) 6a + 12b
   - *4(2a+3b) = 8a+12b; 2(a+b) = 2a+2b. 8a+12b − 2a−2b = 6a + 10b.*

85. Expand and simplify 3(x − 2y) + 2(3x + y).
   - **A) 9x − 4y** | B) 9x + 4y | C) 9x − 8y | D) 3x − 4y
   - *3(x−2y) = 3x−6y; 2(3x+y) = 6x+2y. Combine: 9x − 4y.*

86. Expand and simplify 5(2x − 1) − 3(3x + 2).
   - **A) x − 11** | B) x + 11 | C) x − 1 | D) 11x − 11
   - *5(2x−1) = 10x−5; 3(3x+2) = 9x+6. 10x−5 − 9x−6 = x − 11.*

87. Expand and simplify 2(4p − 3) + 3(p + 2).
   - **A) 11p** | B) 11p + 5 | C) 11p − 5 | D) 11p + 1
   - *2(4p−3) = 8p−6; 3(p+2) = 3p+6. Combine: 11p + 0 = 11p.*

88. Expand and simplify 4(3x − 2) − 2(5x − 1).
   - **A) 2x − 6** | B) 2x + 6 | C) 2x − 10 | D) 12x − 6
   - *4(3x−2) = 12x−8; 2(5x−1) = 10x−2. 12x−8 − 10x+2 = 2x − 6.*

89. Expand and simplify 3(a + b) + 4(a − b).
   - **A) 7a − b** | B) 7a + b | C) 7a − 7b | D) a − b
   - *3(a+b) = 3a+3b; 4(a−b) = 4a−4b. Combine: 7a − b.*

90. Expand and simplify 2(3n + 4) + 3(n − 2).
   - **A) 9n + 2** | B) 9n − 2 | C) 9n + 8 | D) 6n + 2
   - *2(3n+4) = 6n+8; 3(n−2) = 3n−6. Combine: 9n + 2.*

91. Expand and simplify 5(2x + 3) − 2(4x − 1).
   - **A) 2x + 17** | B) 2x − 17 | C) 18x + 17 | D) 2x + 13
   - *5(2x+3) = 10x+15; 2(4x−1) = 8x−2. 10x+15 − 8x+2 = 2x + 17.*

92. Expand and simplify 3(x + 4) − (x − 2).
   - **A) 2x + 14** | B) 2x + 10 | C) 2x + 2 | D) 4x + 14
   - *3(x+4) = 3x+12; −(x−2) = −x+2. Combine: 2x + 14.*

93. Expand and simplify 2x(x + 3) + x(x − 1).
   - **A) 3x² + 5x** | B) 3x² + 7x | C) 2x² + 5x | D) 3x² − 5x
   - *2x(x+3) = 2x²+6x; x(x−1) = x²−x. Combine: 3x² + 5x.*

94. Expand and simplify a(2a + 1) + 3(a − 4).
   - **A) 2a² + 4a − 12** | B) 2a² + a − 12 | C) 2a² + 4a + 12 | D) 2a + 4a − 12
   - *a(2a+1) = 2a²+a; 3(a−4) = 3a−12. Combine: 2a² + 4a − 12.*

95. Expand and simplify 3(2m − 1) − 2(m + 3).
   - **A) 4m − 9** | B) 4m + 9 | C) 4m − 3 | D) 8m − 9
   - *3(2m−1) = 6m−3; 2(m+3) = 2m+6. 6m−3 − 2m−6 = 4m − 9.*

### FACTORISATION (Q96–125)

96. Expand and simplify 4(x − 2) + 3(2 − x).
   - **A) x − 2** | B) x + 2 | C) 7x − 2 | D) x − 14
   - *4(x−2) = 4x−8; 3(2−x) = 6−3x. 4x−8 + 6−3x = x − 2.*

97. Expand and simplify 2(3x − 4) − 3(x − 2) + x.
   - **A) 4x − 2** | B) 4x + 2 | C) 10x − 2 | D) 4x − 10
   - *6x−8 − 3x+6 + x = 4x − 2.*

98. Factorise 6x + 9.
   - **A) 3(2x + 3)** | B) 6(x + 3) | C) 3(2x + 9) | D) 9(x + 1)
   - *HCF of 6 and 9 is 3. 6x ÷ 3 = 2x; 9 ÷ 3 = 3. Answer: 3(2x + 3).*

99. Factorise 4a² − 8a.
   - A) 4(a² − 8) | **B) 4a(a − 2)** | C) 2a(2a − 4) | D) 4a(a² − 2)
   - *HCF is 4a. 4a² ÷ 4a = a; −8a ÷ 4a = −2. Answer: 4a(a − 2).*

100. Factorise 5xy + 10y.
   - **A) 5y(x + 2)** | B) 5x(y + 2) | C) 10y(x + 1) | D) 5(xy + 2y)
   - *HCF is 5y. 5xy ÷ 5y = x; 10y ÷ 5y = 2. Answer: 5y(x + 2).*

101. Factorise 12m + 8.
   - **A) 4(3m + 2)** | B) 4(3m + 8) | C) 2(6m + 4) | D) 8(m + 1)
   - *HCF of 12 and 8 is 4. 12m ÷ 4 = 3m; 8 ÷ 4 = 2. Answer: 4(3m + 2).*

102. Factorise 15x − 10.
   - **A) 5(3x − 2)** | B) 5(3x − 10) | C) 10(x − 1) | D) 15(x − 1)
   - *HCF of 15 and 10 is 5. 15x ÷ 5 = 3x; 10 ÷ 5 = 2. Answer: 5(3x − 2).*

103. Factorise 7a + 7b.
   - A) 7(a − b) | **B) 7(a + b)** | C) a(7 + b) | D) 14(a + b)
   - *HCF is 7. 7a ÷ 7 = a; 7b ÷ 7 = b. Answer: 7(a + b).*

104. Factorise 9x² − 6x.
   - A) 3x(3x − 6) | **B) 3x(3x − 2)** | C) x(9x − 6) | D) 6x(x − 1)
   - *HCF is 3x. 9x² ÷ 3x = 3x; −6x ÷ 3x = −2. Answer: 3x(3x − 2).*

105. Factorise 8p + 12q.
   - **A) 4(2p + 3q)** | B) 4(2p + 12q) | C) 2(4p + 6q) | D) 8(p + q)
   - *HCF of 8 and 12 is 4. 8p ÷ 4 = 2p; 12q ÷ 4 = 3q. Answer: 4(2p + 3q).*

106. Factorise 3x² + 6x.
   - A) 3x(x + 6) | **B) 3x(x + 2)** | C) 3(x² + 2x) | D) 6x(x + 1)
   - *HCF is 3x. 3x² ÷ 3x = x; 6x ÷ 3x = 2. Answer: 3x(x + 2).*

107. Factorise 20ab − 15a.
   - **A) 5a(4b − 3)** | B) 5(4ab − 3a) | C) a(20b − 15) | D) 5a(4b − 15)
   - *HCF is 5a. 20ab ÷ 5a = 4b; −15a ÷ 5a = −3. Answer: 5a(4b − 3).*

108. Factorise 2x + 4.
   - A) 2(x + 4) | **B) 2(x + 2)** | C) 4(x + 1) | D) x(2 + 4)
   - *HCF is 2. 2x ÷ 2 = x; 4 ÷ 2 = 2. Answer: 2(x + 2).*

109. Factorise 14y − 21.
   - **A) 7(2y − 3)** | B) 7(2y − 21) | C) 14(y − 1) | D) 3(y − 7)
   - *HCF of 14 and 21 is 7. 14y ÷ 7 = 2y; 21 ÷ 7 = 3. Answer: 7(2y − 3).*

110. Factorise 10a² + 5a.
   - **A) 5a(2a + 1)** | B) 5a(2a + 5) | C) 5(2a + a) | D) 10a(a + 1)
   - *HCF is 5a. 10a² ÷ 5a = 2a; 5a ÷ 5a = 1. Answer: 5a(2a + 1).*

111. Factorise 6m − 18n.
   - **A) 6(m − 3n)** | B) 6(m − 18n) | C) 3(2m − 6n) | D) 18(m − n)
   - *HCF of 6 and 18 is 6. 6m ÷ 6 = m; 18n ÷ 6 = 3n. Answer: 6(m − 3n).*

112. Factorise 4x² + 8xy.
   - **A) 4x(x + 2y)** | B) 4x(x + 8y) | C) 4(x² + 2y) | D) 8x(x + y)
   - *HCF is 4x. 4x² ÷ 4x = x; 8xy ÷ 4x = 2y. Answer: 4x(x + 2y).*

113. Factorise 3a + 6b − 9c.
   - **A) 3(a + 2b − 3c)** | B) 3(a + 6b − 9c) | C) 9(a + 2b − c) | D) 3(a + 2b − 9c)
   - *HCF is 3. 3a ÷ 3 = a; 6b ÷ 3 = 2b; 9c ÷ 3 = 3c. Answer: 3(a + 2b − 3c).*

114. Factorise 16x − 24.
   - **A) 8(2x − 3)** | B) 4(4x − 6) | C) 8(2x − 24) | D) 16(x − 1)
   - *HCF of 16 and 24 is 8. 16x ÷ 8 = 2x; 24 ÷ 8 = 3. Answer: 8(2x − 3).*

115. Factorise 5ab + 15b.
   - **A) 5b(a + 3)** | B) 5b(a + 15) | C) 5(ab + 3b) | D) b(5a + 15)
   - *HCF is 5b. 5ab ÷ 5b = a; 15b ÷ 5b = 3. Answer: 5b(a + 3).*

116. Factorise 6x²y + 9xy.
   - **A) 3xy(2x + 3)** | B) 3xy(2x + 9) | C) 3x(2xy + 3y) | D) 9xy(x + 1)
   - *HCF is 3xy. 6x²y ÷ 3xy = 2x; 9xy ÷ 3xy = 3. Answer: 3xy(2x + 3).*

117. Factorise 25a − 15.
   - **A) 5(5a − 3)** | B) 5(5a − 15) | C) 25(a − 1) | D) 15(a − 1)
   - *HCF of 25 and 15 is 5. 25a ÷ 5 = 5a; 15 ÷ 5 = 3. Answer: 5(5a − 3).*

118. Factorise 8m²n − 12mn².
   - **A) 4mn(2m − 3n)** | B) 4mn(2m − 12n) | C) 4m(2mn − 3n²) | D) mn(8m − 12n)
   - *HCF is 4mn. 8m²n ÷ 4mn = 2m; 12mn² ÷ 4mn = 3n. Answer: 4mn(2m − 3n).*

119. Factorise 2x + 10.
   - **A) 2(x + 5)** | B) 2(x + 10) | C) 10(x + 1) | D) 2x(1 + 5)
   - *HCF is 2. 2x ÷ 2 = x; 10 ÷ 2 = 5. Answer: 2(x + 5).*

120. Factorise 18p + 24q.
   - **A) 6(3p + 4q)** | B) 6(3p + 24q) | C) 3(6p + 8q) | D) 18(p + q)
   - *HCF of 18 and 24 is 6. 18p ÷ 6 = 3p; 24q ÷ 6 = 4q. Answer: 6(3p + 4q).*

121. Factorise 7x² − 14x.
   - **A) 7x(x − 2)** | B) 7x(x − 14) | C) 7(x² − 2x) | D) 14x(x − 1)
   - *HCF is 7x. 7x² ÷ 7x = x; 14x ÷ 7x = 2. Answer: 7x(x − 2).*

122. Factorise 4a + 4b + 4c.
   - **A) 4(a + b + c)** | B) 4(a + b + 4c) | C) a(4 + b + c) | D) 4a(1 + b + c)
   - *HCF is 4. Divide each term: a + b + c. Answer: 4(a + b + c).*

123. Factorise 10xy − 5x.
   - **A) 5x(2y − 1)** | B) 5x(2y − 5) | C) 5(2xy − x) | D) x(10y − 5)
   - *HCF is 5x. 10xy ÷ 5x = 2y; 5x ÷ 5x = 1. Answer: 5x(2y − 1).*

124. Factorise 3n² + 9n.
   - **A) 3n(n + 3)** | B) 3n(n + 9) | C) n(3n + 9) | D) 9n(n + 1)
   - *HCF is 3n. 3n² ÷ 3n = n; 9n ÷ 3n = 3. Answer: 3n(n + 3).*

125. Factorise 15ab − 20a.
   - **A) 5a(3b − 4)** | B) 5a(3b − 20) | C) a(15b − 20) | D) 5(3ab − 4a)
   - *HCF is 5a. 15ab ÷ 5a = 3b; 20a ÷ 5a = 4. Answer: 5a(3b − 4).*

### SUBSTITUTION (Q126–150)

126. Factorise 12x + 18y − 6.
   - **A) 6(2x + 3y − 1)** | B) 6(2x + 3y − 6) | C) 3(4x + 6y − 2) | D) 6(2x + 18y − 1)
   - *HCF is 6. 12x ÷ 6 = 2x; 18y ÷ 6 = 3y; 6 ÷ 6 = 1. Answer: 6(2x + 3y − 1).*

127. Factorise 4p² + 6pq.
   - **A) 2p(2p + 3q)** | B) 2p(2p + 6q) | C) p(4p + 6q) | D) 4p(p + q)
   - *HCF is 2p. 4p² ÷ 2p = 2p; 6pq ÷ 2p = 3q. Answer: 2p(2p + 3q).*

128. Which is the fully factorised form of 6x + 12?
   - A) 2(3x + 6) | B) 3(2x + 4) | **C) 6(x + 2)** | D) x(6 + 12)
   - *HCF of 6 and 12 is 6. 6x ÷ 6 = x; 12 ÷ 6 = 2. Fully factorised: 6(x + 2). Options A and B are partially factorised.*

129. If x = 4, find 3x − 5.
   - **A) 7** | B) 17 | C) 12 | D) 2
   - *3(4) − 5 = 12 − 5 = 7.*

130. If a = 3 and b = −2, find 2a² − 3b.
   - **A) 24** | B) 12 | C) 18 | D) 0
   - *2(3)² − 3(−2) = 2(9) + 6 = 18 + 6 = 24.*

131. If x = 2, find 5x + 3.
   - **A) 13** | B) 11 | C) 10 | D) 16
   - *5(2) + 3 = 10 + 3 = 13.*

132. If y = −3, find 4y + 7.
   - **A) −5** | B) 19 | C) −19 | D) 5
   - *4(−3) + 7 = −12 + 7 = −5.*

133. If p = 5 and q = 2, find 3p − 4q.
   - **A) 7** | B) 23 | C) −7 | D) 22
   - *3(5) − 4(2) = 15 − 8 = 7.*

134. If a = 0, find 6a² + 3a − 9.
   - **A) −9** | B) 9 | C) 0 | D) 3
   - *6(0)² + 3(0) − 9 = 0 + 0 − 9 = −9.*

135. If x = 3, find x².
   - **A) 9** | B) 6 | C) 3 | D) 27
   - *x² = 3² = 9.*

136. If m = 2 and n = 5, find mn + m.
   - **A) 12** | B) 10 | C) 14 | D) 7
   - *mn + m = 2(5) + 2 = 10 + 2 = 12.*

137. If x = −1, find x³.
   - **A) −1** | B) 1 | C) −3 | D) 3
   - *(−1)³ = −1 × −1 × −1 = −1.*

138. If a = 4, find 3(a − 2).
   - **A) 6** | B) 4 | C) 10 | D) 14
   - *3(4 − 2) = 3(2) = 6.*

139. If x = 5 and y = −2, find x + y.
   - **A) 3** | B) 7 | C) −3 | D) 10
   - *5 + (−2) = 5 − 2 = 3.*

140. If k = 3, find 2k² − k.
   - **A) 15** | B) 21 | C) 9 | D) 6
   - *2(3)² − 3 = 2(9) − 3 = 18 − 3 = 15.*

141. If a = −2 and b = 3, find a² + b.
   - **A) 7** | B) 1 | C) −1 | D) 11
   - *(−2)² + 3 = 4 + 3 = 7.*

142. If x = ½, find 4x + 6.
   - **A) 8** | B) 6 | C) 4 | D) 10
   - *4(½) + 6 = 2 + 6 = 8.*

143. If m = 10, find m/5 − 1.
   - **A) 1** | B) 3 | C) −1 | D) 21
   - *10 ÷ 5 − 1 = 2 − 1 = 1.*

144. If p = 2 and q = −1, find p² − q².
   - **A) 3** | B) 5 | C) −3 | D) 1
   - *p² − q² = 4 − 1 = 3.*

145. If x = 6, find 2(x − 3).
   - **A) 6** | B) 14 | C) 3 | D) 12
   - *2(6 − 3) = 2(3) = 6.*

146. If a = 2 and b = 4, find a(b + 1).
   - **A) 10** | B) 12 | C) 6 | D) 14
   - *a(b + 1) = 2(4 + 1) = 2(5) = 10.*

147. If y = −4, find y² − 2y.
   - **A) 24** | B) 8 | C) −8 | D) 16
   - *(−4)² − 2(−4) = 16 + 8 = 24.*

148. If x = 3 and y = 2, find 2xy − y².
   - **A) 8** | B) 16 | C) 10 | D) 2
   - *2(3)(2) − (2)² = 12 − 4 = 8.*

149. If a = 5, find (a − 3)².
   - **A) 4** | B) 2 | C) 10 | D) 22
   - *(5 − 3)² = (2)² = 4.*

150. If x = −2, find 3 − x.
   - **A) 5** | B) 1 | C) −5 | D) −1
   - *3 − (−2) = 3 + 2 = 5.*

### Additional

151. If p = 4 and q = 3, find 2p + 3q.
   - **A) 17** | B) 14 | C) 19 | D) 8
   - *2(4) + 3(3) = 8 + 9 = 17.*

152. If m = −3 and n = 2, find m² − n².
   - **A) 5** | B) 13 | C) 1 | D) −5
   - *m² − n² = (−3)² − 2² = 9 − 4 = 5.*

153. If x = 2, find x³ + 2x.
   - **A) 12** | B) 10 | C) 14 | D) 16
   - *2³ + 2(2) = 8 + 4 = 12.*

---

## Topic 5: Linear Equations
*Solving equations, word problems, changing subject* — 150 questions

1. Solve: x + 5 = 12
   - A) x = 5 | **B) x = 7** | C) x = 17 | D) x = 12
   - *x = 12 − 5 = 7*

2. Solve: x − 3 = 8
   - A) x = 5 | B) x = 3 | **C) x = 11** | D) x = 8
   - *x = 8 + 3 = 11*

3. Solve: x + 9 = 15
   - A) x = 24 | B) x = 9 | **C) x = 6** | D) x = 15
   - *x = 15 − 9 = 6*

4. Solve: 4x = 20
   - A) x = 4 | **B) x = 5** | C) x = 16 | D) x = 80
   - *x = 20 ÷ 4 = 5*

5. Solve: x/3 = 7
   - A) x = 10 | B) x = 4 | **C) x = 21** | D) x = 3
   - *x = 7 × 3 = 21*

6. Solve: x − 12 = 0
   - A) x = 0 | B) x = −12 | **C) x = 12** | D) x = 24
   - *x = 0 + 12 = 12*

7. Solve: 7x = 49
   - A) x = 6 | **B) x = 7** | C) x = 42 | D) x = 56
   - *x = 49 ÷ 7 = 7*

8. Solve: x/5 = 4
   - A) x = 9 | B) x = 1 | **C) x = 20** | D) x = 25
   - *x = 4 × 5 = 20*

9. Solve: x + 14 = 30
   - A) x = 44 | B) x = 14 | **C) x = 16** | D) x = 30
   - *x = 30 − 14 = 16*

10. Solve: 9x = 63
   - A) x = 54 | B) x = 72 | C) x = 9 | **D) x = 7**
   - *x = 63 ÷ 9 = 7*

11. Solve: 2x + 3 = 11
   - A) x = 3 | **B) x = 4** | C) x = 7 | D) x = 5.5
   - *2x = 8, x = 4*

12. Solve: 3x − 5 = 16
   - **A) x = 7** | B) x = 3 | C) x = 21 | D) x = 11
   - *3x = 21, x = 7*

13. Solve: 5x + 2 = 27
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 29 | C) x = 6 | D) x = 4
   - *5x = 25, x = 5*

14. Solve: 4x − 1 = 19
   - A) x = 18 | B) x = 4 | **C) x = 5** | D) x = 80
   - *4x = 20, x = 5*

15. Solve: x/2 + 3 = 10
   - A) x = 7 | B) x = 26 | **C) x = 14** | D) x = 20
   - *x/2 = 7, x = 14*

16. Solve: x/4 − 2 = 3
   - A) x = 4 | **B) x = 20** | C) x = 12 | D) x = 1
   - *x/4 = 5, x = 20*

17. Solve: 6x + 7 = 43
   - A) x = 7 | **B) x = 6** | C) x = 36 | D) x = 8
   - *6x = 36, x = 6*

18. Solve: 2x − 9 = 1
   - A) x = 4 | **B) x = 5** | C) x = 10 | D) x = −4
   - *2x = 10, x = 5*

19. Solve: 7x + 4 = 32
   - **A) x = 4** | B) x = 28 | C) x = 5 | D) x = 3
   - *7x = 28, x = 4*

20. Solve: 3x + 11 = 29
   - A) x = 18 | B) x = 40 | **C) x = 6** | D) x = 9
   - *3x = 18, x = 6*

21. Solve: 5x = 3x + 10
   - A) x = 2 | **B) x = 5** | C) x = 10 | D) x = 3
   - *2x = 10, x = 5*

22. Solve: 7x − 4 = 3x + 8
   - **A) x = 3** | B) x = 1 | C) x = 4 | D) x = 12
   - *4x = 12, x = 3*

23. Solve: 6x + 1 = 4x + 9
   - A) x = 5 | **B) x = 4** | C) x = 10 | D) x = 8
   - *2x = 8, x = 4*

24. Solve: 8x − 3 = 5x + 12
   - A) x = 15 | B) x = 3 | C) x = 9 | **D) x = 5**
   - *3x = 15, x = 5*

25. Solve: 2x + 15 = 5x
   - A) x = 3 | **B) x = 5** | C) x = 15 | D) x = 7
   - *15 = 3x, x = 5*

26. Solve: 9x − 2 = 7x + 6
   - **A) x = 4** | B) x = 2 | C) x = 8 | D) x = 1
   - *2x = 8, x = 4*

27. Solve: 4x + 7 = x + 22
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 15 | C) x = 29 | D) x = 3
   - *3x = 15, x = 5*

28. Solve: 10x − 6 = 6x + 14
   - A) x = 2 | B) x = 20 | **C) x = 5** | D) x = 8
   - *4x = 20, x = 5*

29. Solve: x/3 + x/6 = 5
   - **A) x = 10** | B) x = 15 | C) x = 6 | D) x = 30
   - *LCD 6: 2x/6 + x/6 = 5, so x/2 = 5, x = 10*

30. Solve: 2x/5 = 6
   - A) x = 12 | **B) x = 15** | C) x = 3 | D) x = 30
   - *2x = 30, x = 15*

31. Solve: −3x = 18
   - A) x = 6 | **B) x = −6** | C) x = 21 | D) x = −21
   - *x = 18 ÷ (−3) = −6*

   - A) x = 3 | **B) x = −3** | C) x = 10 | D) x = −10
   - *−2x = 6, x = −3*

33. Solve: x/2 − x/3 = 4
   - A) x = 12 | **B) x = 24** | C) x = 6 | D) x = 8
   - *LCD 6: 3x/6 − 2x/6 = 4, x/6 = 4, x = 24*

34. Solve: −x + 5 = 12
   - A) x = 7 | **B) x = −7** | C) x = 17 | D) x = −17
   - *−x = 7, x = −7*

   - **A) x = 17** | B) x = 20 | C) x = 23 | D) x = 2
   - *x + 3 = 20, x = 17*

   - **A) x = 3** | B) x = 2 | C) x = −3 | D) x = 6
   - *−2x = −6, x = 3*

   - A) x = 7 | **B) x = 8** | C) x = 16 | D) x = 7.5
   - *2x − 1 = 15, 2x = 16, x = 8*

   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 2.5 | C) x = 10.2 | D) x = 7.6
   - *0.5x = 2.5, x = 5*

   - A) x = 5 | **B) x = 7** | C) x = 6 | D) x = 3
   - *3(x−1) = 18, x−1 = 6, x = 7*

   - *x = 5.0*

   - *3x = 12, x = 4*

   - *3(3x+2) = 5(x+6), 9x+6 = 5x+30, 4x = 24, x = 6*

   - **A) x = 4** | B) x = 5.5 | C) x = 7 | D) x = 8

   - *4x − 20 = 8, 4x = 28, x = 7*

   - **A) x = 3** | B) x = 7 | C) x = 10 | D) x = 9
   - *6x + 2 = 20, 6x = 18, x = 3*

   - *2(x+2) = 3(x−1), 2x+4 = 3x−3, x = 7*

   - *2(3x−1) = 16, 6x−2 = 16, 6x = 18, x = 3*

   - **A) x = 2** | B) x = 5 | C) x = 0 | D) x = 8
   - *5(5−x) = 15, 25−5x = 15, 5x = 10, x = 2*

77. Solve: (x + 2)/3 + (x − 4)/6 = 3
   - **A) x = 6** | B) x = 18 | C) x = 4 | D) x = 10

78. Solve: 4(x − 1) = 2(x + 3) + 10
   - **A) x = 10** | B) x = 8 | C) x = 5 | D) x = 12
   - *4x−4 = 2x+16, 2x = 20, x = 10*

79. Solve: (3x − 5)/4 = (x + 7)/2
   - **A) x = 19** | B) x = 9 | C) x = 33 | D) x = 12
   - *3x−5 = 2(x+7), 3x−5 = 2x+14, x = 19*

80. Solve: 3(x + 4)/2 − (x − 2) = 10
   - A) x = 2 | B) x = 6 | **C) x = 4** | D) x = 8
   - *Multiply by 2: 3(x+4)−2(x−2) = 20, 3x+12−2x+4 = 20, x+16 = 20, x = 4*

81. Solve: 5 − 3(2x − 1) = 2(4 − x)
   - **A) x = 0** | B) x = 1 | C) x = −1 | D) x = 2
   - *5−6x+3 = 8−2x, 8−6x = 8−2x, −4x = 0, x = 0*

82. Solve: 7(x − 2) − 4(x + 1) = 0
   - **A) x = 6** | B) x = 4 | C) x = 18 | D) x = 2
   - *7x−14−4x−4 = 0, 3x−18 = 0, x = 6*

83. Solve: 2(5x − 3) = 3(2x + 4)
   - **A) x = 9/2** | B) x = 9 | C) x = 3 | D) x = 18
   - *10x−6 = 6x+12, 4x = 18, x = 9/2*

84. Solve: (2x + 5)/3 = (x + 4)/2
   - **A) x = 2** | B) x = −2 | C) x = 7 | D) x = 1
   - *2(2x+5) = 3(x+4), 4x+10 = 3x+12, x = 2*

85. Solve: 3(4x − 1) − 5(2x + 3) = 0
   - **A) x = 9** | B) x = 3 | C) x = 18 | D) x = 6
   - *12x−3−10x−15 = 0, 2x−18 = 0, x = 9*

86. Solve: 2[x − 3(x − 2)] = 8
   - A) x = −1 | **B) x = 1** | C) x = 2 | D) x = −2
   - *2[x−3x+6] = 8, 2(−2x+6) = 8, −4x+12 = 8, −4x = −4, x = 1*

87. Solve: (4x − 3)/5 = (2x + 1)/3
   - **A) x = 7** | B) x = 14 | C) x = 2 | D) x = 4
   - *3(4x−3) = 5(2x+1), 12x−9 = 10x+5, 2x = 14, x = 7*

88. Solve: 5(x − 2) + 3 = 2(x + 4)
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 3 | C) x = 15 | D) x = 7
   - *5x−10+3 = 2x+8, 5x−7 = 2x+8, 3x = 15, x = 5*

89. Mei Ling bought 3 pens at $x each and paid $12. Find x.
   - A) $3 | **B) $4** | C) $6 | D) $36
   - *3x = 12, x = $4*

90. A bowl of laksa costs $x. Ahmad pays $6 for 2 bowls. Find x.
   - **A) $3** | B) $4 | C) $12 | D) $2
   - *2x = 6, x = $3*

91. Wei Ming is x years old. His father is 30 years older and is 42. Find x.
   - A) x = 72 | B) x = 30 | **C) x = 12** | D) x = 42
   - *x + 30 = 42, x = 12*

92. A hawker sold x plates in the morning and 45 in the afternoon, totalling 120. Find x.
   - A) x = 165 | **B) x = 75** | C) x = 45 | D) x = 85
   - *x + 45 = 120, x = 75*

93. The MRT fare is $x. Siti rides 5 times and spends $7.50. Find x.
   - A) $2.50 | **B) $1.50** | C) $37.50 | D) $12.50
   - *5x = 7.50, x = $1.50*

94. A packet of nasi lemak costs $x. Kumar buys 4 for $14. Find x.
   - **A) $3.50** | B) $4.00 | C) $10.00 | D) $56.00
   - *4x = 14, x = $3.50*

95. Raj bought 4 kaya toasts at $x each and a kopi for $1.80, paying $7.00. Find x.
   - **A) $1.30** | B) $1.80 | C) $2.20 | D) $1.05
   - *4x + 1.80 = 7.00, 4x = 5.20, x = $1.30*

96. A rectangular garden is (2x + 3) m long and 5 m wide. Perimeter is 36 m. Find x.
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 4 | C) x = 3.5 | D) x = 6
   - *2(2x+3)+2(5) = 36, 4x+16 = 36, 4x = 20, x = 5*

97. Three friends split a $45 meal equally. Each also pays $2 for drinks. Total per person?
   - **A) $17** | B) $15 | C) $47 | D) $45
   - *45/3 + 2 = $17*

98. An HDB flat has x rooms. The next-door flat has 2 more. Together they have 10 rooms. Find x.
   - **A) x = 4** | B) x = 6 | C) x = 5 | D) x = 8
   - *x+(x+2) = 10, 2x = 8, x = 4*

99. Lina scores x marks. Her friend scores twice her marks. Total is 96. Find x.
   - A) x = 48 | **B) x = 32** | C) x = 64 | D) x = 24
   - *3x = 96, x = 32*

100. A hawker sells nasi lemak at $3.50 and mee siam at $x. He sold 20 nasi lemak and 15 mee siam for $115. Find x.
   - **A) $3.00** | B) $4.00 | C) $3.50 | D) $2.50
   - *70+15x = 115, 15x = 45, x = $3.00*

101. The sum of three consecutive numbers is 72. Find the smallest.
   - **A) 23** | B) 24 | C) 25 | D) 22
   - *x+(x+1)+(x+2) = 72, 3x+3 = 72, x = 23*

102. Ah Huat is 3 times as old as his nephew. In 10 years, he will be twice as old. How old is the nephew?
   - **A) 10** | B) 15 | C) 5 | D) 20
   - *3x+10 = 2(x+10), x = 10*

103. A taxi charges $3.90 flag-down plus $0.25 per 400 m. Total fare is $8.90. How many 400 m units?
   - **A) 20** | B) 18 | C) 25 | D) 35
   - *0.25n = 5.00, n = 20*

104. Mrs Tan bought x kg rice at $2.80/kg and 3 kg sugar at $1.50/kg for $18.50. Find x.
   - **A) 5** | B) 4 | C) 3 | D) 6
   - *2.80x+4.50 = 18.50, 2.80x = 14, x = 5*

105. A class has x boys and (x + 5) girls, totalling 35. How many boys?
   - **A) 15** | B) 20 | C) 10 | D) 25
   - *2x+5 = 35, x = 15*

106. A rectangle is (3x − 1) cm by (x + 2) cm with perimeter 42 cm. Find x.
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 6 | C) x = 4 | D) x = 7
   - *2(3x−1)+2(x+2) = 42, 8x+2 = 42, x = 5*

107. Ali has $200 and spends $x/day for 5 days then $2x/day for 3 days. He has $35 left. Find x.
   - **A) $15** | B) $20 | C) $12 | D) $25
   - *200−5x−6x = 35, 11x = 165, x = $15*

108. Triangle angles are x°, (x + 20)° and (2x − 8)°. Find x.
   - **A) 42** | B) 40 | C) 38 | D) 45
   - *4x+12 = 180, x = 42*

109. Beng Huat buys 2 bubble teas at $(x+1) each and 1 waffle at $4.50. He pays $20 with $5.50 change. Find x.
   - **A) $4** | B) $5 | C) $3 | D) $6
   - *2(x+1)+4.50 = 14.50, 2x = 8, x = $4*

110. A fruit seller has x durians and sells half, leaving 12. Find x.
   - A) x = 6 | **B) x = 24** | C) x = 18 | D) x = 12
   - *x/2 = 12, x = 24*

111. Priya has $x, gives $15 to charity and splits the rest among 4 friends who each get $10. Find x.
   - **A) $55** | B) $40 | C) $25 | D) $65
   - *(x−15)/4 = 10, x = $55*

112. An isosceles triangle has two sides of (2x+1) cm and base 10 cm. Perimeter is 30 cm. Find x.
   - **A) x = 4.5** | B) x = 5 | C) x = 4 | D) x = 3
   - *2(2x+1)+10 = 30, 4x = 18, x = 4.5*

113. A bus has x passengers. At the next stop 8 get off, 15 get on — now full at 40. Find x.
   - **A) x = 33** | B) x = 47 | C) x = 25 | D) x = 63
   - *x−8+15 = 40, x = 33*

114. A number is doubled, then 7 is subtracted. The result is 23. Find the number.
   - **A) 15** | B) 8 | C) 30 | D) 16
   - *2x−7 = 23, x = 15*

115. Three-quarters of a number is 45. Find the number.
   - **A) 60** | B) 33.75 | C) 180 | D) 15
   - *(3/4)x = 45, x = 60*

116. After spending 2/5 of his money, Jason has $36 left. How much did he start with?
   - **A) $60** | B) $90 | C) $14.40 | D) $50
   - *(3/5)x = 36, x = $60*

117. A regular pentagon has perimeter (5x + 10) cm and each side is 7 cm. Find x.
   - **A) x = 5** | B) x = 3 | C) x = 4 | D) x = 7
   - *35 = 5x+10, x = 5*

118. Five apples and 3 oranges cost $5.80. Each apple is $0.50. Find the cost of an orange.
   - **A) $1.10** | B) $0.80 | C) $1.00 | D) $0.60
   - *2.50+3y = 5.80, y = $1.10*

119. Two MRT stations are x km apart. A train at 60 km/h takes 5 minutes. Find x.
   - **A) 5 km** | B) 300 km | C) 12 km | D) 10 km
   - *5 min = 1/12 hr, distance = 60×(1/12) = 5 km*

120. A number increased by 20% gives 60. Find the number.
   - **A) 50** | B) 48 | C) 72 | D) 12
   - *1.2x = 60, x = 50*

121. Samy buys x books at $8 each. He has $5 left from $45. Find x.
   - **A) 5** | B) 4 | C) 6 | D) 3
   - *8x+5 = 45, 8x = 40, x = 5*

122. Two brothers have a combined age of 28. The older is 4 years older. Find the younger brother's age.
   - **A) 12** | B) 16 | C) 14 | D) 10
   - *x+(x+4) = 28, 2x = 24, x = 12*

123. At a kopitiam, 3 teh tariks and 2 kopi-o cost $9.20. Each kopi-o is $1.60. Find the price of teh tarik.
   - **A) $2.00** | B) $2.20 | C) $1.80 | D) $2.50
   - *3x+3.20 = 9.20, 3x = 6.00, x = $2.00*

124. A rectangle's length is 3 times its width w. Perimeter is 48 cm. Find w.
   - **A) 6 cm** | B) 12 cm | C) 16 cm | D) 8 cm
   - *2(3w)+2w = 48, 8w = 48, w = 6*

125. In a school of 720 students, the ratio of boys to girls is 5 : 4. How many boys are there?
   - **A) 400** | B) 320 | C) 360 | D) 450
   - *Boys = (5/9)×720 = 400*

126. The average of 4 numbers is 15. Three numbers are 12, 18 and 14. Find the fourth.
   - **A) 16** | B) 15 | C) 20 | D) 60
   - *Sum = 60, fourth = 60−44 = 16*

127. A shop gives 20% discount. The sale price is $64. Find the original price.
   - **A) $80** | B) $76.80 | C) $51.20 | D) $84
   - *0.8x = 64, x = $80*

128. Cheng Wei cycles at x km/h for 3 hours, covering 36 km. Find x.
   - **A) 12** | B) 108 | C) 33 | D) 9
   - *3x = 36, x = 12*

129. Make x the subject: y = x + 5
   - **A) x = y − 5** | B) x = y + 5 | C) x = 5 − y | D) x = 5y
   - *x = y − 5*

130. Make x the subject: y = x − 3
   - A) x = y − 3 | B) x = 3 − y | **C) x = y + 3** | D) x = 3y
   - *x = y + 3*

131. Make x the subject: y = 4x
   - A) x = 4y | **B) x = y/4** | C) x = y − 4 | D) x = y + 4
   - *x = y/4*

132. Make x the subject: y = x/6
   - A) x = y/6 | B) x = 6/y | **C) x = 6y** | D) x = y + 6
   - *x = 6y*

133. Make b the subject: a = b + c
   - A) b = a + c | **B) b = a − c** | C) b = c − a | D) b = ac
   - *b = a − c*

134. Make x the subject: y = 2x + 7
   - **A) x = (y − 7)/2** | B) x = (y + 7)/2 | C) x = 2y − 7 | D) x = y/2 + 7
   - *2x = y − 7, x = (y − 7)/2*

135. Make x the subject: y = 3x − 4
   - A) x = (y − 4)/3 | **B) x = (y + 4)/3** | C) x = 3y + 4 | D) x = (4 − y)/3
   - *3x = y + 4, x = (y + 4)/3*

136. Make r the subject: C = 2πr
   - A) r = C − 2π | B) r = 2πC | **C) r = C/(2π)** | D) r = 2C/π
   - *r = C/(2π)*

137. Make t the subject: d = st
   - A) t = d − s | B) t = ds | **C) t = d/s** | D) t = s/d
   - *t = d/s*

138. Make h the subject: A = bh/2
   - A) h = A/(2b) | **B) h = 2A/b** | C) h = Ab/2 | D) h = 2b/A
   - *2A = bh, h = 2A/b*

139. Make a the subject: v = u + at
   - A) a = (v + u)/t | **B) a = (v − u)/t** | C) a = v − ut | D) a = t(v − u)
   - *at = v − u, a = (v − u)/t*

140. Make l the subject: P = 2(l + w)
   - A) l = P/2 + w | B) l = (P − w)/2 | **C) l = P/2 − w** | D) l = 2P − w
   - *l + w = P/2, l = P/2 − w*

141. Make b the subject: A = (a + b)h/2
   - A) b = 2A/h + a | **B) b = 2A/h − a** | C) b = A/(2h) − a | D) b = 2Ah − a
   - *a + b = 2A/h, b = 2A/h − a*

142. Make x the subject: y = (3x + 1)/5
   - **A) x = (5y − 1)/3** | B) x = 5y/3 − 1 | C) x = (5y + 1)/3 | D) x = 5(y − 1)/3
   - *5y = 3x + 1, x = (5y − 1)/3*

143. Make x the subject: y = 5 − 2x
   - A) x = (5 + y)/2 | B) x = (y − 5)/2 | **C) x = (5 − y)/2** | D) x = 5 − y/2
   - *2x = 5 − y, x = (5 − y)/2*

144. Make R the subject: V = IR
   - A) R = V − I | B) R = VI | C) R = I/V | **D) R = V/I**
   - *R = V/I*

145. Make h the subject: V = πr²h
   - **A) h = V/(πr²)** | B) h = Vπr² | C) h = πr²/V | D) h = V − πr²
   - *h = V/(πr²)*

146. Make u the subject: v² = u² + 2as
   - A) u = v² − 2as | B) u² = v² + 2as | **C) u = √(v² − 2as)** | D) u = (v² − 2as)/2
   - *u² = v² − 2as, u = √(v² − 2as)*

147. Make n the subject: S = n(a + l)/2
   - A) n = S(a + l)/2 | **B) n = 2S/(a + l)** | C) n = S/(2(a + l)) | D) n = 2S(a + l)
   - *2S = n(a+l), n = 2S/(a+l)*

148. Make c the subject: E = mc²
   - A) c = E/m | **B) c = √(E/m)** | C) c = E/m² | D) c = Em²
   - *c² = E/m, c = √(E/m)*

149. Make y the subject: x = 3y − 7
   - **A) y = (x + 7)/3** | B) y = (x − 7)/3 | C) y = 3x + 7 | D) y = x/3 + 7
   - *x + 7 = 3y, y = (x + 7)/3*

150. Make a the subject: s = ut + at²/2
   - A) a = (s − ut)/t² | **B) a = 2(s − ut)/t²** | C) a = (2s − ut)/t² | D) a = 2s/t² − u
   - *s − ut = at²/2, 2(s − ut) = at², a = 2(s − ut)/t²*

---

## Topic 6: Linear Functions
*Cartesian coordinates, gradient, y = mx + c, graphing* — 150 questions

1. What are the coordinates of the origin?
   - A) (1, 1) | B) (0, 1) | **C) (0, 0)** | D) (1, 0)
   - *The origin is the point where the x-axis and y-axis meet, at (0, 0).*

2. The point (3, 5) lies in which quadrant?
   - **A) Quadrant I** | B) Quadrant II | C) Quadrant III | D) Quadrant IV
   - *Both coordinates are positive, so it is in Quadrant I.*

3. The point (−2, 4) lies in which quadrant?
   - A) Quadrant I | **B) Quadrant II** | C) Quadrant III | D) Quadrant IV
   - *x is negative, y is positive → Quadrant II.*

4. The point (−3, −7) lies in which quadrant?
   - A) Quadrant I | B) Quadrant II | **C) Quadrant III** | D) Quadrant IV
   - *Both coordinates are negative → Quadrant III.*

5. The point (5, −2) lies in which quadrant?
   - A) Quadrant I | B) Quadrant II | C) Quadrant III | **D) Quadrant IV**
   - *x is positive, y is negative → Quadrant IV.*

6. Which point lies on the x-axis?
   - A) (0, 3) | **B) (3, 0)** | C) (3, 3) | D) (−3, −3)
   - *Points on the x-axis have y = 0.*

7. Which point lies on the y-axis?
   - A) (5, 0) | **B) (0, −4)** | C) (−4, 5) | D) (5, −4)
   - *Points on the y-axis have x = 0.*

8. What is the x-coordinate of the point (7, −3)?
   - A) −3 | **B) 7** | C) 3 | D) −7
   - *The x-coordinate is the first number: 7.*

9. What is the y-coordinate of the point (−1, 6)?
   - A) −1 | B) 1 | **C) 6** | D) −6
   - *The y-coordinate is the second number: 6.*

10. Point A is 4 units right and 3 units up from the origin. What are its coordinates?
   - A) (3, 4) | **B) (4, 3)** | C) (−4, 3) | D) (4, −3)
   - *4 right → x = 4, 3 up → y = 3, so A = (4, 3).*

11. Point B is at (2, 5). If it moves 3 units left, what are the new coordinates?
   - A) (5, 5) | **B) (−1, 5)** | C) (2, 2) | D) (2, 8)
   - *Moving left decreases x: (2−3, 5) = (−1, 5).*

12. Point C is at (−1, 3). If it moves 4 units down, what are the new coordinates?
   - A) (−1, 7) | B) (3, 3) | **C) (−1, −1)** | D) (−5, 3)
   - *Moving down decreases y: (−1, 3−4) = (−1, −1).*

13. Which of these points has the same x-coordinate as (4, −2)?
   - **A) (4, 7)** | B) (−2, 4) | C) (7, −2) | D) (−4, 2)
   - *(4, 7) has x = 4, same as (4, −2).*

14. The midpoint of (2, 4) and (6, 8) is:
   - A) (3, 5) | **B) (4, 6)** | C) (8, 12) | D) (2, 2)
   - *Midpoint = ((2+6)/2, (4+8)/2) = (4, 6).*

15. The midpoint of (−2, 3) and (4, 7) is:
   - **A) (1, 5)** | B) (2, 10) | C) (−6, −4) | D) (3, 2)
   - *Midpoint = ((−2+4)/2, (3+7)/2) = (1, 5).*

16. Which point is a reflection of (3, 2) in the x-axis?
   - A) (−3, 2) | **B) (3, −2)** | C) (−3, −2) | D) (2, 3)
   - *Reflection in x-axis changes sign of y: (3, −2).*

17. Which point is a reflection of (3, 2) in the y-axis?
   - **A) (−3, 2)** | B) (3, −2) | C) (−3, −2) | D) (2, 3)
   - *Reflection in y-axis changes sign of x: (−3, 2).*

18. The distance from (0, 0) to (3, 4) is:
   - A) 7 | **B) 5** | C) 1 | D) 25
   - *Distance = √(3² + 4²) = √(9+16) = √25 = 5.*

19. The distance from (1, 2) to (4, 6) is:
   - **A) 5** | B) 7 | C) 3 | D) 25
   - *Distance = √(3² + 4²) = √25 = 5.*

20. Point P(a, 3) lies on the y-axis. What is a?
   - A) 3 | **B) 0** | C) −3 | D) 1
   - *Points on the y-axis have x = 0, so a = 0.*

21. Point Q(5, b) lies on the x-axis. What is b?
   - A) 5 | B) −5 | **C) 0** | D) 1
   - *Points on the x-axis have y = 0, so b = 0.*

22. Which of these points lies in Quadrant IV?
   - A) (−2, 3) | B) (2, 3) | C) (−2, −3) | **D) (2, −3)**
   - *Quadrant IV has positive x and negative y: (2, −3).*

23. The point (0, −5) lies on which axis?
   - A) x-axis | **B) y-axis** | C) Both axes | D) Neither axis
   - *x = 0 means it lies on the y-axis.*

24. Which pair of points lie on the same horizontal line?
   - A) (1, 3) and (1, 7) | **B) (2, 5) and (6, 5)** | C) (3, 1) and (1, 3) | D) (0, 0) and (1, 1)
   - *Same horizontal line means same y-coordinate. Both have y = 5.*

25. Which pair of points lie on the same vertical line?
   - **A) (3, 1) and (3, 8)** | B) (1, 3) and (8, 3) | C) (2, 2) and (5, 5) | D) (0, 1) and (1, 0)
   - *Same vertical line means same x-coordinate. Both have x = 3.*

26. If point A(2, k) and point B(2, 7) are the same point, what is k?
   - A) 2 | **B) 7** | C) 9 | D) 0
   - *Same point means same coordinates, so k = 7.*

27. The midpoint of (0, 0) and (8, 6) is:
   - A) (8, 6) | **B) (4, 3)** | C) (16, 12) | D) (2, 1.5)
   - *Midpoint = (8/2, 6/2) = (4, 3).*

28. Point (−4, 0) is how many units from the origin?
   - **A) 4** | B) −4 | C) 0 | D) 8
   - *Distance along x-axis = |−4| = 4 units.*

29. A point moves from (1, 2) right 5 and up 3. New position?
   - **A) (6, 5)** | B) (4, 7) | C) (−4, −1) | D) (6, −1)
   - *(1+5, 2+3) = (6, 5).*

30. What is the midpoint of (−3, 4) and (5, −2)?
   - **A) (1, 1)** | B) (2, 2) | C) (−8, 6) | D) (4, −3)
   - *((-3+5)/2, (4+(−2))/2) = (1, 1).*

31. Point (a, −a) always lies in which quadrant(s) when a > 0?
   - A) Quadrant I | B) Quadrant II | C) Quadrant III | **D) Quadrant IV**
   - *When a > 0: x = a > 0, y = −a < 0 → Quadrant IV.*

32. The points (1, 3), (2, 3), (5, 3) all lie on which line?
   - A) x = 3 | **B) y = 3** | C) y = x | D) x + y = 3
   - *All have y = 3, so they lie on the horizontal line y = 3.*

33. The distance between (−1, 3) and (5, 3) is:
   - **A) 6** | B) 4 | C) 8 | D) 2
   - *Same y-coordinate, so distance = |5−(−1)| = 6.*

34. The distance between (4, 1) and (4, 9) is:
   - A) 5 | B) 4 | **C) 8** | D) 13
   - *Same x-coordinate, so distance = |9−1| = 8.*

35. Point A(2, 5) is translated 3 units left and 4 units down. New position?
   - **A) (−1, 1)** | B) (5, 9) | C) (5, 1) | D) (−1, 9)
   - *(2−3, 5−4) = (−1, 1).*

36. Which point is closest to the origin?
   - A) (3, 4) | **B) (1, 1)** | C) (5, 0) | D) (0, 4)
   - *Distances: √25=5, √2≈1.4, 5, 4. (1,1) is closest.*

37. The point (6, −2) is reflected in the origin. What is the image?
   - **A) (−6, 2)** | B) (6, 2) | C) (−6, −2) | D) (2, −6)
   - *Reflection in origin changes both signs: (−6, 2).*

38. If M(3, k) is the midpoint of A(1, 2) and B(5, 8), find k.
   - **A) 5** | B) 4 | C) 6 | D) 3
   - *k = (2+8)/2 = 5.*

39. Point P is at (−2, −5). How far is P from the x-axis?
   - A) 2 | **B) 5** | C) 7 | D) √29
   - *Distance from x-axis = |y-coordinate| = |−5| = 5.*

40. Point Q is at (−2, −5). How far is Q from the y-axis?
   - **A) 2** | B) 5 | C) 7 | D) √29
   - *Distance from y-axis = |x-coordinate| = |−2| = 2.*

41. Find the gradient of the line through (1, 2) and (3, 8).
   - A) 2 | **B) 3** | C) 6 | D) 1/3
   - *m = (8−2)/(3−1) = 6/2 = 3*

42. Find the gradient of the line through (0, 0) and (4, 8).
   - A) 4 | B) 8 | **C) 2** | D) 1/2
   - *m = (8−0)/(4−0) = 8/4 = 2*

43. Find the gradient of the line through (2, 5) and (6, 5).
   - **A) 0** | B) 1 | C) Undefined | D) 4
   - *m = (5−5)/(6−2) = 0/4 = 0 (horizontal line)*

44. Find the gradient of the line through (3, 1) and (3, 7).
   - A) 0 | B) 6 | C) 1 | **D) Undefined**
   - *m = (7−1)/(3−3) = 6/0 → undefined (vertical line)*

45. Find the gradient of the line through (0, 4) and (2, 0).
   - A) 2 | **B) −2** | C) 1/2 | D) −1/2
   - *m = (0−4)/(2−0) = −4/2 = −2*

46. Find the gradient of the line through (1, 3) and (5, 11).
   - **A) 2** | B) 4 | C) 8 | D) 1/2
   - *m = (11−3)/(5−1) = 8/4 = 2*

47. Find the gradient of the line through (−2, 1) and (4, 7).
   - **A) 1** | B) 6 | C) −1 | D) 3
   - *m = (7−1)/(4−(−2)) = 6/6 = 1*

48. Find the gradient of the line through (−1, −3) and (2, 6).
   - **A) 3** | B) −3 | C) 1/3 | D) 9
   - *m = (6−(−3))/(2−(−1)) = 9/3 = 3*

49. A line has gradient 2. If it passes through (1, 5), what is y when x = 3?
   - A) 7 | **B) 9** | C) 11 | D) 8
   - *Rise = 2 × (3−1) = 4. y = 5 + 4 = 9.*

50. A line has gradient −1. If it passes through (2, 7), what is y when x = 5?
   - **A) 4** | B) 10 | C) 2 | D) 5
   - *Rise = −1 × (5−2) = −3. y = 7 − 3 = 4.*

51. A line rises 6 units for every 2 units it runs to the right. What is its gradient?
   - A) 6 | B) 2 | **C) 3** | D) 1/3
   - *Gradient = rise/run = 6/2 = 3*

52. A line drops 4 units for every 2 units it runs to the right. What is its gradient?
   - A) 2 | **B) −2** | C) 4 | D) −4
   - *Gradient = −4/2 = −2 (negative because it drops)*

53. Which line is steeper: gradient 3 or gradient −5?
   - A) Gradient 3 | **B) Gradient −5** | C) Both the same | D) Cannot tell
   - *Steepness is |gradient|. |−5| = 5 > |3| = 3, so gradient −5 is steeper.*

54. The gradient of a horizontal line is:
   - A) 1 | **B) 0** | C) Undefined | D) −1
   - *Horizontal lines have zero rise, so gradient = 0.*

55. The gradient of a vertical line is:
   - A) 1 | B) 0 | **C) Undefined** | D) ∞
   - *Vertical lines have zero run, so gradient is undefined.*

56. Find the gradient of the line through (0, −2) and (3, 7).
   - **A) 3** | B) −3 | C) 5/3 | D) 3/5
   - *m = (7−(−2))/(3−0) = 9/3 = 3*

57. Find the gradient of the line through (−4, 2) and (2, −1).
   - A) 1/2 | **B) −1/2** | C) 2 | D) −2
   - *m = (−1−2)/(2−(−4)) = −3/6 = −1/2*

58. Find the gradient of the line through (0, 5) and (10, 0).
   - A) 2 | B) −2 | C) 1/2 | **D) −1/2**
   - *m = (0−5)/(10−0) = −5/10 = −1/2*

59. A line passes through (2, 1) and (8, 4). What is its gradient?
   - **A) 1/2** | B) 2 | C) 3/6 | D) 6/3
   - *m = (4−1)/(8−2) = 3/6 = 1/2*

60. A line passes through (−3, −1) and (1, 7). What is its gradient?
   - **A) 2** | B) −2 | C) 4 | D) 1/2
   - *m = (7−(−1))/(1−(−3)) = 8/4 = 2*

61. Two points on a line are (0, 3) and (6, 3). The gradient is:
   - **A) 0** | B) 1 | C) 3 | D) 6
   - *m = (3−3)/(6−0) = 0*

62. If the gradient is 4/3 and the line passes through (0, 0), what is y when x = 6?
   - **A) 8** | B) 4.5 | C) 2 | D) 18
   - *y = (4/3)(6) = 8*

63. The gradient between (a, 3) and (5, 11) is 2. Find a.
   - **A) 1** | B) −3 | C) 3 | D) 9
   - *(11−3)/(5−a) = 2, 8/(5−a) = 2, 5−a = 4, a = 1*

64. The gradient between (2, b) and (6, 10) is 3. Find b.
   - **A) −2** | B) 22 | C) −4 | D) 1
   - *(10−b)/(6−2) = 3, 10−b = 12, b = −2*

65. Line AB has gradient 2/5. If A = (0, 1) and B = (10, k), find k.
   - **A) 5** | B) 3 | C) 4 | D) 21
   - *(k−1)/10 = 2/5, k−1 = 4, k = 5*

66. A road rises 50 m over a horizontal distance of 200 m. What is the gradient?
   - **A) 1/4** | B) 4 | C) 50 | D) 150
   - *Gradient = 50/200 = 1/4*

67. An MRT escalator rises 6 m over a horizontal distance of 10 m. What is the gradient?
   - **A) 3/5** | B) 5/3 | C) 6/10 | D) 10/6
   - *Gradient = 6/10 = 3/5*

68. Which line is parallel to a line with gradient 3?
   - A) A line with gradient −3 | B) A line with gradient 1/3 | **C) A line with gradient 3** | D) A line with gradient −1/3
   - *Parallel lines have the same gradient.*

69. If two lines are parallel, their gradients are:
   - A) Negative reciprocals | **B) Equal** | C) Both zero | D) Opposite signs
   - *Parallel lines have equal gradients.*

70. The gradient of the line through (−5, 2) and (−5, 10) is:
   - A) 0 | B) 8 | **C) Undefined** | D) −8
   - *Same x-coordinates → vertical line → undefined gradient.*

71. The gradient of the line from (1, 1) to (4, 1) is:
   - **A) 0** | B) 1 | C) 3 | D) Undefined
   - *Same y-coordinates → horizontal line → gradient = 0.*

72. Find the gradient: (−2, −3) to (4, 9).
   - **A) 2** | B) −2 | C) 1/2 | D) 6
   - *m = (9−(−3))/(4−(−2)) = 12/6 = 2*

73. Find the gradient: (3, 8) to (7, 2).
   - A) 3/2 | **B) −3/2** | C) 2/3 | D) −2/3
   - *m = (2−8)/(7−3) = −6/4 = −3/2*

74. A line with gradient −1 passes through (0, 6). Where does it cross the x-axis?
   - **A) (6, 0)** | B) (−6, 0) | C) (0, 6) | D) (3, 0)
   - *y = −x + 6. At y=0: x=6, so (6,0).*

75. A line with gradient 2 passes through (1, 3). Find y when x = 4.
   - A) 6 | **B) 9** | C) 11 | D) 8
   - *Rise = 2×(4−1) = 6. y = 3+6 = 9.*

76. The gradient of y = 7 is:
   - A) 7 | **B) 0** | C) 1 | D) Undefined
   - *y = 7 is a horizontal line with gradient 0.*

77. The gradient of x = −3 is:
   - A) −3 | B) 0 | C) 3 | **D) Undefined**
   - *x = −3 is a vertical line with undefined gradient.*

78. Points A(0, 1), B(2, 5), C(4, 9) are collinear if:
   - **A) AB gradient = BC gradient** | B) AB gradient ≠ BC gradient | C) All x-values are equal | D) All y-values are equal
   - *Collinear points lie on the same line, so the gradient between any pair must be equal.*

79. Gradient of AB = (5−1)/(2−0) = 2. Gradient of BC = (9−5)/(4−2) = 2. Are A, B, C collinear?
   - **A) Yes** | B) No | C) Cannot tell | D) Only if c = 1
   - *Both gradients are 2 (equal), so the points are collinear.*

80. What is the gradient of y = 3x + 2?
   - A) 2 | **B) 3** | C) 5 | D) 3/2
   - *In y = mx + c, m = 3.*

81. What is the y-intercept of y = 3x + 2?
   - A) 3 | **B) 2** | C) 0 | D) 5
   - *In y = mx + c, c = 2.*

82. What is the gradient of y = −2x + 5?
   - A) 5 | B) 2 | **C) −2** | D) −5
   - *m = −2*

83. What is the y-intercept of y = −2x + 5?
   - A) −2 | **B) 5** | C) −5 | D) 2
   - *c = 5*

84. What is the gradient of y = x − 4?
   - A) −4 | B) 0 | C) 4 | **D) 1**
   - *y = 1·x − 4, so m = 1.*

85. What is the y-intercept of y = x − 4?
   - A) 1 | **B) −4** | C) 4 | D) 0
   - *c = −4*

86. Write the equation of a line with gradient 2 and y-intercept 3.
   - A) y = 3x + 2 | **B) y = 2x + 3** | C) y = 2x − 3 | D) y = 3x − 2
   - *y = mx + c = 2x + 3*

87. Write the equation of a line with gradient −1 and y-intercept 6.
   - A) y = 6x − 1 | B) y = −x − 6 | **C) y = −x + 6** | D) y = x + 6
   - *y = −1·x + 6 = −x + 6*

88. The line y = 4x − 1 passes through (0, ?).
   - A) 4 | **B) −1** | C) 1 | D) 0
   - *At x = 0: y = −1. The y-intercept is −1.*

89. The line y = 4x − 1 passes through (1, ?).
   - **A) 3** | B) 4 | C) 5 | D) −1
   - *y = 4(1) − 1 = 3*

90. Which line passes through the origin?
   - A) y = 2x + 1 | **B) y = 2x** | C) y = x + 2 | D) y = 2
   - *y = 2x has c = 0, so it passes through (0, 0).*

91. Which equation represents a horizontal line?
   - A) x = 5 | **B) y = 5** | C) y = x | D) y = 5x
   - *y = 5 is horizontal (gradient = 0).*

92. Which equation represents a vertical line?
   - A) y = 3 | **B) x = 3** | C) y = 3x | D) y = x + 3
   - *x = 3 is a vertical line.*

93. The line y = 2x + 3 and y = 2x − 1 are:
   - A) Perpendicular | B) The same line | **C) Parallel** | D) Intersecting
   - *Same gradient (m = 2) but different y-intercepts → parallel.*

94. Which line is parallel to y = 5x − 3?
   - A) y = −5x + 3 | **B) y = 5x + 7** | C) y = 3x − 5 | D) y = x/5 + 3
   - *Parallel means same gradient. y = 5x + 7 has m = 5.*

95. A line has gradient 3 and passes through (0, −2). Its equation is:
   - A) y = −2x + 3 | B) y = 3x + 2 | **C) y = 3x − 2** | D) y = −2x − 3
   - *y = 3x + (−2) = 3x − 2*

96. A line has gradient −2 and passes through (0, 4). Its equation is:
   - A) y = 4x − 2 | B) y = −2x − 4 | **C) y = −2x + 4** | D) y = 2x + 4
   - *y = −2x + 4*

97. Convert to y = mx + c form: 2y = 6x + 4
   - A) y = 6x + 4 | **B) y = 3x + 2** | C) y = 3x + 4 | D) y = 2x + 6
   - *Divide by 2: y = 3x + 2*

98. Convert to y = mx + c form: 3y − 9x = 6
   - A) y = 9x + 6 | B) y = 3x + 6 | **C) y = 3x + 2** | D) y = −3x + 2
   - *3y = 9x + 6, y = 3x + 2*

99. Convert to y = mx + c form: x + y = 10
   - A) y = x + 10 | **B) y = −x + 10** | C) y = 10x + 1 | D) y = 10 − 10x
   - *y = −x + 10*

100. The equation 2x + y = 8 in the form y = mx + c is:
   - A) y = 2x + 8 | **B) y = −2x + 8** | C) y = 2x − 8 | D) y = −2x − 8
   - *y = −2x + 8*

101. Find the equation of a line with gradient 1/2 passing through (0, 1).
   - **A) y = x/2 + 1** | B) y = x + 1/2 | C) y = 2x + 1 | D) y = x/2 − 1
   - *y = (1/2)x + 1*

102. A line passes through (0, 0) with gradient −3. Its equation is:
   - A) y = 3x | **B) y = −3x** | C) y = −3 | D) x = −3
   - *y = −3x + 0 = −3x*

103. The gradient and y-intercept of y = −x/2 + 3 are:
   - **A) m = −1/2, c = 3** | B) m = 1/2, c = 3 | C) m = −2, c = 3 | D) m = 3, c = −1/2
   - *y = (−1/2)x + 3, so m = −1/2, c = 3.*

104. The gradient and y-intercept of y = 7 are:
   - A) m = 7, c = 0 | **B) m = 0, c = 7** | C) m = 1, c = 7 | D) m = 7, c = 7
   - *y = 0·x + 7, so m = 0, c = 7.*

105. If y = mx + c passes through (2, 7) and (0, 3), find m and c.
   - **A) m = 2, c = 3** | B) m = 3, c = 2 | C) m = 2, c = 7 | D) m = 7, c = 3
   - *c = 3 (y-intercept). m = (7−3)/(2−0) = 2.*

106. If y = mx + c passes through (0, −1) and (3, 5), find the equation.
   - **A) y = 2x − 1** | B) y = −2x + 5 | C) y = 2x + 1 | D) y = 3x − 1
   - *c = −1. m = (5−(−1))/(3−0) = 6/3 = 2. y = 2x − 1.*

107. A line passes through (1, 5) and (3, 9). Find the equation.
   - **A) y = 2x + 3** | B) y = 4x + 1 | C) y = 2x + 5 | D) y = x + 4
   - *m = (9−5)/(3−1) = 2. Using (1,5): 5 = 2(1)+c, c = 3. y = 2x + 3.*

108. A line passes through (2, 1) and (4, 7). Find the equation.
   - **A) y = 3x − 5** | B) y = 3x + 1 | C) y = 2x − 3 | D) y = 3x − 7
   - *m = (7−1)/(4−2) = 3. Using (2,1): 1 = 3(2)+c, c = −5. y = 3x − 5.*

109. The line y = 2x + k passes through (3, 11). Find k.
   - **A) 5** | B) 6 | C) 17 | D) 3
   - *11 = 2(3) + k, 11 = 6 + k, k = 5*

110. The line y = −x + k passes through (4, 1). Find k.
   - **A) 5** | B) −3 | C) 3 | D) −5
   - *1 = −4 + k, k = 5*

111. Where does y = 3x − 6 cross the x-axis?
   - **A) (2, 0)** | B) (−2, 0) | C) (0, −6) | D) (−6, 0)
   - *At y = 0: 0 = 3x − 6, x = 2. So (2, 0).*

112. Where does y = −2x + 8 cross the x-axis?
   - A) (−4, 0) | **B) (4, 0)** | C) (0, 8) | D) (8, 0)
   - *At y = 0: 0 = −2x + 8, x = 4. So (4, 0).*

113. Where does y = x/2 + 3 cross the y-axis?
   - **A) (0, 3)** | B) (0, 1/2) | C) (3, 0) | D) (−6, 0)
   - *y-intercept at x = 0: y = 3. So (0, 3).*

114. Which line has the steepest positive gradient?
   - A) y = x + 1 | **B) y = 3x − 2** | C) y = 2x + 5 | D) y = 0.5x + 4
   - *Gradients: 1, 3, 2, 0.5. The steepest positive is 3.*

115. Which line slopes downward from left to right?
   - A) y = 2x + 1 | B) y = x | **C) y = −3x + 4** | D) y = 5
   - *Negative gradient (m = −3) means downward slope.*

116. The x-intercept of y = 4x − 8 is:
   - **A) (2, 0)** | B) (0, −8) | C) (−2, 0) | D) (8, 0)
   - *Set y=0: 4x = 8, x = 2. x-intercept is (2, 0).*

117. The y-intercept of y = 4x − 8 is:
   - A) (2, 0) | **B) (0, −8)** | C) (−2, 0) | D) (0, 4)
   - *Set x=0: y = −8. y-intercept is (0, −8).*

118. For the line 3x + 2y = 12, find the y-intercept.
   - **A) (0, 6)** | B) (0, 4) | C) (0, 12) | D) (4, 0)
   - *Set x=0: 2y = 12, y = 6. y-intercept is (0, 6).*

119. A line is parallel to y = 4x + 1 and passes through (0, −3). Its equation is:
   - **A) y = 4x − 3** | B) y = −4x − 3 | C) y = 4x + 3 | D) y = −3x + 4
   - *Same gradient m = 4, y-intercept = −3. y = 4x − 3.*

120. To sketch y = 2x + 1, which two points could you plot?
   - **A) (0, 1) and (1, 3)** | B) (0, 2) and (1, 1) | C) (1, 1) and (2, 2) | D) (0, 0) and (1, 2)
   - *At x=0: y=1. At x=1: y=3. So (0,1) and (1,3).*

121. The graph of y = −x + 4 passes through (0, 4) and (4, 0). What shape is it?
   - A) Curve | **B) Straight line** | C) Parabola | D) Circle
   - *y = mx + c is always a straight line.*

122. A straight line graph passes through (0, 2) and (3, 8). Its equation is:
   - **A) y = 2x + 2** | B) y = 3x + 2 | C) y = 2x + 8 | D) y = 8x + 2
   - *m = (8−2)/3 = 2. c = 2. y = 2x + 2.*

123. The graph of y = 3 is:
   - A) A line through the origin | **B) A horizontal line at y = 3** | C) A vertical line at x = 3 | D) A line with gradient 3
   - *y = 3 is a horizontal line.*

124. The graph of x = −2 is:
   - A) A horizontal line | B) A line through the origin | **C) A vertical line at x = −2** | D) A line with gradient −2
   - *x = −2 is a vertical line.*

125. Which of these lines passes through the origin?
   - A) y = 3x + 1 | B) y = x − 2 | **C) y = −5x** | D) y = 2
   - *y = −5x has c = 0, so it passes through (0, 0).*

126. If a line crosses the y-axis at (0, −3) and the x-axis at (6, 0), the gradient is:
   - **A) 1/2** | B) −1/2 | C) 2 | D) −2
   - *m = (0−(−3))/(6−0) = 3/6 = 1/2*

127. The line y = −2x + 6 crosses the x-axis at:
   - **A) (3, 0)** | B) (−3, 0) | C) (6, 0) | D) (0, 6)
   - *Set y=0: 2x = 6, x = 3.*

128. The line y = x/3 − 2 crosses the y-axis at:
   - **A) (0, −2)** | B) (0, 1/3) | C) (6, 0) | D) (−2, 0)
   - *At x=0: y = −2.*

129. From the graph, a line passes through (−1, 0) and (0, 2). Its equation is:
   - **A) y = 2x + 2** | B) y = −2x + 2 | C) y = x + 2 | D) y = 2x − 2
   - *m = (2−0)/(0−(−1)) = 2. c = 2. y = 2x + 2.*

130. Two lines y = 3x + 1 and y = 3x − 4 are graphed. They will:
   - A) Cross at one point | B) Be identical | **C) Never meet (parallel)** | D) Cross at two points
   - *Same gradient (3) but different y-intercepts → parallel, never meet.*

131. The line y = x and the line y = −x intersect at:
   - A) (1, −1) | **B) (0, 0)** | C) (1, 1) | D) They do not intersect
   - *x = −x gives 2x = 0, x = 0. Both pass through (0, 0).*

132. How many points do the lines y = 2x + 1 and y = 3x − 2 share?
   - A) 0 | **B) 1** | C) 2 | D) Infinite
   - *Two non-parallel lines intersect at exactly one point.*

133. At which point do y = x + 3 and y = 2x + 1 intersect?
   - **A) (2, 5)** | B) (1, 3) | C) (3, 7) | D) (−2, 1)
   - *x + 3 = 2x + 1, x = 2. y = 2 + 3 = 5. Intersection at (2, 5).*

134. At which point do y = −x + 7 and y = x + 1 intersect?
   - **A) (3, 4)** | B) (4, 3) | C) (2, 5) | D) (6, 1)
   - *−x + 7 = x + 1, 6 = 2x, x = 3. y = 4. Intersection at (3, 4).*

135. The line y = 2x − 4 has a positive x-intercept. True or false?
   - **A) True** | B) False | C) Cannot determine | D) Only if c > 0
   - *At y=0: x = 2, which is positive.*

136. Which table of values matches y = 2x − 1?
   - **A) x: 0,1,2 → y: −1,1,3** | B) x: 0,1,2 → y: 1,3,5 | C) x: 0,1,2 → y: −1,0,1 | D) x: 0,1,2 → y: 2,3,4
   - *y(0) = −1, y(1) = 1, y(2) = 3.*

137. Which table of values matches y = −x + 5?
   - A) x: 0,1,2 → y: 5,6,7 | **B) x: 0,1,2 → y: 5,4,3** | C) x: 0,1,2 → y: −5,−4,−3 | D) x: 0,1,2 → y: 5,3,1
   - *y(0) = 5, y(1) = 4, y(2) = 3.*

138. A line on a graph goes through (0, 4) and slopes downward to the right. Which could be its equation?
   - A) y = 2x + 4 | **B) y = −3x + 4** | C) y = x − 4 | D) y = 4x
   - *y-intercept 4 and negative gradient → y = −3x + 4.*

139. A line on a graph goes through the origin and slopes upward. Which could be its equation?
   - A) y = −2x | B) y = 3 | **C) y = 4x** | D) y = x − 1
   - *Through origin (c = 0) and positive gradient → y = 4x.*

140. The graph of y = 2x + 3 is shifted up by 2 units. The new equation is:
   - **A) y = 2x + 5** | B) y = 4x + 3 | C) y = 2x + 1 | D) y = 2x − 2
   - *Shifting up 2 units adds 2 to c: y = 2x + 5.*

141. The graph of y = 3x − 1 is shifted down by 4 units. The new equation is:
   - A) y = 3x + 3 | **B) y = 3x − 5** | C) y = −x − 1 | D) y = 3x − 4
   - *Shifting down 4: c = −1 − 4 = −5. y = 3x − 5.*

142. A linear graph has x-intercept (5, 0) and y-intercept (0, 10). Find its equation.
   - A) y = 2x + 10 | **B) y = −2x + 10** | C) y = 2x − 10 | D) y = −2x − 10
   - *m = (10−0)/(0−5) = −2. c = 10. y = −2x + 10.*

143. The graph of y = mx + c has a negative gradient and positive y-intercept. Which quadrant does it NOT pass through?
   - A) Quadrant I | B) Quadrant II | **C) Quadrant III** | D) Quadrant IV
   - *With negative gradient and positive c, the line goes through Q I, II, and IV but not Q III (for typical values).*

144. A straight line passes through (−2, −5) and (2, 3). Find the equation.
   - **A) y = 2x − 1** | B) y = 2x + 1 | C) y = −2x − 1 | D) y = x − 3
   - *m = (3−(−5))/(2−(−2)) = 8/4 = 2. Using (2,3): 3 = 4+c, c = −1. y = 2x − 1.*

145. The line y = 5x − 10 passes through (2, 0). What is the significance of this point?
   - A) It is the y-intercept | **B) It is the x-intercept** | C) It is the origin | D) It is the midpoint
   - *At (2, 0), y = 0, so this is the x-intercept.*

146. Which of these lines has a y-intercept of 0?
   - A) y = 2x + 3 | **B) y = 3x** | C) y = x − 1 | D) y = 5
   - *y = 3x has c = 0.*

147. A student plots (1, 4), (2, 6), (3, 8). What is the equation of this line?
   - **A) y = 2x + 2** | B) y = 4x | C) y = x + 3 | D) y = 2x + 4
   - *m = (6−4)/(2−1) = 2. Using (1,4): 4 = 2+c, c = 2. y = 2x + 2.*

148. The graph of y = −x + 3 forms a triangle with the axes. What is its area?
   - **A) 4.5** | B) 9 | C) 3 | D) 6
   - *x-intercept: (3,0). y-intercept: (0,3). Area = (1/2)(3)(3) = 4.5.*

149. The graph of y = 2x − 6 forms a triangle with the axes. What is its area?
   - **A) 9** | B) 6 | C) 12 | D) 18
   - *x-intercept: (3,0). y-intercept: (0,−6). Area = (1/2)(3)(6) = 9.*

150. Lines y = 2x + 1 and y = −x + 7 intersect at (2, 5). Which line has the steeper slope?
   - **A) y = 2x + 1** | B) y = −x + 7 | C) Both equal | D) Cannot tell
   - *|2| = 2 > |−1| = 1, so y = 2x + 1 is steeper.*

---

## Topic 7: Number Patterns
*Sequences, nth term, general term, special patterns* — 150 questions

1. What is the next number in the sequence: 2, 5, 8, 11, ...?
   - A) 12 | B) 13 | **C) 14** | D) 15
   - *Common difference = 3. Next term = 11 + 3 = 14.*

2. What is the next number in the sequence: 3, 7, 11, 15, ...?
   - A) 17 | B) 18 | **C) 19** | D) 20
   - *Common difference = 4. Next term = 15 + 4 = 19.*

3. What is the next number in the sequence: 10, 8, 6, 4, ...?
   - A) 3 | **B) 2** | C) 0 | D) 1
   - *Common difference = −2. Next term = 4 − 2 = 2.*

4. What is the next number in the sequence: 1, 4, 9, 16, ...?
   - A) 20 | B) 21 | C) 24 | **D) 25**
   - *These are square numbers: 1², 2², 3², 4². Next = 5² = 25.*

5. What is the next number in the sequence: 2, 4, 8, 16, ...?
   - A) 24 | **B) 32** | C) 18 | D) 20
   - *Each term is doubled. Next = 16 × 2 = 32.*

6. What is the next number in the sequence: 1, 3, 6, 10, ...?
   - A) 13 | B) 14 | **C) 15** | D) 16
   - *Triangular numbers. Differences: +2, +3, +4, so next +5: 10 + 5 = 15.*

7. What is the next number in the sequence: 100, 95, 90, 85, ...?
   - A) 75 | **B) 80** | C) 70 | D) 82
   - *Common difference = −5. Next = 85 − 5 = 80.*

8. What is the next number in the sequence: 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, ...?
   - A) 11 | B) 12 | **C) 13** | D) 10
   - *Fibonacci: each term = sum of previous two. 5 + 8 = 13.*

9. What is the common difference of: 4, 9, 14, 19, 24?
   - A) 4 | **B) 5** | C) 6 | D) 9
   - *9 − 4 = 5*

10. What is the common difference of: 20, 17, 14, 11, 8?
   - **A) −3** | B) 3 | C) −2 | D) 2
   - *17 − 20 = −3*

11. What is the common difference of: 1, 5, 9, 13, 17?
   - A) 3 | **B) 4** | C) 5 | D) 6
   - *5 − 1 = 4*

12. Which sequence is arithmetic?
   - A) 1, 2, 4, 8, 16 | **B) 3, 6, 9, 12, 15** | C) 1, 1, 2, 3, 5 | D) 1, 4, 9, 16, 25
   - *An arithmetic sequence has constant common difference. 3, 6, 9, 12, 15 has d = 3.*

13. Which sequence is NOT arithmetic?
   - A) 5, 10, 15, 20 | B) 2, 5, 8, 11 | **C) 1, 2, 4, 7** | D) −3, 0, 3, 6
   - *1, 2, 4, 7 has differences 1, 2, 3 — not constant.*

14. What is the 5th term of: 6, 10, 14, 18, ...?
   - A) 20 | **B) 22** | C) 24 | D) 26
   - *d = 4. T(5) = 18 + 4 = 22.*

15. What is the 6th term of: 3, 8, 13, 18, 23, ...?
   - A) 27 | **B) 28** | C) 30 | D) 33
   - *d = 5. T(6) = 23 + 5 = 28.*

16. Find the missing term: 7, ?, 15, 19, 23
   - A) 9 | B) 10 | **C) 11** | D) 12
   - *d = 4. Second term = 7 + 4 = 11.*

17. Find the missing term: 2, 6, ?, 14, 18
   - A) 8 | B) 9 | **C) 10** | D) 12
   - *d = 4. Third term = 6 + 4 = 10.*

18. The first term is 5 and the common difference is 3. What is the 4th term?
   - **A) 14** | B) 17 | C) 11 | D) 20
   - *T(4) = 5 + 3(3) = 5 + 9 = 14.*

19. The first term is 100 and the common difference is −7. What is the 5th term?
   - **A) 72** | B) 79 | C) 65 | D) 86
   - *T(5) = 100 + 4(−7) = 100 − 28 = 72.*

20. In the pattern 2, 6, 18, 54, ..., each term is multiplied by:
   - A) 2 | **B) 3** | C) 4 | D) 6
   - *6/2 = 3, 18/6 = 3, 54/18 = 3. Common ratio = 3.*

21. What is the next term: 2, 6, 18, 54, ...?
   - A) 108 | **B) 162** | C) 72 | D) 216
   - *54 × 3 = 162*

22. What is the next term: 81, 27, 9, 3, ...?
   - A) 0 | **B) 1** | C) −3 | D) 1/3
   - *Each term ÷ 3. Next = 3 ÷ 3 = 1.*

23. What is the next term: 5, 10, 20, 40, ...?
   - A) 50 | B) 60 | **C) 80** | D) 100
   - *Each term × 2. Next = 40 × 2 = 80.*

24. In the pattern 1, 4, 9, 16, 25, what type of numbers are these?
   - A) Prime numbers | B) Triangular numbers | **C) Square numbers** | D) Cube numbers
   - *1 = 1², 4 = 2², 9 = 3², 16 = 4², 25 = 5². Square numbers.*

25. In the pattern 1, 3, 6, 10, 15, what type of numbers are these?
   - A) Square numbers | B) Prime numbers | **C) Triangular numbers** | D) Cube numbers
   - *These are triangular numbers: T(n) = n(n+1)/2.*

26. What is the 6th triangular number?
   - A) 18 | **B) 21** | C) 15 | D) 28
   - *T(6) = 6(7)/2 = 21*

27. What is the 7th square number?
   - A) 36 | B) 42 | **C) 49** | D) 56
   - *7² = 49*

28. What are the first 5 cube numbers?
   - A) 1, 4, 9, 16, 25 | **B) 1, 8, 27, 64, 125** | C) 1, 3, 9, 27, 81 | D) 2, 4, 8, 16, 32
   - *1³=1, 2³=8, 3³=27, 4³=64, 5³=125*

29. What is the next number: 1, 8, 27, 64, ...?
   - A) 100 | B) 81 | **C) 125** | D) 216
   - *Cube numbers. Next = 5³ = 125.*

30. The sequence 2, 4, 8, 16, 32 are powers of:
   - A) 3 | B) 4 | **C) 2** | D) 8
   - *2¹, 2², 2³, 2⁴, 2⁵ — powers of 2.*

31. What is the 8th term of: 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, ...?
   - A) 64 | **B) 128** | C) 256 | D) 32
   - *T(n) = 2^(n−1). T(8) = 2⁷ = 128.*

32. Find the pattern rule: 5, 11, 17, 23, 29, ...
   - A) Add 5 | **B) Add 6** | C) Add 7 | D) Multiply by 2
   - *11 − 5 = 6. Common difference = 6.*

33. Find the pattern rule: 50, 43, 36, 29, 22, ...
   - A) Subtract 6 | **B) Subtract 7** | C) Subtract 8 | D) Divide by 2
   - *43 − 50 = −7. Common difference = −7.*

34. Which number comes next: 3, 5, 9, 15, 23, ...?
   - A) 29 | B) 31 | **C) 33** | D) 35
   - *Differences: 2, 4, 6, 8 → next difference = 10. 23 + 10 = 33.*

35. Which number comes next: 1, 2, 5, 10, 17, ...?
   - A) 24 | B) 25 | **C) 26** | D) 28
   - *Differences: 1, 3, 5, 7 → next difference = 9. 17 + 9 = 26.*

36. A student counts chairs arranged in rows: Row 1 has 5, Row 2 has 8, Row 3 has 11. How many in Row 5?
   - A) 14 | **B) 17** | C) 20 | D) 23
   - *d = 3. Row 4 = 14, Row 5 = 17.*

37. At a kopitiam, Table 1 seats 4 people, Table 2 seats 6, Table 3 seats 8. How many does Table 7 seat?
   - A) 14 | **B) 16** | C) 18 | D) 20
   - *d = 2. T(7) = 4 + 6(2) = 16.*

38. HDB Block 1 has 10 floors, Block 2 has 14 floors, Block 3 has 18 floors. Block 6 has:
   - A) 26 | B) 28 | **C) 30** | D) 32
   - *d = 4. T(6) = 10 + 5(4) = 30.*

39. MRT Station 1 is 2 km from home, Station 2 is 5 km, Station 3 is 8 km. Station 10 is:
   - **A) 29 km** | B) 32 km | C) 27 km | D) 30 km
   - *d = 3. T(10) = 2 + 9(3) = 29 km.*

40. A pattern of dots: Row 1 = 1, Row 2 = 3, Row 3 = 5, Row 4 = 7. What kind of numbers are these?
   - A) Even | **B) Odd** | C) Prime | D) Square
   - *1, 3, 5, 7 — these are odd numbers (also an arithmetic sequence with d = 2).*

41. The sequence 2, 6, 12, 20, 30 has differences 4, 6, 8, 10. What is the next term?
   - A) 40 | **B) 42** | C) 36 | D) 38
   - *Next difference = 12. 30 + 12 = 42.*

42. Identify the pattern: 0, 3, 8, 15, 24, ...
   - **A) n² − 1** | B) n² + 1 | C) 2n + 1 | D) n(n+1)
   - *When n=1: 0, n=2: 3, n=3: 8, n=4: 15, n=5: 24. These are n² − 1.*

43. A sequence starts 10, 7, 4, 1, −2. The common difference is:
   - A) 3 | **B) −3** | C) 7 | D) −7
   - *7 − 10 = −3*

44. Fill in the blank: 4, 11, 18, __, 32
   - A) 24 | **B) 25** | C) 26 | D) 27
   - *d = 7. Fourth term = 18 + 7 = 25.*

45. The pattern 1, 2, 4, 7, 11, 16 has second differences of:
   - **A) 1** | B) 2 | C) 3 | D) Not constant
   - *First differences: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5. Second differences: 1, 1, 1, 1 — constant at 1.*

46. What are the next two terms: 1, 4, 10, 20, 35, ...?
   - **A) 56, 84** | B) 50, 70 | C) 55, 80 | D) 42, 56
   - *Differences: 3, 6, 10, 15 → next: 21, 28. So 35+21=56, 56+28=84.*

47. In a stack of oranges, Layer 1 has 1, Layer 2 has 4, Layer 3 has 9, Layer 4 has 16. Layer 8 has:
   - A) 36 | B) 49 | **C) 64** | D) 81
   - *Square numbers. Layer n = n². Layer 8 = 64.*

48. A tiling pattern needs 3 tiles for Figure 1, 5 tiles for Figure 2, 7 tiles for Figure 3. Figure 10 needs:
   - A) 19 | **B) 21** | C) 23 | D) 25
   - *d = 2. T(10) = 3 + 9(2) = 21.*

49. Mei Ling saves $5 in Week 1, $8 in Week 2, $11 in Week 3. How much in Week 10?
   - A) $30 | **B) $32** | C) $35 | D) $38
   - *d = 3. T(10) = 5 + 9(3) = $32.*

50. The number of handshakes between n people is n(n−1)/2. For 6 people:
   - A) 12 | **B) 15** | C) 18 | D) 30
   - *6(5)/2 = 15 handshakes.*

51. Find the nth term: 3, 5, 7, 9, ...
   - **A) 2n + 1** | B) 2n − 1 | C) n + 2 | D) 3n
   - *d = 2. T(n) = 2n + b. T(1) = 2+b = 3, b = 1. T(n) = 2n + 1.*

52. Find the nth term: 5, 8, 11, 14, ...
   - A) 3n + 5 | **B) 3n + 2** | C) 5n + 3 | D) 3n − 1
   - *d = 3. T(n) = 3n + b. T(1) = 3+b = 5, b = 2. T(n) = 3n + 2.*

53. Find the nth term: 2, 7, 12, 17, ...
   - **A) 5n − 3** | B) 5n + 2 | C) 2n + 5 | D) 5n − 2
   - *d = 5. T(n) = 5n + b. T(1) = 5+b = 2, b = −3. T(n) = 5n − 3.*

54. Find the nth term: 4, 7, 10, 13, ...
   - A) 3n + 4 | **B) 3n + 1** | C) 4n + 3 | D) 3n − 1
   - *d = 3. T(1) = 3+b = 4, b = 1. T(n) = 3n + 1.*

55. Find the nth term: 1, 6, 11, 16, ...
   - **A) 5n − 4** | B) 5n + 1 | C) 6n − 5 | D) 5n − 1
   - *d = 5. T(1) = 5+b = 1, b = −4. T(n) = 5n − 4.*

56. Find the nth term: 10, 13, 16, 19, ...
   - A) 3n + 10 | **B) 3n + 7** | C) 10n + 3 | D) n + 9
   - *d = 3. T(1) = 3+b = 10, b = 7. T(n) = 3n + 7.*

57. Find the nth term: 6, 10, 14, 18, ...
   - A) 4n + 6 | **B) 4n + 2** | C) 6n + 4 | D) 2n + 4
   - *d = 4. T(1) = 4+b = 6, b = 2. T(n) = 4n + 2.*

58. Find the nth term: 20, 17, 14, 11, ...
   - **A) −3n + 23** | B) −3n + 20 | C) 3n + 17 | D) 20 − n
   - *d = −3. T(1) = −3+b = 20, b = 23. T(n) = −3n + 23.*

59. Find the nth term: 50, 45, 40, 35, ...
   - **A) −5n + 55** | B) −5n + 50 | C) 5n − 45 | D) 50 − n
   - *d = −5. T(1) = −5+b = 50, b = 55. T(n) = −5n + 55.*

60. Find the nth term: 0, 3, 6, 9, ...
   - A) 3n | **B) 3n − 3** | C) n + 3 | D) 3n + 3
   - *d = 3. T(1) = 3+b = 0, b = −3. T(n) = 3n − 3.*

61. The nth term of a sequence is 4n − 1. What is T(5)?
   - **A) 19** | B) 20 | C) 15 | D) 21
   - *T(5) = 4(5) − 1 = 19*

62. The nth term of a sequence is 4n − 1. What is T(10)?
   - **A) 39** | B) 40 | C) 41 | D) 36
   - *T(10) = 4(10) − 1 = 39*

63. The nth term is 2n + 5. What is T(1)?
   - A) 5 | **B) 7** | C) 2 | D) 3
   - *T(1) = 2(1) + 5 = 7*

64. The nth term is 2n + 5. What is T(20)?
   - **A) 45** | B) 25 | C) 40 | D) 50
   - *T(20) = 2(20) + 5 = 45*

65. The nth term is 7n − 2. Find T(8).
   - **A) 54** | B) 56 | C) 58 | D) 50
   - *T(8) = 7(8) − 2 = 54*

66. The nth term is −2n + 30. Find T(10).
   - **A) 10** | B) 50 | C) 20 | D) 8
   - *T(10) = −2(10) + 30 = 10*

67. If T(n) = 3n + 4, which term equals 25?
   - A) n = 6 | **B) n = 7** | C) n = 8 | D) n = 9
   - *3n + 4 = 25, 3n = 21, n = 7*

68. If T(n) = 5n − 2, which term equals 48?
   - **A) n = 10** | B) n = 8 | C) n = 9 | D) n = 46
   - *5n − 2 = 48, 5n = 50, n = 10*

69. If T(n) = 2n + 1, which term equals 41?
   - **A) n = 20** | B) n = 21 | C) n = 19 | D) n = 42
   - *2n + 1 = 41, 2n = 40, n = 20*

70. If T(n) = 4n + 3, is 50 a term in this sequence?
   - A) Yes, n = 12 | **B) No** | C) Yes, n = 47/4 | D) Yes, n = 13
   - *4n + 3 = 50, 4n = 47, n = 47/4. Not a whole number, so 50 is not a term.*

71. If T(n) = 6n − 1, is 35 a term in this sequence?
   - **A) Yes, n = 6** | B) Yes, n = 5 | C) No | D) Yes, n = 7
   - *6n − 1 = 35, 6n = 36, n = 6. Yes, 35 is the 6th term.*

72. The sequence has T(n) = n + 5. The first 4 terms are:
   - **A) 6, 7, 8, 9** | B) 5, 6, 7, 8 | C) 1, 2, 3, 4 | D) 6, 8, 10, 12
   - *T(1)=6, T(2)=7, T(3)=8, T(4)=9.*

73. The sequence has T(n) = 10 − n. The first 4 terms are:
   - A) 10, 9, 8, 7 | **B) 9, 8, 7, 6** | C) 11, 12, 13, 14 | D) 10, 20, 30, 40
   - *T(1)=9, T(2)=8, T(3)=7, T(4)=6.*

74. Find the nth term: 8, 11, 14, 17, ...
   - A) 3n + 8 | **B) 3n + 5** | C) 8n + 3 | D) n + 7
   - *d = 3. T(1) = 3+b = 8, b = 5. T(n) = 3n + 5.*

75. Find the nth term: 7, 13, 19, 25, ...
   - A) 6n − 1 | **B) 6n + 1** | C) 7n − 6 | D) 6n + 7
   - *d = 6. T(1) = 6+b = 7, b = 1. T(n) = 6n + 1.*

76. Find the nth term: 1, 3, 5, 7, ...
   - **A) 2n − 1** | B) 2n + 1 | C) n + 1 | D) n − 1
   - *d = 2. T(1) = 2+b = 1, b = −1. T(n) = 2n − 1. (Odd numbers!)*

77. Find the nth term: 2, 4, 6, 8, ...
   - A) n + 2 | **B) 2n** | C) 2n + 2 | D) n²
   - *d = 2. T(1) = 2+b = 2, b = 0. T(n) = 2n. (Even numbers!)*

78. The 10th term of the sequence with T(n) = 3n − 2 is:
   - **A) 28** | B) 30 | C) 32 | D) 27
   - *T(10) = 3(10) − 2 = 28*

79. The 50th term of the sequence with T(n) = 2n + 3 is:
   - A) 100 | **B) 103** | C) 53 | D) 105
   - *T(50) = 2(50) + 3 = 103*

80. The 100th term of the sequence with T(n) = n + 99 is:
   - **A) 199** | B) 200 | C) 100 | D) 198
   - *T(100) = 100 + 99 = 199*

81. A matchstick pattern: Fig 1 = 4, Fig 2 = 7, Fig 3 = 10. Find T(n).
   - **A) 3n + 1** | B) 4n + 3 | C) 3n + 4 | D) n + 3
   - *d = 3. T(1) = 3+b = 4, b = 1. T(n) = 3n + 1.*

82. A matchstick pattern: Fig 1 = 5, Fig 2 = 9, Fig 3 = 13. Find T(n).
   - A) 4n + 5 | B) 5n + 4 | **C) 4n + 1** | D) 5n − 1
   - *d = 4. T(1) = 4+b = 5, b = 1. T(n) = 4n + 1.*

83. A tile pattern: Fig 1 = 3, Fig 2 = 5, Fig 3 = 7. Find T(20).
   - **A) 41** | B) 43 | C) 40 | D) 39
   - *T(n) = 2n + 1. T(20) = 41.*

84. A dot pattern: Fig 1 = 6, Fig 2 = 11, Fig 3 = 16. Find T(n).
   - **A) 5n + 1** | B) 6n + 5 | C) 5n − 1 | D) 5n + 6
   - *d = 5. T(1) = 5+b = 6, b = 1. T(n) = 5n + 1.*

85. Using T(n) = 5n + 1, how many dots in Figure 12?
   - A) 60 | **B) 61** | C) 62 | D) 65
   - *T(12) = 5(12) + 1 = 61*

86. The first term of a sequence is 8 and the common difference is 5. What is T(n)?
   - A) 5n + 8 | **B) 5n + 3** | C) 8n + 5 | D) 5n − 3
   - *T(n) = a + (n−1)d = 8 + 5(n−1) = 8 + 5n − 5 = 5n + 3.*

87. The first term is 100 and the common difference is −4. What is T(n)?
   - **A) −4n + 104** | B) −4n + 100 | C) 4n + 96 | D) 100 − n
   - *T(n) = 100 + (n−1)(−4) = 100 − 4n + 4 = −4n + 104.*

88. T(n) = −4n + 104. What is T(25)?
   - **A) 4** | B) 0 | C) −4 | D) 8
   - *T(25) = −100 + 104 = 4*

89. A sequence has T(3) = 14 and T(7) = 30. Find the common difference.
   - **A) 4** | B) 8 | C) 16 | D) 2
   - *d = (30 − 14)/(7 − 3) = 16/4 = 4*

90. A sequence has T(2) = 9 and T(5) = 21. Find the common difference.
   - A) 3 | **B) 4** | C) 6 | D) 12
   - *d = (21 − 9)/(5 − 2) = 12/3 = 4*

91. A sequence has a = 3 and d = 6. Which term equals 57?
   - **A) n = 10** | B) n = 9 | C) n = 8 | D) n = 11
   - *3 + (n−1)(6) = 57, 6n − 3 = 57, 6n = 60, n = 10.*

92. A sequence has a = 7 and d = 4. Which term first exceeds 100?
   - A) n = 24 | **B) n = 25** | C) n = 23 | D) n = 26
   - *T(n) = 4n + 3 > 100, 4n > 97, n > 24.25. So n = 25 is the first integer. T(25) = 103.*

93. Find the nth term: 100, 93, 86, 79, ...
   - **A) −7n + 107** | B) −7n + 100 | C) 7n − 93 | D) 100 − 7n
   - *d = −7. T(1) = −7+b = 100, b = 107. T(n) = −7n + 107.*

94. Find the nth term: 1/2, 1, 3/2, 2, ...
   - **A) n/2** | B) (n+1)/2 | C) (n−1)/2 | D) 2n
   - *d = 1/2. T(n) = (1/2)n + b. T(1) = 1/2+b = 1/2, b = 0. T(n) = n/2.*

95. The first term of a sequence is 12 and T(n) = 4n + 8. Is this correct?
   - **A) Yes** | B) No, should be 4n + 12 | C) No, should be 4n − 8 | D) No, should be 12n + 4
   - *T(1) = 4(1) + 8 = 12. Yes, this matches.*

96. Ahmad writes: T(n) = 3n + 2. He claims T(5) = 18. Is he correct?
   - A) Yes | **B) No, T(5) = 17** | C) No, T(5) = 13 | D) No, T(5) = 15
   - *T(5) = 3(5) + 2 = 17, not 18.*

97. How many terms of the sequence T(n) = 2n − 1 are less than 30?
   - A) 14 | **B) 15** | C) 16 | D) 13
   - *2n − 1 < 30, 2n < 31, n < 15.5. So n can be 1 to 15 — that is 15 terms.*

98. In the sequence T(n) = 5n + 2, find the sum of the first 3 terms.
   - A) 30 | **B) 36** | C) 33 | D) 27
   - *T(1)=7, T(2)=12, T(3)=17. Sum = 7+12+17 = 36.*

99. What is the 10th square number?
   - A) 81 | **B) 100** | C) 121 | D) 90
   - *10² = 100*

100. What is the 8th triangular number?
   - A) 28 | **B) 36** | C) 45 | D) 21
   - *T(8) = 8(9)/2 = 36*

101. What is the 5th triangular number?
   - A) 10 | **B) 15** | C) 20 | D) 25
   - *T(5) = 5(6)/2 = 15*

102. The sum of the first n natural numbers is:
   - A) n² | **B) n(n+1)/2** | C) n(n−1)/2 | D) 2n
   - *1+2+3+...+n = n(n+1)/2 (triangular number formula).*

103. What is 1 + 2 + 3 + ... + 20?
   - A) 190 | B) 200 | **C) 210** | D) 220
   - *20(21)/2 = 210*

104. What is 1 + 2 + 3 + ... + 50?
   - A) 1225 | B) 1250 | **C) 1275** | D) 1300
   - *50(51)/2 = 1275*

105. The 4th cube number is:
   - A) 12 | B) 27 | **C) 64** | D) 81
   - *4³ = 64*

106. Which of these is both a square and a triangular number?
   - A) 4 | B) 9 | **C) 36** | D) 25
   - *36 = 6² and 36 = 8(9)/2 = 36. It is both.*

107. The sequence 1, 3, 6, 10, 15 ... The 10th term is:
   - A) 45 | B) 50 | **C) 55** | D) 60
   - *T(10) = 10(11)/2 = 55*

108. How many dots form the 6th triangular number?
   - A) 15 | B) 18 | **C) 21** | D) 24
   - *T(6) = 6(7)/2 = 21*

109. The pattern of square numbers: 1, 4, 9, 16, 25. The differences between consecutive terms are:
   - A) 1, 2, 3, 4 | **B) 3, 5, 7, 9** | C) 2, 4, 6, 8 | D) 1, 3, 5, 7
   - *4−1=3, 9−4=5, 16−9=7, 25−16=9. The differences are consecutive odd numbers.*

110. The sum of the first n odd numbers equals:
   - A) n(n+1)/2 | **B) n²** | C) 2n | D) n(n+1)
   - *1+3+5+...+(2n−1) = n². For example: 1+3+5+7 = 16 = 4².*

111. 1 + 3 + 5 + 7 + 9 = ?
   - A) 20 | **B) 25** | C) 16 | D) 36
