   - *Sum of first 5 odd numbers = 5² = 25.*

112. 2 + 4 + 6 + 8 + 10 = ?
   - A) 20 | B) 25 | **C) 30** | D) 35
   - *Sum = 5 × 6 = 30. (Or: n(n+1) where n = 5.)*

113. The Fibonacci sequence starts 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8. What is the 8th term?
   - A) 13 | **B) 21** | C) 34 | D) 55
   - *Continuing: 13, 21. The 8th term is 21.*

114. In the Fibonacci sequence, T(10) = 55. What is T(11)?
   - **A) 89** | B) 76 | C) 110 | D) 66
   - *T(9) = 34, T(10) = 55. T(11) = 34 + 55 = 89.*

115. Which number is a perfect square?
   - A) 50 | **B) 64** | C) 72 | D) 80
   - *64 = 8² is a perfect square.*

116. Which number is a perfect cube?
   - A) 16 | B) 25 | **C) 27** | D) 36
   - *27 = 3³ is a perfect cube.*

117. Which number is both a perfect square and a perfect cube?
   - A) 8 | B) 27 | C) 36 | **D) 64**
   - *64 = 8² = 4³ — both a perfect square and cube.*

118. The sequence 1, 8, 27, 64, 125 — the differences are 7, 19, 37, 61. Are these constant?
   - A) Yes | **B) No** | C) Almost constant | D) Only the first two
   - *7, 19, 37, 61 are not constant. Cube numbers are not arithmetic.*

119. A square number can be expressed as the sum of consecutive odd numbers. 16 = ?
   - **A) 1+3+5+7** | B) 2+4+6+4 | C) 4+4+4+4 | D) 8+8
   - *16 = 1+3+5+7 (sum of first 4 odd numbers = 4²).*

120. The pattern of pentagonal numbers starts: 1, 5, 12, 22, 35. The common second difference is:
   - A) 2 | **B) 3** | C) 4 | D) 5
   - *First differences: 4, 7, 10, 13. Second differences: 3, 3, 3. Constant at 3.*

121. A tower of cubes: Level 1 uses 1 cube, Level 2 uses 4, Level 3 uses 9. Total cubes for 4 levels?
   - A) 16 | B) 20 | C) 25 | **D) 30**
   - *1 + 4 + 9 + 16 = 30*

122. A staircase has 1 block on top, 2 on the next step, 3 on the next, etc. Total blocks for 8 steps?
   - A) 28 | **B) 36** | C) 45 | D) 64
   - *1+2+...+8 = 8(9)/2 = 36*

123. The nth term of square numbers is:
   - A) n(n+1) | **B) n²** | C) 2n | D) n(n+1)/2
   - *Square numbers: T(n) = n².*

124. The nth term of triangular numbers is:
   - A) n² | B) n(n+1) | **C) n(n+1)/2** | D) (n+1)/2
   - *Triangular numbers: T(n) = n(n+1)/2.*

125. The sequence 0, 1, 4, 9, 16, 25 has nth term:
   - **A) (n−1)²** | B) n² − 1 | C) n² | D) (n+1)²
   - *T(1)=0=0², T(2)=1=1², T(3)=4=2². So T(n) = (n−1)².*

126. The sequence 2, 5, 10, 17, 26 has nth term:
   - **A) n² + 1** | B) n² − 1 | C) 2n + 1 | D) n² + n
   - *2=1²+1, 5=2²+1, 10=3²+1, 17=4²+1. T(n) = n² + 1.*

127. The sequence 0, 3, 8, 15, 24 has nth term:
   - **A) n² − 1** | B) n(n+1) | C) n² + 1 | D) (n+1)² − 2
   - *0=1²−1, 3=2²−1, 8=3²−1, 15=4²−1. T(n) = n² − 1.*

128. The sequence 3, 6, 11, 18, 27 has nth term:
   - **A) n² + 2** | B) n² + 3 | C) 3n² | D) n² − 2
   - *3=1²+2, 6=2²+2, 11=3²+2, 18=4²+2. T(n) = n² + 2.*

129. The sequence 4, 7, 12, 19, 28 has nth term:
   - **A) n² + 3** | B) n² + 4 | C) 4n + 3 | D) (n+1)²
   - *4=1²+3, 7=2²+3, 12=3²+3, 19=4²+3. T(n) = n² + 3.*

130. The sequence 1, 4, 9, 16, 25 is produced by T(n) = n². What is T(15)?
   - **A) 225** | B) 210 | C) 240 | D) 150
   - *15² = 225*

131. Using T(n) = n(n+1)/2, find T(12).
   - A) 66 | B) 72 | **C) 78** | D) 84
   - *12(13)/2 = 78*

132. A student builds L-shaped figures. Fig 1 has 3 squares, Fig 2 has 5, Fig 3 has 7. Find the nth term.
   - **A) 2n + 1** | B) 2n − 1 | C) 3n | D) n + 2
   - *d = 2. T(1) = 2+b = 3, b = 1. T(n) = 2n + 1.*

133. A growing pattern: Fig 1 = 1 circle, Fig 2 = 4, Fig 3 = 9, Fig 4 = 16. What kind of pattern?
   - A) Arithmetic | **B) Square numbers** | C) Triangular numbers | D) Fibonacci
   - *1, 4, 9, 16 = 1², 2², 3², 4². Square numbers.*

134. In the sequence 2, 6, 12, 20, 30, the nth term is:
   - A) n(n+1) | B) n²+n | **C) Both A and B** | D) n²+1
   - *n(n+1) = n²+n. T(1)=2, T(2)=6, T(3)=12. Both A and B are the same expression.*

135. The number of diagonals in a polygon with n sides is n(n−3)/2. A hexagon has:
   - A) 6 | **B) 9** | C) 12 | D) 15
   - *6(6−3)/2 = 6(3)/2 = 9 diagonals.*

136. The number of diagonals in an octagon (8 sides) is:
   - A) 16 | **B) 20** | C) 24 | D) 28
   - *8(8−3)/2 = 8(5)/2 = 20 diagonals.*

137. A pattern gives: n=1→2, n=2→6, n=3→12, n=4→20. The formula is:
   - A) 2n | B) n(n+1) | C) n²+n | **D) Both B and C**
   - *1(2)=2, 2(3)=6, 3(4)=12, 4(5)=20. T(n) = n(n+1) = n²+n.*

138. The sum of first n even numbers is n(n+1). What is 2+4+6+...+20?
   - A) 100 | **B) 110** | C) 90 | D) 120
   - *There are 10 even numbers from 2 to 20. Sum = 10(11) = 110.*

139. How many square numbers are between 1 and 100 (inclusive)?
   - A) 9 | **B) 10** | C) 11 | D) 8
   - *1², 2², ..., 10² = 100. There are 10 square numbers.*

140. What is the next triangular number after 15?
   - A) 18 | B) 20 | **C) 21** | D) 24
   - *15 is T(5). T(6) = 6(7)/2 = 21.*

141. The sum 1² + 2² + 3² + 4² = ?
   - A) 20 | B) 25 | **C) 30** | D) 16
   - *1 + 4 + 9 + 16 = 30*

142. In a pattern, each figure adds a border of dots. Fig 1 = 1, Fig 2 = 4, Fig 3 = 9. These are:
   - A) Triangular numbers | **B) Square numbers** | C) Cube numbers | D) Even numbers
   - *1, 4, 9 are 1², 2², 3².*

143. The nth even number is:
   - A) n + 2 | **B) 2n** | C) 2n − 1 | D) n²
   - *1st even = 2, 2nd = 4, 3rd = 6. T(n) = 2n.*

144. The nth odd number is:
   - A) 2n + 1 | **B) 2n − 1** | C) n + 1 | D) n²
   - *1st odd = 1, 2nd = 3, 3rd = 5. T(n) = 2n − 1.*

145. A pattern: 2, 8, 18, 32, 50. The nth term is:
   - **A) 2n²** | B) n² + 1 | C) 4n − 2 | D) n(n+1)
   - *2(1)²=2, 2(2)²=8, 2(3)²=18, 2(4)²=32, 2(5)²=50. T(n) = 2n².*

146. The sequence 5, 20, 45, 80, 125 has nth term:
   - **A) 5n²** | B) 5n + 15 | C) n² + 4 | D) 5n(n+1)
   - *5(1)²=5, 5(2)²=20, 5(3)²=45, 5(4)²=80, 5(5)²=125. T(n) = 5n².*

147. A pattern of triangles: Fig 1 = 1, Fig 2 = 3, Fig 3 = 6, Fig 4 = 10. What type of numbers?
   - A) Square | B) Cube | **C) Triangular** | D) Fibonacci
   - *1, 3, 6, 10 are triangular numbers.*

148. The 20th term of the sequence T(n) = n² + 1 is:
   - A) 400 | **B) 401** | C) 441 | D) 421
   - *T(20) = 20² + 1 = 401*

149. The sequence 0, 2, 6, 12, 20 has nth term:
   - A) n² − n | B) n(n−1) | **C) Both A and B** | D) n² + n
   - *n(n−1) = n²−n. T(1)=0, T(2)=2, T(3)=6, T(4)=12, T(5)=20. Both A and B are the same expression.*

150. Siti notices that 1³ = 1, 1³+2³ = 9, 1³+2³+3³ = 36. Each sum is a perfect square. What is 1³+2³+3³+4³?
   - A) 64 | **B) 100** | C) 81 | D) 144
   - *1+8+27+64 = 100 = 10². The sum of the first n cubes equals [n(n+1)/2]². Here: [4(5)/2]² = 10² = 100.*

---

## Topic 8: Percentage
*Percentage of a quantity, increase/decrease, reverse percentage* — 150 questions

### PERCENTAGE OF A QUANTITY (Q1–38)

1. Find 10% of $50.
   - **A) $5** | B) $10 | C) $15 | D) $50
   - *10% of $50 = 0.10 × $50 = $5.*

2. Find 25% of 80.
   - A) 15 | **B) 20** | C) 25 | D) 40
   - *25% of 80 = 0.25 × 80 = 20.*

3. Find 50% of 120.
   - A) 24 | B) 50 | **C) 60** | D) 100
   - *50% of 120 = 0.50 × 120 = 60.*

4. Find 75% of 200.
   - A) 100 | B) 125 | **C) 150** | D) 175
   - *75% of 200 = 0.75 × 200 = 150.*

5. Find 20% of $35.
   - A) $5 | **B) $7** | C) $8 | D) $10
   - *20% of $35 = 0.20 × $35 = $7.*

6. Find 15% of 60.
   - A) 6 | **B) 9** | C) 12 | D) 15
   - *15% of 60 = 0.15 × 60 = 9.*

7. Find 30% of $250.
   - A) $25 | B) $50 | **C) $75** | D) $100
   - *30% of $250 = 0.30 × $250 = $75.*

8. Find 5% of 400.
   - A) 5 | B) 10 | **C) 20** | D) 40
   - *5% of 400 = 0.05 × 400 = 20.*

9. Find 12.5% of 80.
   - A) 8 | **B) 10** | C) 12 | D) 16
   - *12.5% of 80 = 0.125 × 80 = 10.*

10. Find 40% of $150.
   - A) $40 | B) $50 | **C) $60** | D) $70
   - *40% of $150 = 0.40 × $150 = $60.*

11. Express 15 as a percentage of 60.
   - A) 15% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 30%
   - *15/60 × 100% = 25%.*

12. Express 9 as a percentage of 36.
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 36%
   - *9/36 × 100% = 25%.*

13. Express $12 as a percentage of $80.
   - A) 12% | **B) 15%** | C) 18% | D) 20%
   - *12/80 × 100% = 15%.*

14. Express 45 as a percentage of 180.
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 45%
   - *45/180 × 100% = 25%.*

15. Express 7 as a percentage of 20.
   - A) 25% | B) 30% | **C) 35%** | D) 40%
   - *7/20 × 100% = 35%.*

16. Convert 3/8 to a percentage.
   - A) 35% | **B) 37.5%** | C) 38% | D) 40%
   - *3/8 × 100% = 37.5%.*

17. Convert 0.65 to a percentage.
   - A) 6.5% | B) 60% | **C) 65%** | D) 650%
   - *0.65 × 100% = 65%.*

18. Convert 45% to a decimal.
   - A) 0.045 | **B) 0.45** | C) 4.5 | D) 45
   - *45% = 45 ÷ 100 = 0.45.*

19. Convert 7/25 to a percentage.
   - A) 25% | **B) 28%** | C) 30% | D) 35%
   - *7/25 × 100% = 28%.*

20. What percentage of 2 kg is 500 g?
   - A) 5% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 50%
   - *500 g out of 2000 g = 500/2000 × 100% = 25%.*

21. A hawker stall sells 120 bowls of laksa in a day. 30 are sold before noon. What percentage is sold before noon?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 35%
   - *30/120 × 100% = 25%.*

22. An NTUC FairPrice basket of groceries costs $80. Fruits make up $20. What percentage is spent on fruits?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 40%
   - *20/80 × 100% = 25%.*

23. Find 35% of $240.
   - A) $72 | B) $78 | **C) $84** | D) $90
   - *35% of $240 = 0.35 × $240 = $84.*

24. Find 2% of $1500.
   - A) $15 | **B) $30** | C) $50 | D) $150
   - *2% of $1500 = 0.02 × $1500 = $30.*

25. In a class of 40 students, 60% are girls. How many are girls?
   - A) 16 | B) 20 | **C) 24** | D) 30
   - *60% of 40 = 0.60 × 40 = 24 girls.*

26. A student scored 72 out of 90 on a math test. What is the percentage score?
   - A) 72% | B) 75% | C) 78% | **D) 80%**
   - *72/90 × 100% = 80%.*

27. A durian costs $18. GST is 9%. What is the GST amount?
   - A) $0.90 | B) $1.08 | **C) $1.62** | D) $1.80
   - *9% of $18 = 0.09 × $18 = $1.62.*

28. Express 0.008 as a percentage.
   - A) 0.008% | B) 0.08% | **C) 0.8%** | D) 8%
   - *0.008 × 100% = 0.8%.*

29. What is 150% of 60?
   - A) 60 | B) 75 | **C) 90** | D) 120
   - *150% of 60 = 1.50 × 60 = 90.*

30. Convert 5/6 to a percentage (to 1 d.p.).
   - A) 80.0% | **B) 83.3%** | C) 85.0% | D) 86.7%
   - *5/6 × 100% = 83.333...% ≈ 83.3%.*

31. A box contains 250 apples. 8% are rotten. How many apples are rotten?
   - A) 8 | B) 16 | **C) 20** | D) 25
   - *8% of 250 = 0.08 × 250 = 20 apples.*

32. Find 66⅔% of 210.
   - A) 105 | B) 120 | C) 130 | **D) 140**
   - *66⅔% = 2/3. 2/3 × 210 = 140.*

33. What percentage of 1 hour is 45 minutes?
   - A) 45% | B) 55% | C) 65% | **D) 75%**
   - *45/60 × 100% = 75%.*

34. What percentage of 1 km is 350 m?
   - A) 3.5% | B) 30% | **C) 35%** | D) 350%
   - *350/1000 × 100% = 35%.*

35. An MRT station has 800 commuters in the morning. 480 tap in before 8 am. What percentage is this?
   - A) 48% | B) 52% | C) 58% | **D) 60%**
   - *480/800 × 100% = 60%.*

36. Find 0.5% of $2000.
   - A) $1 | B) $5 | **C) $10** | D) $100
   - *0.5% of $2000 = 0.005 × $2000 = $10.*

37. A bubble tea costs $5.80. If 9% GST is added, what is the GST amount (to nearest cent)?
   - A) $0.29 | **B) $0.52** | C) $0.58 | D) $5.80
   - *9% of $5.80 = 0.09 × $5.80 = $0.522 ≈ $0.52.*

38. Express 3 out of 8 as a percentage.
   - A) 30% | B) 33.3% | **C) 37.5%** | D) 38%
   - *3/8 × 100% = 37.5%.*

### PERCENTAGE CHANGE (Q39–80)

39. A shirt's price increases from $40 to $50. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 10% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 50%
   - *Increase = $10. % increase = 10/40 × 100% = 25%.*

40. A bag's price decreases from $60 to $45. What is the percentage decrease?
   - A) 15% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 30%
   - *Decrease = $15. % decrease = 15/60 × 100% = 25%.*

41. A population grows from 200 to 250. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 50%
   - *Increase = 50. % increase = 50/200 × 100% = 25%.*

42. A laptop's price drops from $1200 to $900. What is the percentage decrease?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 33.3%
   - *Decrease = $300. % decrease = 300/1200 × 100% = 25%.*

43. Increase $80 by 15%.
   - A) $90 | **B) $92** | C) $95 | D) $96
   - *$80 × 1.15 = $92.*

44. Decrease $120 by 30%.
   - A) $36 | B) $72 | **C) $84** | D) $90
   - *$120 × 0.70 = $84.*

45. A hawker increases the price of chicken rice from $3.50 to $4.20. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 15% | B) 18% | **C) 20%** | D) 25%
   - *Increase = $0.70. % increase = 0.70/3.50 × 100% = 20%.*

46. The price of a HDB flat increases from $300,000 to $360,000. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 15% | B) 18% | **C) 20%** | D) 25%
   - *Increase = $60,000. % increase = 60,000/300,000 × 100% = 20%.*

47. An MRT fare increases from $1.50 to $1.65. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 5% | B) 8% | **C) 10%** | D) 15%
   - *Increase = $0.15. % increase = 0.15/1.50 × 100% = 10%.*

48. Increase 250 by 12%.
   - A) 262 | B) 270 | **C) 280** | D) 290
   - *250 × 1.12 = 280.*

49. Decrease 400 by 5%.
   - A) 360 | B) 370 | **C) 380** | D) 395
   - *400 × 0.95 = 380.*

50. A school's enrolment drops from 1000 to 850. What is the percentage decrease?
   - A) 10% | B) 12% | **C) 15%** | D) 18%
   - *Decrease = 150. % decrease = 150/1000 × 100% = 15%.*

51. After a 10% increase, the new value is 110. What was the original?
   - A) 90 | B) 99 | **C) 100** | D) 105
   - *Original × 1.10 = 110. Original = 110 ÷ 1.10 = 100.*

52. A coat originally costs $200. It is first increased by 10%, then decreased by 10%. What is the final price?
   - A) $196 | **B) $198** | C) $200 | D) $202
   - *After 10% increase: $200 × 1.10 = $220. After 10% decrease: $220 × 0.90 = $198.*

53. Increase $350 by 20%.
   - A) $370 | B) $390 | C) $410 | **D) $420**
   - *$350 × 1.20 = $420.*

54. Decrease 600 by 35%.
   - A) 210 | B) 300 | C) 360 | **D) 390**
   - *600 × 0.65 = 390.*

55. A taxi fare goes from $12 to $14.40. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 15% | B) 18% | **C) 20%** | D) 24%
   - *Increase = $2.40. % increase = 2.40/12 × 100% = 20%.*

56. A discount of 40% is applied to a $90 dress. What is the sale price?
   - A) $36 | B) $45 | C) $50 | **D) $54**
   - *$90 × 0.60 = $54.*

57. NTUC offers a 15% discount on a $6.00 packet of rice. What is the discounted price?
   - A) $4.80 | **B) $5.10** | C) $5.25 | D) $5.50
   - *$6.00 × 0.85 = $5.10.*

58. The number of MRT breakdowns decreased from 40 to 30 in a year. What is the percentage decrease?
   - A) 10% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 30%
   - *Decrease = 10. % decrease = 10/40 × 100% = 25%.*

59. A worker's salary increases from $2400 to $2640. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 8% | **B) 10%** | C) 12% | D) 15%
   - *Increase = $240. % increase = 240/2400 × 100% = 10%.*

60. The temperature drops from 32°C to 28°C. What is the percentage decrease (to 1 d.p.)?
   - A) 8.5% | B) 10.0% | **C) 12.5%** | D) 15.0%
   - *Decrease = 4. % decrease = 4/32 × 100% = 12.5%.*

61. A shopkeeper bought a toy for $25 and sold it for $35. What is the percentage profit?
   - A) 28% | B) 35% | **C) 40%** | D) 45%
   - *Profit = $10. % profit = 10/25 × 100% = 40%.*

62. A phone bought for $800 is sold for $600. What is the percentage loss?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 35%
   - *Loss = $200. % loss = 200/800 × 100% = 25%.*

63. A bowl of fishball noodles costs $4.00. After a price increase of 25%, what is the new price?
   - A) $4.25 | B) $4.50 | C) $4.75 | **D) $5.00**
   - *$4.00 × 1.25 = $5.00.*

64. After a 20% discount, you save $16. What was the original price?
   - A) $64 | B) $72 | **C) $80** | D) $96
   - *20% of original = $16. Original = $16 ÷ 0.20 = $80.*

65. A value increases from 80 to 120. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 30% | B) 40% | C) 45% | **D) 50%**
   - *Increase = 40. % increase = 40/80 × 100% = 50%.*

66. Decrease $450 by 8%.
   - A) $396 | B) $405 | **C) $414** | D) $420
   - *$450 × 0.92 = $414.*

67. A item's price is first increased by 20% then decreased by 20%. The final price compared to the original is:
   - A) Same | **B) 4% less** | C) 4% more | D) 2% less
   - *Original × 1.20 × 0.80 = Original × 0.96. This is 4% less.*

68. A hawker sells 200 plates of nasi lemak on Monday and 260 on Tuesday. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 20% | B) 25% | **C) 30%** | D) 35%
   - *Increase = 60. % increase = 60/200 × 100% = 30%.*

69. A company made a profit of $15,000 on a cost of $60,000. What is the percentage profit?
   - A) 15% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 30%
   - *% profit = 15,000/60,000 × 100% = 25%.*

70. During a sale, a $240 bag is marked down by $72. What is the percentage discount?
   - A) 25% | B) 28% | **C) 30%** | D) 33%
   - *% discount = 72/240 × 100% = 30%.*

71. A BTO flat increased in value from $250,000 to $325,000. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 25% | B) 28% | **C) 30%** | D) 35%
   - *Increase = $75,000. % increase = 75,000/250,000 × 100% = 30%.*

72. The number of tourists rose from 1.2 million to 1.5 million. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 20% | **B) 25%** | C) 30% | D) 35%
   - *Increase = 0.3 million. % increase = 0.3/1.2 × 100% = 25%.*

73. A $500 bicycle is sold at a 12% loss. What is the selling price?
   - A) $420 | B) $430 | **C) $440** | D) $460
   - *$500 × 0.88 = $440.*

74. After an 8% increase, the new salary is $5400. What was the original salary?
   - A) $4968 | **B) $5000** | C) $5100 | D) $5200
   - *Original × 1.08 = $5400. Original = $5400 ÷ 1.08 = $5000.*

75. After a 20% discount, a pair of shoes costs $80. Find the original price.
   - A) $96 | **B) $100** | C) $104 | D) $120
   - *80% of original = $80. Original = $80 ÷ 0.80 = $100.*

76. After a 25% increase, a value is 150. Find the original value.
   - A) 100 | B) 112.5 | **C) 120** | D) 125
   - *125% of original = 150. Original = 150 ÷ 1.25 = 120.*

77. A price including 9% GST is $54.50. What is the price before GST?
   - A) $49.54 | **B) $50.00** | C) $50.46 | D) $51.00
   - *109% of original = $54.50. Original = $54.50 ÷ 1.09 = $50.00.*

78. After a 10% discount, a bag costs $63. Find the original price.
   - A) $56.70 | B) $65 | C) $69.30 | **D) $70**
   - *90% of original = $63. Original = $63 ÷ 0.90 = $70.*

79. After a 30% increase, a population is 5200. Find the original population.
   - A) 3640 | B) 3800 | **C) 4000** | D) 4200
   - *130% of original = 5200. Original = 5200 ÷ 1.30 = 4000.*

80. A phone costs $872 after 9% GST. What is the price before GST?
   - A) $790 | **B) $800** | C) $810 | D) $820
   - *109% of original = $872. Original = $872 ÷ 1.09 = $800.*

### REVERSE PERCENTAGE (Q81–115)

81. After a 15% discount, a jacket costs $170. Find the original price.
   - A) $190 | B) $195 | C) $196 | **D) $200**
   - *85% of original = $170. Original = $170 ÷ 0.85 = $200.*

82. A shop sells an item at 40% profit. The selling price is $84. Find the cost price.
   - A) $50 | B) $55 | **C) $60** | D) $65
   - *140% of cost = $84. Cost = $84 ÷ 1.40 = $60.*

83. After a 5% decrease, a tank holds 475 litres. Find the original capacity.
   - A) 490 | B) 495 | **C) 500** | D) 505
   - *95% of original = 475. Original = 475 ÷ 0.95 = 500.*

84. A hawker meal costs $5.45 including 9% GST. What is the price before GST?
   - A) $4.95 | **B) $5.00** | C) $5.05 | D) $5.10
   - *109% of original = $5.45. Original = $5.45 ÷ 1.09 = $5.00.*

85. After a 20% increase, a flat costs $360,000. Find the original price.
   - A) $280,000 | B) $288,000 | **C) $300,000** | D) $320,000
   - *120% of original = $360,000. Original = $360,000 ÷ 1.20 = $300,000.*

86. After a 35% discount, a television costs $650. Find the original price.
   - A) $900 | B) $950 | **C) $1000** | D) $1050
   - *65% of original = $650. Original = $650 ÷ 0.65 = $1000.*

87. A car depreciates by 12%. Its current value is $44,000. Find the value before depreciation.
   - A) $48,000 | B) $49,000 | **C) $50,000** | D) $52,000
   - *88% of original = $44,000. Original = $44,000 ÷ 0.88 = $50,000.*

88. After adding 9% GST, a restaurant bill is $163.50. What is the bill before GST?
   - A) $145 | B) $148.50 | **C) $150** | D) $155
   - *109% of original = $163.50. Original = $163.50 ÷ 1.09 = $150.*

89. After a 25% discount, a watch costs $375. Find the original price.
   - A) $450 | B) $468.75 | C) $475 | **D) $500**
   - *75% of original = $375. Original = $375 ÷ 0.75 = $500.*

90. A bookshop makes a 20% profit selling a book for $18. Find the cost price.
   - A) $14 | B) $14.40 | **C) $15** | D) $16
   - *120% of cost = $18. Cost = $18 ÷ 1.20 = $15.*

91. After an 8% pay rise, a worker earns $3240. What was the original pay?
   - A) $2900 | B) $2980 | **C) $3000** | D) $3050
   - *108% of original = $3240. Original = $3240 ÷ 1.08 = $3000.*

92. After a 50% increase, the number of volunteers is 180. How many were there originally?
   - A) 90 | B) 100 | C) 110 | **D) 120**
   - *150% of original = 180. Original = 180 ÷ 1.50 = 120.*

93. A laptop costs $1635 after 9% GST. Find the price before GST.
   - A) $1450 | B) $1480 | **C) $1500** | D) $1520
   - *109% of original = $1635. Original = $1635 ÷ 1.09 = $1500.*

94. After a 40% discount, a sofa costs $780. Find the original price.
   - A) $1100 | B) $1200 | C) $1250 | **D) $1300**
   - *60% of original = $780. Original = $780 ÷ 0.60 = $1300.*

95. After a 15% increase, a bus fare is $1.38. What was the original fare?
   - A) $1.10 | B) $1.15 | C) $1.17 | **D) $1.20**
   - *115% of original = $1.38. Original = $1.38 ÷ 1.15 = $1.20.*

96. A shirt is sold at a 25% loss for $45. Find the cost price.
   - A) $55 | B) $56.25 | C) $58 | **D) $60**
   - *75% of cost = $45. Cost = $45 ÷ 0.75 = $60.*

97. After a 6% increase, electricity consumption is 530 kWh. Find the original consumption.
   - A) $490 | B) 495 | C) 498 | **D) 500**
   - *106% of original = 530. Original = 530 ÷ 1.06 = 500.*

98. A dinner costs $87.20 including 9% GST. What is the price before GST?
   - A) $78 | B) $79 | **C) $80** | D) $82
   - *109% of original = $87.20. Original = $87.20 ÷ 1.09 = $80.*

99. After losing 18% of its weight, a bag of rice weighs 8.2 kg. Find the original weight.
   - A) 9.5 kg | B) 9.8 kg | **C) 10 kg** | D) 10.2 kg
   - *82% of original = 8.2. Original = 8.2 ÷ 0.82 = 10 kg.*

100. A taxi fare including a 10% surcharge is $16.50. What is the base fare?
   - A) $14 | B) $14.50 | **C) $15** | D) $15.50
   - *110% of base = $16.50. Base = $16.50 ÷ 1.10 = $15.*

101. After a 45% discount, a pair of sneakers costs $110. Find the original price.
   - A) $180 | B) $190 | C) $195 | **D) $200**
   - *55% of original = $110. Original = $110 ÷ 0.55 = $200.*

102. A property increased by 25% to $625,000. Find the original value.
   - A) $468,750 | B) $480,000 | **C) $500,000** | D) $520,000
   - *125% of original = $625,000. Original = $625,000 ÷ 1.25 = $500,000.*

103. After a 2% decrease, a population is 49,000. Find the original population.
   - A) 48,000 | B) 49,500 | **C) 50,000** | D) 50,500
   - *98% of original = 49,000. Original = 49,000 ÷ 0.98 = 50,000.*

104. A bike sold at a 30% profit for $520. Find the cost price.
   - A) $364 | B) $380 | C) $390 | **D) $400**
   - *130% of cost = $520. Cost = $520 ÷ 1.30 = $400.*

105. A hotel room costs $327 after 9% GST. Find the price before GST.
   - A) $295 | B) $298 | **C) $300** | D) $305
   - *109% of original = $327. Original = $327 ÷ 1.09 = $300.*

106. After a 16% increase, rent is $1740. Find the original rent.
   - A) $1400 | B) $1450 | **C) $1500** | D) $1550
   - *116% of original = $1740. Original = $1740 ÷ 1.16 = $1500.*

107. The price of a washing machine after a 22% discount is $3120. Find the original price.
   - A) $3800 | B) $3900 | **C) $4000** | D) $4200
   - *78% of original = $3120. Original = $3120 ÷ 0.78 = $4000.*

108. After a 60% increase, a share price is $4.80. What was the original price?
   - A) $2.80 | **B) $3.00** | C) $3.20 | D) $3.50
   - *160% of original = $4.80. Original = $4.80 ÷ 1.60 = $3.00.*

109. A spa treatment costs $218 including 9% GST. Find the price before GST.
   - A) $195 | B) $198 | **C) $200** | D) $205
   - *109% of original = $218. Original = $218 ÷ 1.09 = $200.*

110. A dress costs $120 before GST. After adding 9% GST and then a 20% discount on the GST-inclusive price, what is the final price?
   - A) $96.00 | B) $100.80 | **C) $104.64** | D) $108.00
   - *With GST: $120 × 1.09 = $130.80. After 20% discount: $130.80 × 0.80 = $104.64.*

111. Ali saves 15% of his monthly salary. If he saves $525, what is his salary?
   - A) $3000 | B) $3200 | **C) $3500** | D) $4000
   - *15% of salary = $525. Salary = $525 ÷ 0.15 = $3,500.*

112. A school has 1200 students. 55% are boys. How many girls are there?
   - A) 480 | **B) 540** | C) 600 | D) 660
   - *Girls = 45% of 1200 = 0.45 × 1200 = 540.*

113. A hawker buys chicken for $4 per kg and sells it at $5 per kg. What is the percentage profit?
   - A) 15% | B) 20% | **C) 25%** | D) 30%
   - *Profit = $1. % profit = 1/4 × 100% = 25%.*

114. A $1500 laptop depreciates by 20% each year. What is its value after 2 years?
   - A) $900 | **B) $960** | C) $1000 | D) $1080
   - *After 1 year: $1500 × 0.80 = $1200. After 2 years: $1200 × 0.80 = $960.*

115. Mei buys 3 items at NTUC: $4.50, $7.20, $8.30. She has a 10% member discount on the total. What does she pay?
   - A) $16.00 | **B) $18.00** | C) $18.90 | D) $20.00
   - *Total = $4.50 + $7.20 + $8.30 = $20.00. After 10% discount: $20.00 × 0.90 = $18.00.*

### PERCENTAGE WORD PROBLEMS (Q116–150)

116. A class of 40 students took a test. 85% passed. How many failed?
   - A) 4 | B) 5 | **C) 6** | D) 8
   - *Failed = 15% of 40 = 0.15 × 40 = 6.*

117. A car costs $80,000. A down payment of 30% is required. How much is the down payment?
   - A) $20,000 | **B) $24,000** | C) $28,000 | D) $30,000
   - *30% of $80,000 = 0.30 × $80,000 = $24,000.*

118. A recipe needs 400 g of flour. Siti wants to increase it by 75%. How much flour does she need?
   - A) 475 g | B) 600 g | C) 675 g | **D) 700 g**
   - *400 g × 1.75 = 700 g.*

119. An employee earns $3600. After a 5% pay cut and then a 5% pay rise, what is the new salary?
   - **A) $3591** | B) $3596 | C) $3600 | D) $3609
   - *After cut: $3600 × 0.95 = $3420. After rise: $3420 × 1.05 = $3591.*

120. Ahmad scored 45 out of 60 on Paper 1 and 56 out of 80 on Paper 2. Which paper had a higher percentage score?
   - **A) Paper 1 (75%)** | B) Paper 2 (70%) | C) Both the same | D) Cannot tell
   - *Paper 1: 45/60 × 100% = 75%. Paper 2: 56/80 × 100% = 70%. Paper 1 is higher.*

121. A shop buys 50 shirts at $20 each. 80% sell at $26 and the rest at $24. Find the overall percentage profit.
   - A) 25% | B) 27% | **C) 28%** | D) 30%
   - *Cost = 50 × $20 = $1000. Revenue = 40 × $26 + 10 × $24 = $1040 + $240 = $1280. Profit = $280. % profit = 280/1000 × 100% = 28%.*

122. Water makes up 60% of a person's body weight. If a student weighs 50 kg, how much water is in their body?
   - A) 20 kg | B) 25 kg | **C) 30 kg** | D) 35 kg
   - *60% of 50 kg = 0.60 × 50 = 30 kg.*

123. A tank is 40% full and contains 200 litres. What is the full capacity?
   - A) 300 litres | B) 400 litres | **C) 500 litres** | D) 600 litres
   - *40% of capacity = 200. Capacity = 200 ÷ 0.40 = 500 litres.*

124. In a sale, successive discounts of 10% and 20% are applied. What single discount is equivalent?
   - **A) 28%** | B) 29% | C) 30% | D) 32%
   - *Combined multiplier: 0.90 × 0.80 = 0.72. Equivalent discount = 1 − 0.72 = 0.28 = 28%.*

125. A $50 meal is subject to 10% service charge, then 9% GST on the total. What is the final bill?
   - A) $57.50 | **B) $59.95** | C) $60.50 | D) $62.00
   - *After service charge: $50 × 1.10 = $55. After GST: $55 × 1.09 = $59.95.*

126. The price of petrol increased by 8% to $2.70 per litre. What was the original price?
   - A) $2.40 | B) $2.48 | **C) $2.50** | D) $2.55
   - *108% of original = $2.70. Original = $2.70 ÷ 1.08 = $2.50.*

127. A student answered 90% of 40 questions correctly. How many did they get wrong?
   - A) 2 | B) 3 | **C) 4** | D) 6
   - *Correct = 90% of 40 = 36. Wrong = 40 − 36 = 4.*

128. A shopkeeper marks up an item by 50% then offers a 20% discount. What is the overall percentage profit?
   - **A) 20%** | B) 25% | C) 30% | D) 35%
   - *Markup: × 1.50. Discount: × 0.80. Overall: 1.50 × 0.80 = 1.20. Profit = 20%.*

129. Lina spent 25% of her allowance on food, 40% on transport, and saved the rest. If she saved $21, what was her allowance?
   - A) $50 | B) $55 | **C) $60** | D) $70
   - *Saved = 100% − 25% − 40% = 35%. 35% of allowance = $21. Allowance = $21 ÷ 0.35 = $60.*

130. A shop bought 100 pens for $0.80 each and sold them at $1.20 each. 15 pens were damaged and thrown away. Find the percentage profit.
   - A) 20% | B) 25% | **C) 27.5%** | D) 30%
   - *Cost = 100 × $0.80 = $80. Revenue = 85 × $1.20 = $102. Profit = $22. % profit = 22/80 × 100% = 27.5%.*

131. The value of a car decreased from $60,000 to $48,000 over 2 years. What is the average percentage decrease per year if the decrease is the same each year?
   - A) 8% | **B) 10%** | C) 12% | D) 15%
   - *Total decrease = $12,000 over 2 years = $6,000 per year. % decrease = 6,000/60,000 × 100% = 10%. (Note: this is simple, not compound, depreciation.)*

132. A fruit seller bought 200 oranges at $0.50 each. 10% were rotten. He sold the good ones at $0.80 each. Find his percentage profit.
   - A) 32% | B) 40% | **C) 44%** | D) 48%
   - *Cost = 200 × $0.50 = $100. Good oranges = 180. Revenue = 180 × $0.80 = $144. Profit = $44. % profit = 44/100 × 100% = 44%.*

133. A concert venue with 2000 seats is 85% full. If 5% of ticket holders don't show up, how many people attend?
   - A) 1600 | **B) 1615** | C) 1620 | D) 1700
   - *Tickets sold = 85% of 2000 = 1700. Attend = 95% of 1700 = 1615.*

134. GST in Singapore is raised from 8% to 9%. A meal costs $25 before GST. How much more do you pay under the new GST rate?
   - A) $0.15 | **B) $0.25** | C) $0.50 | D) $1.00
   - *Old GST: 8% of $25 = $2.00. New GST: 9% of $25 = $2.25. Difference = $0.25.*

135. A compound increases by 10% in the first year and 20% in the second year. What is the overall percentage increase?
   - A) 30% | B) 31% | **C) 32%** | D) 33%
   - *Overall multiplier = 1.10 × 1.20 = 1.32. Overall increase = 32%.*

136. After spending 30% of his money on a bag and 25% of the remainder on shoes, Ravi has $315 left. How much did he start with?
   - A) $500 | B) $550 | **C) $600** | D) $650
   - *After bag: 70% left. After shoes: 75% of 70% = 52.5% left. 52.5% of original = $315. Original = $315 ÷ 0.525 = $600.*

137. An item's price is increased by 25%. What percentage decrease is needed to return to the original price?
   - A) 15% | **B) 20%** | C) 25% | D) 30%
   - *New = 1.25 × original. To return: need to multiply by 1/1.25 = 0.80. Decrease = 20%.*

138. A shop offers 'Buy 2 Get 1 Free' on $12 items. What is the effective percentage discount per item?
   - A) 25% | B) 30% | **C) 33⅓%** | D) 50%
   - *Pay for 2, get 3. Average cost = $24/3 = $8. Discount per item = $4/$12 × 100% = 33⅓%.*

139. The population of a town increased by 10% in 2023 and decreased by 10% in 2024. If the population at the end of 2024 was 19,800, what was it at the start of 2023?
   - A) 18,000 | B) 19,000 | **C) 20,000** | D) 21,000
   - *Let original = x. After +10%: 1.1x. After −10%: 1.1x × 0.9 = 0.99x. 0.99x = 19,800. x = 20,000.*

140. A retailer buys goods at $400 and wants a 30% profit after allowing a 20% discount on the marked price. What should the marked price be?
   - A) $520 | B) $600 | **C) $650** | D) $700
   - *Selling price needed = $400 × 1.30 = $520. Marked price × 0.80 = $520. Marked price = $520 ÷ 0.80 = $650.*

141. Samy invested $10,000. He gained 15% in Year 1 and lost 10% in Year 2. How much does he have at the end of Year 2?
   - A) $10,250 | **B) $10,350** | C) $10,450 | D) $10,500
   - *After Year 1: $10,000 × 1.15 = $11,500. After Year 2: $11,500 × 0.90 = $10,350.*

142. A meal at a restaurant has a list price of $40. A 10% service charge is added first, then 9% GST on the total. Find the final amount.
   - A) $47.60 | **B) $47.96** | C) $48.00 | D) $48.40
   - *After service charge: $40 × 1.10 = $44. After GST: $44 × 1.09 = $47.96.*

143. Three friends split a restaurant bill. The food costs $90 before 10% service charge and 9% GST (applied on the total including service charge). How much does each person pay?
   - A) $35.64 | **B) $35.97** | C) $36.30 | D) $37.00
   - *After service charge: $90 × 1.10 = $99. After GST: $99 × 1.09 = $107.91. Per person: $107.91 ÷ 3 = $35.97.*

144. A property worth $500,000 appreciates by 4% per year (compound). What is its value after 2 years?
   - A) $540,000 | **B) $540,800** | C) $541,200 | D) $542,000
   - *After 1 year: $500,000 × 1.04 = $520,000. After 2 years: $520,000 × 1.04 = $540,800.*

145. A school canteen raises the price of a set meal from $2.50 to $3.00. What is the percentage increase?
   - A) 15% | B) 18% | **C) 20%** | D) 25%
   - *Increase = $0.50. % increase = 0.50/2.50 × 100% = 20%.*

146. Xiao Ming scored 68% on his first test and 85% on his second test. By how many percentage points did his score improve?
   - A) 15 | **B) 17** | C) 20 | D) 25
   - *Improvement = 85% − 68% = 17 percentage points.*

147. A shop gives a 10% loyalty discount and then a further 5% off. What is the overall percentage discount?
   - **A) 14.5%** | B) 15% | C) 15.5% | D) 16%
   - *Combined: 0.90 × 0.95 = 0.855. Discount = 1 − 0.855 = 14.5%.*

148. A worker earns $2800 per month. CPF contribution is 20% of salary. How much goes to CPF?
   - A) $420 | B) $480 | C) $540 | **D) $560**
   - *20% of $2800 = 0.20 × $2800 = $560.*

149. A carpark has 500 lots. On Monday 72% are occupied and on Tuesday 85% are occupied. How many more cars on Tuesday?
   - A) 55 | B) 60 | **C) 65** | D) 70
   - *Monday: 360 cars. Tuesday: 425 cars. Difference = 65.*

150. After a 12% discount, you pay $264 for a tablet. What was the original price?
   - A) $280 | B) $290 | C) $295 | **D) $300**
   - *88% of original = $264. Original = $264 ÷ 0.88 = $300.*

## Topic 9: Ratio, Rate & Speed
*Ratio, proportion, rate, speed-distance-time* — 150 questions

### SIMPLIFY RATIO (Q1–38)

1. Simplify the ratio 12 : 18.
   - **A) 2 : 3** | B) 3 : 4 | C) 4 : 6 | D) 6 : 9
   - *HCF of 12 and 18 is 6. 12 ÷ 6 : 18 ÷ 6 = 2 : 3.*

2. Simplify the ratio 15 : 25.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 3 : 5** | C) 5 : 8 | D) 5 : 10
   - *HCF of 15 and 25 is 5. 15 ÷ 5 : 25 ÷ 5 = 3 : 5.*

3. Simplify the ratio 24 : 36.
   - **A) 2 : 3** | B) 3 : 4 | C) 4 : 6 | D) 6 : 9
   - *HCF of 24 and 36 is 12. 24 ÷ 12 : 36 ÷ 12 = 2 : 3.*

4. Simplify the ratio 8 : 12 : 20.
   - A) 2 : 3 : 4 | **B) 2 : 3 : 5** | C) 4 : 6 : 10 | D) 1 : 2 : 3
   - *HCF of 8, 12, 20 is 4. 8 ÷ 4 : 12 ÷ 4 : 20 ÷ 4 = 2 : 3 : 5.*

5. Simplify the ratio 45 : 60.
   - **A) 3 : 4** | B) 4 : 5 | C) 5 : 6 | D) 9 : 12
   - *HCF of 45 and 60 is 15. 45 ÷ 15 : 60 ÷ 15 = 3 : 4.*

6. Express the ratio 1.5 : 2.5 in its simplest form.
   - A) 3 : 4 | **B) 3 : 5** | C) 15 : 25 | D) 1 : 2
   - *Multiply by 2: 3 : 5. Already in simplest form.*

7. Express the ratio ½ : ¾ in its simplest form.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 2 : 3** | C) 3 : 4 | D) 4 : 6
   - *Multiply both by 4: 2 : 3.*

8. Simplify the ratio 100 : 250.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 2 : 5** | C) 4 : 10 | D) 10 : 25
   - *HCF of 100 and 250 is 50. 100 ÷ 50 : 250 ÷ 50 = 2 : 5.*

9. Simplify the ratio 0.6 : 0.9.
   - **A) 2 : 3** | B) 3 : 4 | C) 6 : 9 | D) 1 : 2
   - *Multiply by 10: 6 : 9. HCF = 3. 6 ÷ 3 : 9 ÷ 3 = 2 : 3.*

10. Express 20 cm : 1 m as a ratio in simplest form.
   - **A) 1 : 5** | B) 2 : 10 | C) 20 : 1 | D) 1 : 50
   - *Convert to same units: 20 cm : 100 cm = 20 : 100 = 1 : 5.*

11. Express 500 g : 2 kg in simplest form.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 1 : 4** | C) 5 : 2 | D) 5 : 20
   - *Convert: 500 g : 2000 g = 500 : 2000 = 1 : 4.*

12. Simplify 18 : 27 : 45.
   - **A) 2 : 3 : 5** | B) 6 : 9 : 15 | C) 3 : 4 : 5 | D) 1 : 2 : 3
   - *HCF of 18, 27, 45 is 9. 18 ÷ 9 : 27 ÷ 9 : 45 ÷ 9 = 2 : 3 : 5.*

13. Express the ratio ⅓ : ½ in simplest form.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 2 : 3** | C) 3 : 2 | D) 1 : 3
   - *Multiply both by 6: 2 : 3.*

14. Express 30 minutes : 2 hours as a ratio.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 1 : 4** | C) 3 : 20 | D) 15 : 1
   - *Convert: 30 min : 120 min = 30 : 120 = 1 : 4.*

15. If a : b = 3 : 4, find a : b when a = 15.
   - A) 15 : 16 | B) 15 : 18 | **C) 15 : 20** | D) 15 : 24
   - *3 : 4 = 15 : ? → multiply by 5 → 15 : 20.*

16. The ratio of boys to girls is 5 : 7. If there are 35 boys, how many girls are there?
   - A) 42 | B) 45 | C) 47 | **D) 49**
   - *5 parts = 35, so 1 part = 7. Girls = 7 × 7 = 49.*

17. Simplify 2.4 : 3.6 : 6.
   - **A) 2 : 3 : 5** | B) 4 : 6 : 10 | C) 1 : 2 : 3 | D) 2 : 3 : 5
   - *Multiply by 5: 12 : 18 : 30. HCF = 6. 2 : 3 : 5.*

18. Express 250 ml : 1 litre in simplest form.
   - A) 1 : 2 | **B) 1 : 4** | C) 25 : 1 | D) 5 : 2
   - *250 ml : 1000 ml = 1 : 4.*

19. Divide $180 in the ratio 2 : 3.
   - A) $60 and $120 | **B) $72 and $108** | C) $80 and $100 | D) $90 and $90
   - *Total parts = 5. First = 2/5 × $180 = $72. Second = 3/5 × $180 = $108.*

20. Divide 200 sweets in the ratio 3 : 5.
   - A) 60 and 140 | **B) 75 and 125** | C) 80 and 120 | D) 100 and 100
   - *Total parts = 8. First = 3/8 × 200 = 75. Second = 5/8 × 200 = 125.*

21. Divide $450 among A, B, C in the ratio 2 : 3 : 4.
   - **A) $100, $150, $200** | B) $90, $150, $210 | C) $120, $150, $180 | D) $80, $170, $200
   - *Total parts = 9. A = 2/9 × $450 = $100. B = 3/9 × $450 = $150. C = 4/9 × $450 = $200.*

22. The ratio of red to blue beads is 3 : 7. If there are 50 beads in total, how many are red?
   - A) 10 | B) 12 | **C) 15** | D) 20
   - *Red = 3/10 × 50 = 15.*

23. A recipe for pineapple tarts uses flour and butter in the ratio 5 : 2. If 350 g of flour is used, how much butter is needed?
   - A) 100 g | B) 120 g | C) 130 g | **D) 140 g**
   - *5 parts = 350 g, 1 part = 70 g. Butter = 2 × 70 = 140 g.*

24. Ali and Bala share ang baos in the ratio 4 : 5. If Bala gets $15 more than Ali, how much does Ali get?
   - A) $40 | B) $50 | **C) $60** | D) $75
   - *Difference = 1 part = $15. Ali = 4 × $15 = $60.*

25. In a CNY reunion dinner, the ratio of adults to children is 5 : 3. If there are 40 people, how many children are there?
   - A) 12 | **B) 15** | C) 18 | D) 20
   - *Total parts = 8. Children = 3/8 × 40 = 15.*

26. A rope of length 1.8 m is cut in the ratio 2 : 7. Find the length of the shorter piece.
   - A) 0.2 m | B) 0.36 m | **C) 0.4 m** | D) 0.9 m
   - *Total parts = 9. Shorter = 2/9 × 1.8 = 0.4 m.*

27. The ratio of Malay to Chinese students in a class is 2 : 5. If there are 35 students, how many are Malay?
   - A) 5 | B) 8 | **C) 10** | D) 14
   - *Total parts = 7. Malay = 2/7 × 35 = 10.*

28. Simplify 1¼ : 2½.
   - **A) 1 : 2** | B) 1 : 3 | C) 5 : 10 | D) 3 : 5
   - *1¼ = 5/4 and 2½ = 10/4. Ratio = 5 : 10 = 1 : 2.*

29. If x : 12 = 5 : 6, find x.
   - A) 8 | **B) 10** | C) 12 | D) 15
   - *x/12 = 5/6. x = 12 × 5/6 = 10.*

30. Divide 720 g of rice in the ratio 5 : 3 : 1.
   - **A) 400, 240, 80** | B) 350, 250, 120 | C) 380, 240, 100 | D) 360, 240, 120
   - *Total = 9 parts. 5/9 × 720 = 400. 3/9 × 720 = 240. 1/9 × 720 = 80.*

31. The ages of two siblings are in the ratio 3 : 5. If the older is 15, how old is the younger?
   - A) 7 | B) 8 | **C) 9** | D) 10
   - *5 parts = 15, 1 part = 3. Younger = 3 × 3 = 9.*

32. Map scale is 1 : 50,000. A distance on the map is 4 cm. Find the actual distance in km.
   - A) 0.5 km | B) 1 km | **C) 2 km** | D) 4 km
   - *Actual = 4 × 50,000 = 200,000 cm = 2000 m = 2 km.*

33. If a : b = 2 : 3 and b : c = 3 : 4, find a : b : c.
   - **A) 2 : 3 : 4** | B) 4 : 6 : 8 | C) 2 : 3 : 6 | D) 4 : 3 : 2
   - *b is common. a : b = 2 : 3 and b : c = 3 : 4. So a : b : c = 2 : 3 : 4.*

34. Express 45 seconds : 2 minutes in simplest form.
   - **A) 3 : 8** | B) 9 : 24 | C) 45 : 2 | D) 1 : 3
   - *Convert: 45 s : 120 s. HCF = 15. 3 : 8.*

35. If a : b = 4 : 7 and a + b = 55, find a.
   - A) 15 | **B) 20** | C) 25 | D) 30
   - *Total = 11 parts. a = 4/11 × 55 = 20.*

36. Three siblings share $240 in the ratio of their ages: 4, 6, and 10. The youngest gets:
   - **A) $48** | B) $60 | C) $72 | D) $120
   - *Total parts = 20. Youngest = 4/20 × $240 = $48.*

37. A drink is made by mixing syrup and water in the ratio 1 : 4. How much water is needed for 300 ml of syrup?
   - A) 600 ml | B) 900 ml | **C) 1200 ml** | D) 1500 ml
   - *1 part = 300 ml. Water = 4 × 300 = 1200 ml.*

38. The ratio of savings to spending is 2 : 8. Express savings as a fraction of total income.
   - A) 1/4 | **B) 1/5** | C) 2/8 | D) 2/10
   - *Total = 10 parts. Savings = 2/10 = 1/5.*

### PROPORTION (Q39–72)

39. If 3 pens cost $4.50, how much do 7 pens cost?
   - A) $9.00 | B) $9.50 | **C) $10.50** | D) $12.00
   - *1 pen = $4.50 ÷ 3 = $1.50. 7 pens = 7 × $1.50 = $10.50.*

40. If 5 kg of rice costs $8, how much does 12 kg cost?
   - A) $16.00 | B) $17.60 | **C) $19.20** | D) $20.00
   - *1 kg = $8 ÷ 5 = $1.60. 12 kg = 12 × $1.60 = $19.20.*

41. 8 workers can build a wall in 6 days. How many days will 12 workers take?
   - A) 3 | **B) 4** | C) 5 | D) 9
   - *More workers, less time (inverse proportion). 8 × 6 = 48 worker-days. 48 ÷ 12 = 4 days.*

42. A recipe for 4 servings needs 300 g of chicken. How much for 10 servings?
   - A) 600 g | B) 700 g | **C) 750 g** | D) 800 g
   - *1 serving = 300 ÷ 4 = 75 g. 10 servings = 75 × 10 = 750 g.*

43. If 6 apples cost $2.40, how much do 15 apples cost?
   - A) $4.50 | B) $5.00 | **C) $6.00** | D) $7.50
   - *1 apple = $2.40 ÷ 6 = $0.40. 15 apples = 15 × $0.40 = $6.00.*

44. A car travels 240 km on 20 litres of petrol. How far can it travel on 35 litres?
   - A) 360 km | B) 400 km | **C) 420 km** | D) 450 km
   - *1 litre = 240 ÷ 20 = 12 km. 35 litres = 35 × 12 = 420 km.*

45. If 4 tins of paint cover 60 m², how many tins are needed to cover 105 m²?
   - A) 5 | B) 6 | **C) 7** | D) 8
   - *1 tin covers 15 m². 105 ÷ 15 = 7 tins.*

46. A tap fills a tank in 8 hours. What fraction is filled in 3 hours?
   - A) 1/3 | **B) 3/8** | C) 1/2 | D) 5/8
   - *In 3 hours, 3/8 of the tank is filled.*

47. 12 packets of chips cost $18. How much do 20 packets cost?
   - A) $24 | B) $27 | **C) $30** | D) $36
   - *1 packet = $18 ÷ 12 = $1.50. 20 packets = 20 × $1.50 = $30.*

48. A printer prints 120 pages in 8 minutes. How many pages in 15 minutes?
   - A) 180 | B) 200 | C) 210 | **D) 225**
   - *Rate = 120 ÷ 8 = 15 pages/min. In 15 min: 15 × 15 = 225 pages.*

49. If the exchange rate is S$1 = RM 3.40, how many RM for S$50?
   - A) RM 150 | B) RM 160 | **C) RM 170** | D) RM 180
   - *S$50 × 3.40 = RM 170.*

50. 5 identical books weigh 1.25 kg. What do 8 books weigh?
   - A) 1.60 kg | B) 1.80 kg | **C) 2.00 kg** | D) 2.25 kg
   - *1 book = 1.25 ÷ 5 = 0.25 kg. 8 books = 8 × 0.25 = 2.00 kg.*

51. A map has a scale of 1 : 25,000. Two towns are 8 cm apart on the map. What is the actual distance?
   - A) 1 km | **B) 2 km** | C) 2.5 km | D) 4 km
   - *8 × 25,000 = 200,000 cm = 2000 m = 2 km.*

52. If 3 workers take 10 days to complete a job, how many days will 5 workers take?
   - A) 4 | B) 5 | **C) 6** | D) 8
   - *Inverse proportion. 3 × 10 = 30 worker-days. 30 ÷ 5 = 6 days.*

53. A recipe for kueh lapis uses 200 g sugar for 12 slices. How much sugar for 30 slices?
   - A) 400 g | B) 450 g | **C) 500 g** | D) 600 g
   - *1 slice = 200/12 g. 30 slices = 30 × 200/12 = 500 g.*

54. At NTUC, 3 cans of sardines cost $5.85. How much for 5 cans?
   - A) $8.75 | B) $9.50 | **C) $9.75** | D) $10.25
   - *1 can = $5.85 ÷ 3 = $1.95. 5 cans = 5 × $1.95 = $9.75.*

55. A photocopier makes 60 copies in 4 minutes. How long to make 210 copies?
   - A) 12 min | **B) 14 min** | C) 16 min | D) 18 min
   - *Rate = 15 copies/min. 210 ÷ 15 = 14 min.*

56. 6 identical tiles cover an area of 1800 cm². How many tiles cover 4500 cm²?
   - A) 12 | **B) 15** | C) 18 | D) 20
   - *1 tile = 300 cm². 4500 ÷ 300 = 15 tiles.*

57. If S$1 = US$0.74, convert S$200 to US$.
   - A) US$120 | B) US$135 | **C) US$148** | D) US$170
   - *S$200 × 0.74 = US$148.*

58. A train takes 2 hours to travel 150 km. At the same speed, how far in 3.5 hours?
   - A) 225 km | B) 250 km | **C) 262.5 km** | D) 275 km
   - *Speed = 75 km/h. Distance = 75 × 3.5 = 262.5 km.*

59. A factory produces 840 toys in 7 hours. How many toys in 5 hours?
   - A) 500 | B) 550 | C) 580 | **D) 600**
   - *Rate = 120 toys/hour. In 5 hours: 120 × 5 = 600.*

60. If 4 painters can paint a fence in 9 hours, how long will 6 painters take?
   - A) 4 h | B) 5 h | **C) 6 h** | D) 7 h
   - *Inverse proportion. 4 × 9 = 36. 36 ÷ 6 = 6 hours.*

61. A baker uses 2.5 kg of flour for 50 buns. How much for 80 buns?
   - A) 3.5 kg | **B) 4 kg** | C) 4.5 kg | D) 5 kg
   - *1 bun = 0.05 kg. 80 buns = 80 × 0.05 = 4 kg.*

62. If y is directly proportional to x, and y = 12 when x = 4, find y when x = 7.
   - A) 18 | B) 20 | **C) 21** | D) 24
   - *y = kx. k = 12/4 = 3. When x = 7: y = 3 × 7 = 21.*

63. The cost of 250 g of premium tea is $18. What is the cost of 400 g?
   - A) $24.00 | B) $26.80 | **C) $28.80** | D) $30.00
   - *1 g costs $18/250 = $0.072. 400 g = 400 × $0.072 = $28.80.*

64. A school trip costs $540 shared equally among 18 students. If 24 students go instead, how much does each pay?
   - A) $20.50 | **B) $22.50** | C) $25.00 | D) $27.00
   - *Total cost stays $540. Per student = $540 ÷ 24 = $22.50.*

65. A typist types 240 words in 6 minutes. What is her typing speed?
   - A) 30 wpm | B) 35 wpm | **C) 40 wpm** | D) 45 wpm
   - *240 ÷ 6 = 40 words per minute.*

66. Water flows at 15 litres per minute. How many litres in 20 minutes?
   - A) 200 | B) 250 | **C) 300** | D) 350
   - *15 × 20 = 300 litres.*

67. A phone plan costs $28 for 7 GB. What is the cost per GB?
   - A) $3 | B) $3.50 | **C) $4** | D) $4.50
   - *$28 ÷ 7 = $4 per GB.*

68. Apples cost $3.60 per kg. How much for 2.5 kg?
   - A) $7.20 | B) $8.00 | **C) $9.00** | D) $10.00
   - *$3.60 × 2.5 = $9.00.*

69. A factory makes 480 widgets in 8 hours. What is the production rate?
   - A) 40/h | B) 50/h | C) 55/h | **D) 60/h**
   - *480 ÷ 8 = 60 widgets per hour.*

70. Electricity costs $0.28 per kWh. Find the cost for 350 kWh.
   - A) $84 | B) $90 | **C) $98** | D) $105
   - *$0.28 × 350 = $98.*

71. A runner covers 5 km in 25 minutes. What is her speed in km/h?
   - A) 10 km/h | **B) 12 km/h** | C) 15 km/h | D) 20 km/h
   - *25 min = 5/12 h. Speed = 5 ÷ (5/12) = 12 km/h.*

72. Which is a better buy: 500 g for $4.50 or 750 g for $6.00?
   - A) 500 g pack | **B) 750 g pack** | C) Both same | D) Cannot tell
   - *500 g: $9.00/kg. 750 g: $8.00/kg. The 750 g pack is cheaper per kg.*

### RATE (Q73–108)

73. A heart beats 72 times per minute. How many beats in 5 minutes?
   - A) 320 | B) 340 | **C) 360** | D) 380
   - *72 × 5 = 360 beats.*

74. A taxi charges $3.90 flag-down and $0.25 per 400 m. For a 4 km ride, what is the fare?
   - A) $5.40 | **B) $6.40** | C) $6.90 | D) $7.40
   - *4 km = 4000 m. Units of 400 m = 10. Metered charge = 10 × $0.25 = $2.50. Total = $3.90 + $2.50 = $6.40.*

75. A leaking tap drips at 2 ml per second. How many litres leak in 1 hour?
   - A) 3.6 L | **B) 7.2 L** | C) 12 L | D) 72 L
   - *1 hour = 3600 s. 2 × 3600 = 7200 ml = 7.2 L.*

76. Rice costs $2.80 per kg. How many kg can you buy with $14?
   - A) 4 kg | B) 4.5 kg | **C) 5 kg** | D) 5.5 kg
   - *$14 ÷ $2.80 = 5 kg.*

77. A car uses petrol at 8 litres per 100 km. How much petrol for 350 km?
   - A) 24 L | B) 26 L | **C) 28 L** | D) 30 L
   - *8/100 × 350 = 28 litres.*

78. Printing costs $0.15 per page. How many pages for $6?
   - A) 30 | B) 35 | **C) 40** | D) 45
   - *$6 ÷ $0.15 = 40 pages.*

79. A pipe fills a 600-litre tank in 40 minutes. What is the flow rate?
   - A) 12 L/min | **B) 15 L/min** | C) 18 L/min | D) 20 L/min
   - *600 ÷ 40 = 15 litres per minute.*

80. Internet speed is 100 Mbps. How many seconds to download a 500 MB file? (1 byte = 8 bits)
   - A) 5 s | B) 10 s | **C) 40 s** | D) 50 s
   - *500 MB = 4000 Mb. Time = 4000 ÷ 100 = 40 seconds.*

81. A hawker sells chicken rice at $3.50 per plate. He sells 120 plates. What is his revenue?
   - A) $360 | B) $380 | C) $400 | **D) $420**
   - *120 × $3.50 = $420.*

82. Postage costs $0.37 for the first 20 g and $0.25 for each additional 10 g. What is the cost for a 60 g letter?
   - A) $1.12 | **B) $1.37** | C) $1.47 | D) $1.62
   - *First 20 g: $0.37. Additional 40 g = 4 units of 10 g: 4 × $0.25 = $1.00. Total = $1.37.*

83. A machine fills 200 bottles in 5 minutes. How long to fill 720 bottles?
   - A) 14 min | B) 16 min | **C) 18 min** | D) 20 min
   - *Rate = 40 bottles/min. 720 ÷ 40 = 18 min.*

84. A cleaner is paid $12.50 per hour. How much for a 6-hour shift?
   - A) $65 | B) $70 | **C) $75** | D) $80
   - *$12.50 × 6 = $75.*

85. Fuel costs $2.80 per litre. A car uses 45 litres per week. What is the weekly fuel cost?
   - A) $112 | B) $120 | **C) $126** | D) $135
   - *$2.80 × 45 = $126.*

86. An escalator moves at 0.5 m/s. How long to travel 30 m?
   - A) 30 s | B) 45 s | **C) 60 s** | D) 90 s
   - *30 ÷ 0.5 = 60 seconds.*

87. Water costs $2.74 per cubic metre. A household uses 18 m³. What is the water bill?
   - A) $45.32 | B) $47.92 | **C) $49.32** | D) $51.72
   - *$2.74 × 18 = $49.32.*

88. A bus picks up passengers at a rate of 30 per stop. After 8 stops, how many passengers?
   - A) 200 | B) 220 | **C) 240** | D) 280
   - *30 × 8 = 240 passengers.*

89. Brand A: 1.5 L for $2.10. Brand B: 2 L for $3.00. Which is cheaper per litre?
   - **A) Brand A** | B) Brand B | C) Same price | D) Cannot tell
   - *A: $2.10/1.5 = $1.40/L. B: $3.00/2 = $1.50/L. Brand A is cheaper.*

90. A parking lot charges $1.20 per half hour. How much for 3 hours?
   - A) $3.60 | B) $6.00 | **C) $7.20** | D) $8.40
   - *3 hours = 6 half-hours. 6 × $1.20 = $7.20.*

91. A student reads 45 pages per hour. How long to read a 270-page book?
   - A) 4 h | B) 5 h | **C) 6 h** | D) 7 h
   - *270 ÷ 45 = 6 hours.*

92. A call costs $0.18 per minute. If you have $5, what is the maximum whole minutes you can talk?
   - A) 25 | **B) 27** | C) 28 | D) 30
   - *$5 ÷ $0.18 = 27.78. Maximum whole minutes = 27.*

93. A car travels 180 km in 3 hours. What is its speed?
   - A) 45 km/h | B) 50 km/h | C) 55 km/h | **D) 60 km/h**
   - *Speed = 180 ÷ 3 = 60 km/h.*

94. A cyclist rides at 15 km/h for 2 hours. How far does she travel?
   - A) 20 km | B) 25 km | **C) 30 km** | D) 35 km
   - *Distance = 15 × 2 = 30 km.*

95. A jogger runs at 8 km/h. How long to run 6 km?
   - A) 30 min | B) 40 min | **C) 45 min** | D) 50 min
   - *Time = 6 ÷ 8 = 0.75 h = 45 min.*

96. Convert 72 km/h to m/s.
   - A) 12 m/s | B) 15 m/s | C) 18 m/s | **D) 20 m/s**
   - *72 ÷ 3.6 = 20 m/s.*

97. Convert 15 m/s to km/h.
   - A) 45 km/h | B) 50 km/h | **C) 54 km/h** | D) 60 km/h
   - *15 × 3.6 = 54 km/h.*

98. A train travels at 90 km/h. How far does it go in 40 minutes?
   - A) 45 km | B) 50 km | C) 55 km | **D) 60 km**
   - *40 min = 2/3 h. Distance = 90 × 2/3 = 60 km.*

99. An MRT travels 12 km in 15 minutes. What is its speed in km/h?
   - A) 36 km/h | B) 42 km/h | **C) 48 km/h** | D) 54 km/h
   - *15 min = 0.25 h. Speed = 12 ÷ 0.25 = 48 km/h.*

100. A bus takes 45 minutes to travel 30 km. What is the speed?
   - A) 30 km/h | B) 36 km/h | **C) 40 km/h** | D) 45 km/h
   - *45 min = 0.75 h. Speed = 30 ÷ 0.75 = 40 km/h.*

101. A plane flies at 600 km/h. How long to fly 2400 km?
   - A) 3 h | B) 3.5 h | **C) 4 h** | D) 4.5 h
   - *Time = 2400 ÷ 600 = 4 hours.*

102. A boy walks at 5 km/h for 1.5 hours then rests. How far did he walk?
   - A) 5 km | B) 6.5 km | C) 7 km | **D) 7.5 km**
   - *Distance = 5 × 1.5 = 7.5 km.*

103. Convert 36 km/h to m/s.
   - A) 6 m/s | B) 8 m/s | **C) 10 m/s** | D) 12 m/s
   - *36 ÷ 3.6 = 10 m/s.*

104. A car drives 60 km at 40 km/h, then 60 km at 60 km/h. What is the average speed for the whole journey?
   - A) 45 km/h | **B) 48 km/h** | C) 50 km/h | D) 52 km/h
   - *Time 1 = 60/40 = 1.5 h. Time 2 = 60/60 = 1 h. Total = 120 km in 2.5 h. Avg speed = 120/2.5 = 48 km/h.*

105. An athlete runs 100 m in 12.5 s. What is his speed in m/s?
   - A) 6 m/s | B) 7 m/s | **C) 8 m/s** | D) 10 m/s
   - *100 ÷ 12.5 = 8 m/s.*

106. A taxi from Changi Airport to Orchard Road (20 km) takes 25 minutes. What is the average speed?
   - A) 40 km/h | B) 42 km/h | C) 45 km/h | **D) 48 km/h**
   - *25 min = 5/12 h. Speed = 20 ÷ (5/12) = 48 km/h.*

107. A ship sails at 18 km/h. How long to cover 63 km?
   - A) 2.5 h | B) 3 h | **C) 3.5 h** | D) 4 h
   - *Time = 63 ÷ 18 = 3.5 hours.*

108. Two towns are 270 km apart. A car starts at 9:00 am at 90 km/h. What time does it arrive?
   - A) 11:00 am | B) 11:30 am | **C) 12:00 pm** | D) 12:30 pm
   - *Time = 270 ÷ 90 = 3 hours. Arrives at 12:00 pm.*

### SPEED, DISTANCE & TIME (Q109–150)

109. Convert 25 m/s to km/h.
   - A) 72 km/h | B) 80 km/h | C) 85 km/h | **D) 90 km/h**
   - *25 × 3.6 = 90 km/h.*

110. A snail moves at 0.03 km/h. How far in 2 hours (in metres)?
   - A) 30 m | B) 45 m | **C) 60 m** | D) 90 m
   - *0.03 × 2 = 0.06 km = 60 m.*

111. Ali cycles from home to school (4.5 km) in 15 minutes. What is his speed?
   - A) 12 km/h | B) 15 km/h | **C) 18 km/h** | D) 20 km/h
   - *15 min = 0.25 h. Speed = 4.5 ÷ 0.25 = 18 km/h.*

112. A bus travels 45 km at 60 km/h. How many minutes does the journey take?
   - A) 30 min | B) 35 min | C) 40 min | **D) 45 min**
   - *Time = 45 ÷ 60 = 0.75 h = 45 min.*

113. A car and a bus start from the same point. The car travels at 80 km/h and the bus at 60 km/h. After 2 hours, how far apart are they?
   - A) 20 km | B) 30 km | **C) 40 km** | D) 50 km
   - *Car: 160 km. Bus: 120 km. Difference = 40 km.*

114. A man walks at 4 km/h for 30 min then jogs at 8 km/h for 30 min. Find the total distance.
   - A) 4 km | B) 5 km | **C) 6 km** | D) 8 km
   - *Walk: 4 × 0.5 = 2 km. Jog: 8 × 0.5 = 4 km. Total = 6 km.*

115. A man walks 2 km at 4 km/h then jogs 4 km at 8 km/h. Find his average speed.
   - A) 5 km/h | **B) 6 km/h** | C) 6.5 km/h | D) 7 km/h
   - *Time walk = 0.5 h. Time jog = 0.5 h. Total = 6 km in 1 h. Avg = 6 km/h.*

116. How long does it take to walk 3.6 km at a speed of 1.2 m/s?
   - A) 30 min | B) 40 min | **C) 50 min** | D) 60 min
   - *3.6 km = 3600 m. Time = 3600 ÷ 1.2 = 3000 s = 50 min.*

117. The distance from Woodlands to Jurong is 30 km. If an MRT averages 40 km/h, how long is the journey?
   - A) 30 min | B) 40 min | **C) 45 min** | D) 50 min
   - *Time = 30 ÷ 40 = 0.75 h = 45 min.*

118. A 200 m long train passes a pole in 10 seconds. What is the speed of the train in km/h?
   - A) 60 km/h | B) 68 km/h | **C) 72 km/h** | D) 80 km/h
   - *Speed = 200/10 = 20 m/s = 20 × 3.6 = 72 km/h.*

119. Two cars travel towards each other from towns 300 km apart. Car A goes 70 km/h and Car B goes 80 km/h. When do they meet?
   - A) 1 h | B) 1.5 h | **C) 2 h** | D) 2.5 h
   - *Combined speed = 150 km/h. Time = 300 ÷ 150 = 2 hours.*

120. A student leaves home at 7:15 am and arrives at school 3.6 km away at 7:45 am. What was his average speed?
   - A) 5.4 km/h | B) 6 km/h | **C) 7.2 km/h** | D) 8 km/h
   - *Time = 30 min = 0.5 h. Speed = 3.6 ÷ 0.5 = 7.2 km/h.*

121. A bus travels the first half of a 120 km journey at 40 km/h and the second half at 60 km/h. Find the average speed.
   - A) 45 km/h | **B) 48 km/h** | C) 50 km/h | D) 52 km/h
   - *Time 1 = 60/40 = 1.5 h. Time 2 = 60/60 = 1 h. Total = 120 km in 2.5 h. Avg = 48 km/h.*

122. Convert 108 km/h to m/s.
   - A) 25 m/s | B) 28 m/s | **C) 30 m/s** | D) 36 m/s
   - *108 ÷ 3.6 = 30 m/s.*

123. A boat travels 24 km upstream at 6 km/h and returns at 12 km/h. What is the average speed for the round trip?
   - **A) 8 km/h** | B) 9 km/h | C) 10 km/h | D) 12 km/h
   - *Time up = 24/6 = 4 h. Time down = 24/12 = 2 h. Total = 48 km in 6 h. Avg = 8 km/h.*

124. A delivery rider travels 15 km in 20 minutes. What is his speed in km/h?
   - A) 40 km/h | B) 42 km/h | **C) 45 km/h** | D) 50 km/h
   - *20 min = 1/3 h. Speed = 15 ÷ (1/3) = 45 km/h.*

125. Two MRT stations are 2.5 km apart. A train takes 3 minutes between them. What is the speed in km/h?
   - A) 40 km/h | B) 45 km/h | C) 48 km/h | **D) 50 km/h**
   - *3 min = 1/20 h. Speed = 2.5 ÷ (1/20) = 50 km/h.*

126. A car leaves Town A at 8 am travelling at 60 km/h. Another car leaves Town A at 9 am at 80 km/h. At what time does the second car catch up?
   - A) 11 am | B) 11:30 am | **C) 12 pm** | D) 12:30 pm
   - *At 9 am, first car is 60 km ahead. Closing speed = 80 − 60 = 20 km/h. Time = 60/20 = 3 h. Catches up at 12 pm.*

127. A runner completes a 2.4 km NAPFA run in 12 minutes. What is her speed in km/h?
   - A) 10 km/h | **B) 12 km/h** | C) 14 km/h | D) 16 km/h
   - *12 min = 0.2 h. Speed = 2.4 ÷ 0.2 = 12 km/h.*

128. Express 54 km/h in m/s.
   - A) 10 m/s | B) 12 m/s | **C) 15 m/s** | D) 18 m/s
   - *54 ÷ 3.6 = 15 m/s.*

129. A car travels 100 km at 50 km/h and then 100 km at 100 km/h. What is the average speed?
   - A) 62.5 km/h | **B) 66.7 km/h** | C) 70 km/h | D) 75 km/h
   - *Time 1 = 2 h. Time 2 = 1 h. Total = 200 km in 3 h. Avg = 66.7 km/h.*

130. Simplify 36 : 48 : 60.
   - **A) 3 : 4 : 5** | B) 6 : 8 : 10 | C) 9 : 12 : 15 | D) 12 : 16 : 20
   - *HCF of 36, 48, 60 is 12. 36/12 : 48/12 : 60/12 = 3 : 4 : 5.*

131. A mixture uses milk and water in the ratio 3 : 2. How much milk is in 500 ml of mixture?
   - A) 200 ml | B) 250 ml | **C) 300 ml** | D) 350 ml
   - *Milk = 3/5 × 500 = 300 ml.*

132. If a : b = 3 : 4 and b : c = 2 : 5, find a : b : c.
   - A) 3 : 4 : 5 | **B) 3 : 4 : 10** | C) 6 : 8 : 10 | D) 6 : 8 : 20
   - *Make b same: a : b = 3 : 4 and b : c = 4 : 10 (multiply second by 2). So a : b : c = 3 : 4 : 10.*

133. Divide $600 in the ratio 1 : 2 : 3.
   - **A) $100, $200, $300** | B) $120, $180, $300 | C) $150, $200, $250 | D) $200, $200, $200
   - *Total = 6 parts. $100, $200, $300.*

134. A cyclist takes 45 minutes to travel from Punggol to Tampines (15 km). What is the average speed?
   - A) 15 km/h | B) 18 km/h | **C) 20 km/h** | D) 25 km/h
   - *45 min = 0.75 h. Speed = 15 ÷ 0.75 = 20 km/h.*

135. If 12 workers finish a project in 15 days, how many workers are needed to finish in 10 days?
   - A) 14 | B) 16 | **C) 18** | D) 20
   - *Inverse proportion. 12 × 15 = 180. 180 ÷ 10 = 18 workers.*

136. An express bus travels at 80 km/h. A normal bus travels at 50 km/h. Both leave at the same time. After 2 hours, how far apart are they?
   - A) 40 km | B) 50 km | **C) 60 km** | D) 70 km
   - *Difference in speed = 30 km/h. In 2 h: 30 × 2 = 60 km apart.*

137. A recipe for 6 people needs 450 g of flour. How much flour for 10 people?
   - A) 650 g | B) 700 g | **C) 750 g** | D) 800 g
   - *Per person = 75 g. For 10: 75 × 10 = 750 g.*

138. A car uses 6.5 litres per 100 km. How much petrol for a 260 km trip?
   - A) 14.5 L | B) 15.6 L | **C) 16.9 L** | D) 18.2 L
   - *6.5/100 × 260 = 16.9 litres.*

139. Convert 5 m/s to km/h.
   - A) 15 km/h | B) 16 km/h | C) 17 km/h | **D) 18 km/h**
   - *5 × 3.6 = 18 km/h.*

140. Simplify ⅔ : ⅘.
   - **A) 5 : 6** | B) 6 : 5 | C) 10 : 12 | D) 3 : 4
   - *Multiply by 15: 10 : 12. Simplify by 2: 5 : 6.*

141. A map scale is 1 : 100,000. Two places are 3.5 cm apart on the map. Find the actual distance.
   - **A) 3.5 km** | B) 5 km | C) 7 km | D) 35 km
   - *3.5 × 100,000 = 350,000 cm = 3500 m = 3.5 km.*

142. It costs $2.40 to send 3 parcels. How much for 10 parcels?
   - A) $6.00 | B) $7.00 | **C) $8.00** | D) $9.00
   - *1 parcel = $0.80. 10 parcels = $8.00.*

143. If 8 litres of paint covers 40 m², how many litres for 65 m²?
   - A) 10 L | B) 12 L | **C) 13 L** | D) 15 L
   - *1 L covers 5 m². 65 ÷ 5 = 13 L.*

144. A cheetah runs at 30 m/s. Express this in km/h.
   - A) 90 km/h | B) 100 km/h | **C) 108 km/h** | D) 120 km/h
   - *30 × 3.6 = 108 km/h.*

145. Two places are 450 km apart. A train leaves at 10 am at 120 km/h and another leaves the opposite end at 10 am at 80 km/h. When do they meet?
   - A) 12:00 pm | **B) 12:15 pm** | C) 12:30 pm | D) 12:45 pm
   - *Combined speed = 200 km/h. Time = 450/200 = 2.25 h = 2 h 15 min. Meet at 12:15 pm.*

146. The ratio of boys to girls in a school is 7 : 8. There are 120 more girls than boys. How many students are there?
   - A) 1680 | B) 1780 | **C) 1800** | D) 1920
   - *Difference = 1 part = 120. Total = 15 parts = 15 × 120 = 1800.*

147. Water flows into a pool at 12 L/min and drains out at 8 L/min. How long to fill a 600 L pool?
   - A) 50 min | B) 100 min | C) 120 min | **D) 150 min**
   - *Net rate = 4 L/min. Time = 600 ÷ 4 = 150 min.*

148. A train 150 m long passes a 350 m platform in 25 seconds. What is the speed in km/h?
   - A) 60 km/h | B) 68 km/h | **C) 72 km/h** | D) 80 km/h
   - *Total distance = 150 + 350 = 500 m. Speed = 500/25 = 20 m/s = 72 km/h.*

149. Divide 150 cm of ribbon in the ratio 2 : 3 : 5. Find the longest piece.
   - A) 30 cm | B) 45 cm | C) 50 cm | **D) 75 cm**
   - *Total = 10 parts. Longest = 5/10 × 150 = 75 cm.*

150. A 400 m race is completed in 50 seconds. What is the average speed in m/s?
   - A) 6 m/s | B) 7 m/s | **C) 8 m/s** | D) 9 m/s
   - *400 ÷ 50 = 8 m/s.*

---

## Topic 10: Geometry & Angles
*Points, lines, planes, angle properties, parallel line angles* — 150 questions

### ANGLE TYPES (Q1–38)

1. An angle of 45° is classified as:
   - **A) Acute** | B) Right | C) Obtuse | D) Reflex
   - *An acute angle is between 0° and 90°. Since 45° is in this range, it is acute.*

2. An angle of 90° is classified as:
   - A) Acute | **B) Right** | C) Obtuse | D) Straight
   - *An angle of exactly 90° is a right angle.*

3. An angle of 135° is classified as:
   - A) Acute | B) Right | **C) Obtuse** | D) Reflex
   - *An obtuse angle is between 90° and 180°. Since 135° is in this range, it is obtuse.*

4. An angle of 200° is classified as:
   - A) Obtuse | B) Straight | **C) Reflex** | D) Complete turn
   - *A reflex angle is between 180° and 360°. Since 200° is in this range, it is reflex.*

5. An angle of 180° is called a:
   - A) Right angle | B) Obtuse angle | **C) Straight angle** | D) Reflex angle
   - *An angle of exactly 180° is a straight angle.*

6. An angle of 360° is called a:
   - A) Straight angle | B) Reflex angle | **C) Complete turn** | D) Full reflex
   - *An angle of exactly 360° is a complete turn (or full turn).*

7. Which of the following is an acute angle?
   - **A) 88°** | B) 90° | C) 91° | D) 180°
   - *88° is less than 90°, so it is acute.*

8. Which of the following is an obtuse angle?
   - A) 45° | B) 89° | C) 90° | **D) 120°**
   - *120° is between 90° and 180°, so it is obtuse.*

9. Which of the following is a reflex angle?
   - A) 170° | B) 180° | **C) 190°** | D) 90°
   - *190° is between 180° and 360°, so it is reflex.*

10. The complement of 30° is:
   - A) 30° | **B) 60°** | C) 150° | D) 330°
   - *Complementary angles add to 90°. Complement = 90° − 30° = 60°.*

11. The supplement of 70° is:
   - A) 20° | B) 70° | **C) 110°** | D) 290°
   - *Supplementary angles add to 180°. Supplement = 180° − 70° = 110°.*

12. The complement of 55° is:
   - A) 25° | **B) 35°** | C) 45° | D) 125°
   - *90° − 55° = 35°.*

13. The supplement of 135° is:
   - A) 35° | **B) 45°** | C) 55° | D) 225°
   - *180° − 135° = 45°.*

14. Two angles are complementary. One is 38°. Find the other.
   - A) 42° | B) 48° | **C) 52°** | D) 142°
   - *90° − 38° = 52°.*

15. Two angles are supplementary. One is 63°. Find the other.
   - A) 27° | B) 63° | **C) 117°** | D) 297°
   - *180° − 63° = 117°.*

16. Which pair of angles are complementary?
   - A) 40° and 140° | **B) 55° and 35°** | C) 60° and 60° | D) 90° and 90°
   - *55° + 35° = 90°. They are complementary.*

17. Which pair of angles are supplementary?
   - A) 45° and 45° | B) 60° and 60° | **C) 75° and 105°** | D) 80° and 80°
   - *75° + 105° = 180°. They are supplementary.*

18. An angle is twice its complement. Find the angle.
   - A) 30° | B) 45° | **C) 60°** | D) 90°
   - *Let angle = x. Complement = 90 − x. x = 2(90 − x). x = 180 − 2x. 3x = 180. x = 60°.*

19. An angle is 4 times its supplement. Find the angle.
   - A) 36° | B) 72° | C) 108° | **D) 144°**
   - *Let angle = x. Supplement = 180 − x. x = 4(180 − x). x = 720 − 4x. 5x = 720. x = 144°.*

20. What type of angle does a corner of a square have?
   - A) Acute | **B) Right** | C) Obtuse | D) Reflex
   - *Each corner of a square is 90°, which is a right angle.*

21. The hands of a clock at 3 o'clock form an angle of:
   - A) 60° | **B) 90°** | C) 120° | D) 180°
   - *At 3 o'clock, the hands form a 90° angle (right angle).*

22. The hands of a clock at 6 o'clock form an angle of:
   - A) 90° | B) 120° | C) 150° | **D) 180°**
   - *At 6 o'clock, the hands form a straight angle of 180°.*

23. The hands of a clock at 4 o'clock form an angle of:
   - A) 90° | B) 100° | C) 110° | **D) 120°**
   - *Each hour = 30°. At 4 o'clock: 4 × 30° = 120°.*

24. An angle of 0.5° is classified as:
   - A) Zero angle | **B) Acute** | C) Right | D) Obtuse
   - *0.5° is between 0° and 90°, so it is acute.*

25. An angle of 179° is classified as:
   - A) Acute | B) Right | **C) Obtuse** | D) Reflex
   - *179° is between 90° and 180°, so it is obtuse.*

26. An angle of 181° is classified as:
   - A) Obtuse | B) Straight | **C) Reflex** | D) Complete turn
   - *181° is between 180° and 360°, so it is reflex.*

27. An angle of 359° is classified as:
   - A) Obtuse | B) Straight | **C) Reflex** | D) Complete turn
   - *359° is between 180° and 360°, so it is reflex.*

28. The reflex angle corresponding to 60° is:
   - A) 120° | B) 240° | **C) 300°** | D) 320°
   - *Reflex angle = 360° − 60° = 300°.*

29. The reflex angle corresponding to 150° is:
   - A) 30° | B) 150° | **C) 210°** | D) 330°
   - *Reflex angle = 360° − 150° = 210°.*

30. If two angles are supplementary and equal, each is:
   - A) 45° | B) 60° | **C) 90°** | D) 180°
   - *2x = 180°, so x = 90°.*

31. If two angles are complementary and equal, each is:
   - A) 30° | **B) 45°** | C) 60° | D) 90°
   - *2x = 90°, so x = 45°.*

32. An angle is 20° more than its complement. Find the angle.
   - A) 35° | B) 45° | **C) 55°** | D) 65°
   - *x = (90 − x) + 20. 2x = 110. x = 55°.*

33. An angle is 30° less than its supplement. Find the angle.
   - A) 65° | B) 70° | **C) 75°** | D) 80°
   - *x = (180 − x) − 30. 2x = 150. x = 75°.*

34. How many degrees does the minute hand of a clock turn in 20 minutes?
   - A) 60° | B) 90° | **C) 120°** | D) 180°
   - *The minute hand turns 360° in 60 min. In 20 min: 20/60 × 360° = 120°.*

35. How many degrees does the hour hand turn in 2 hours?
   - A) 30° | B) 45° | **C) 60°** | D) 90°
   - *The hour hand turns 360° in 12 h. In 2 h: 2/12 × 360° = 60°.*

36. What is the angle between North and East on a compass?
   - A) 45° | B) 60° | **C) 90°** | D) 180°
   - *N to E is a quarter turn = 90°.*

37. What is the angle between North and South-West on a compass?
   - A) 135° | B) 180° | **C) 225°** | D) 270°
   - *N to SW (clockwise) = 225°.*

38. An angle and its supplement differ by 40°. Find the larger angle.
   - A) 70° | B) 100° | **C) 110°** | D) 120°
   - *x + (x − 40) = 180. 2x = 220. x = 110°.*

### ANGLES ON A LINE & AT A POINT (Q39–76)

39. Two angles on a straight line are x° and 130°. Find x.
   - A) 30 | B) 40 | **C) 50** | D) 60
   - *Angles on a straight line sum to 180°. x = 180 − 130 = 50°.*

40. Two angles on a straight line are 75° and y°. Find y.
   - A) 95 | B) 100 | **C) 105** | D) 115
   - *y = 180 − 75 = 105°.*

41. Three angles on a straight line are 40°, 60° and z°. Find z.
   - A) 60 | B) 70 | **C) 80** | D) 90
   - *z = 180 − 40 − 60 = 80°.*

42. Angles on a straight line are 2x° and 3x°. Find x.
   - A) 30 | **B) 36** | C) 40 | D) 45
   - *2x + 3x = 180. 5x = 180. x = 36.*

43. Angles on a straight line are (x + 10)° and (2x + 20)°. Find x.
   - A) 40 | B) 45 | **C) 50** | D) 55
   - *(x + 10) + (2x + 20) = 180. 3x + 30 = 180. 3x = 150. x = 50.*

44. Two angles on a straight line are in the ratio 2 : 3. Find the larger angle.
   - A) 72° | B) 90° | **C) 108°** | D) 120°
   - *Total = 180°. Larger = 3/5 × 180 = 108°.*

45. Two angles on a straight line are in the ratio 1 : 5. Find the smaller angle.
   - A) 25° | **B) 30°** | C) 36° | D) 45°
   - *Smaller = 1/6 × 180 = 30°.*

46. Three angles on a straight line are x°, 2x° and 3x°. Find x.
   - A) 20 | B) 25 | **C) 30** | D) 36
   - *x + 2x + 3x = 180. 6x = 180. x = 30.*

47. Angles on a straight line are 55°, x° and 65°. Find x.
   - A) 50 | B) 55 | **C) 60** | D) 65
   - *x = 180 − 55 − 65 = 60°.*

48. Three angles at a point are 120°, 150° and x°. Find x.
   - A) 60 | B) 80 | **C) 90** | D) 100
   - *Angles at a point sum to 360°. x = 360 − 120 − 150 = 90°.*

49. Four angles at a point are 80°, 90°, 100° and x°. Find x.
   - A) 70 | B) 80 | **C) 90** | D) 100
   - *x = 360 − 80 − 90 − 100 = 90°.*

50. Angles at a point are 2x°, 3x° and 5x°. Find x.
   - A) 30 | **B) 36** | C) 40 | D) 45
   - *2x + 3x + 5x = 360. 10x = 360. x = 36.*

51. Two angles at a point are equal and the third angle is 120°. Find each equal angle.
   - A) 100° | B) 110° | **C) 120°** | D) 130°
   - *2x + 120 = 360. 2x = 240. x = 120°.*

52. Three angles at a point are in the ratio 2 : 3 : 4. Find the smallest.
   - A) 60° | **B) 80°** | C) 100° | D) 120°
   - *Total = 9 parts. Smallest = 2/9 × 360 = 80°.*

53. Four angles at a point are in the ratio 1 : 2 : 3 : 3. Find the largest.
   - A) 40° | B) 80° | C) 100° | **D) 120°**
   - *Total = 9 parts. Largest = 3/9 × 360 = 120°.*

54. Five equal angles meet at a point. Find each angle.
   - A) 60° | **B) 72°** | C) 75° | D) 90°
   - *360° ÷ 5 = 72°.*

55. Six equal angles meet at a point. Find each angle.
   - A) 45° | B) 50° | C) 55° | **D) 60°**
   - *360° ÷ 6 = 60°.*

56. Angles at a point are 70°, 2x°, 110° and x°. Find x.
   - A) 50 | B) 55 | **C) 60** | D) 65
   - *70 + 2x + 110 + x = 360. 3x + 180 = 360. 3x = 180. x = 60.*

57. Angles at a point are (3x − 10)°, (2x + 20)° and (x + 50)°. Find x.
   - A) 40 | B) 45 | **C) 50** | D) 55
   - *(3x − 10) + (2x + 20) + (x + 50) = 360. 6x + 60 = 360. 6x = 300. x = 50.*

58. Two straight lines intersect. If one angle is 40°, the angle adjacent to it is:
   - A) 40° | B) 50° | C) 130° | **D) 140°**
   - *Adjacent angles on a straight line: 180° − 40° = 140°.*

59. Angles on a straight line are 3x° and (x + 40)°. Find the larger angle.
   - **A) 105°** | B) 108° | C) 110° | D) 120°
   - *3x + x + 40 = 180. 4x = 140. x = 35. Larger = 3(35) = 105°.*

60. Angles at a point are 5x°, 4x°, 3x° and 2x°. Find the largest angle (in degrees).
   - A) 100.7° | B) 108° | C) 120.9° | **D) 128.6°**
   - *5x + 4x + 3x + 2x = 360. 14x = 360. x ≈ 25.71. Largest = 5 × 25.71 ≈ 128.6°.*

61. On a straight line, angles are (2x + 15)° and (3x − 5)°. Find x.
   - A) 30 | B) 32 | **C) 34** | D) 36
   - *(2x + 15) + (3x − 5) = 180. 5x + 10 = 180. 5x = 170. x = 34.*

62. Three angles on a straight line are equal. What is each?
   - A) 45° | B) 50° | C) 55° | **D) 60°**
   - *3x = 180. x = 60°.*

63. Angles at a point are 145°, x° and 2x°. Find x.
   - A) 65.5° | **B) 71.7°** | C) 72° | D) 73°
   - *145 + x + 2x = 360. 3x = 215. x ≈ 71.7°.*

64. Two angles on a straight line differ by 50°. Find the smaller angle.
   - A) 55° | B) 60° | **C) 65°** | D) 70°
   - *x + (x + 50) = 180. 2x = 130. x = 65°.*

65. Four angles at a point are 2a°, 3a°, 4a° and 90°. Find a.
   - A) 25 | B) 27 | **C) 30** | D) 35
   - *2a + 3a + 4a + 90 = 360. 9a = 270. a = 30.*

66. On a straight line, the angles are x°, (x + 20)° and (x + 40)°. Find x.
   - A) 35 | **B) 40** | C) 45 | D) 50
   - *x + (x+20) + (x+40) = 180. 3x + 60 = 180. 3x = 120. x = 40.*

67. Two straight lines intersect. One angle is 72°. The vertically opposite angle is:
   - A) 18° | **B) 72°** | C) 108° | D) 288°
   - *Vertically opposite angles are equal. The answer is 72°.*

68. Two straight lines intersect. One angle is 115°. The vertically opposite angle is:
   - A) 65° | **B) 115°** | C) 155° | D) 245°
   - *Vertically opposite angles are equal. The answer is 115°.*

69. Two straight lines intersect. One angle is 50°. Find the adjacent angle.
   - A) 50° | B) 100° | **C) 130°** | D) 140°
   - *Adjacent angles on a straight line: 180° − 50° = 130°.*

70. Two straight lines intersect. One angle is 35°. Find all four angles.
   - **A) 35°, 35°, 145°, 145°** | B) 35°, 55°, 145°, 125° | C) 35°, 145°, 35°, 145° | D) 35°, 145°, 55°, 125°
   - *Vertically opposite: 35° and 35°. Adjacent: 180° − 35° = 145° each.*

71. Two straight lines intersect forming angles x° and (3x − 20)°. If these are vertically opposite, find x.
   - A) 5 | **B) 10** | C) 15 | D) 20
   - *Vertically opposite angles are equal: x = 3x − 20. 20 = 2x. x = 10.*

72. Two straight lines cross. One angle is (2x + 10)° and the adjacent angle is (3x − 30)°. Find x.
   - A) 36 | B) 38 | **C) 40** | D) 42
   - *Adjacent angles: (2x + 10) + (3x − 30) = 180. 5x − 20 = 180. 5x = 200. x = 40.*

73. Two straight lines cross. One angle is 4x° and its vertically opposite angle is (x + 60)°. Find x.
   - A) 15 | B) 18 | **C) 20** | D) 25
   - *Vertically opposite: 4x = x + 60. 3x = 60. x = 20.*

74. Two lines intersect. One pair of vertically opposite angles are each 90°. What are the other pair?
   - A) 45° each | B) 60° each | **C) 90° each** | D) 180° each
   - *If one pair is 90°, adjacent = 180° − 90° = 90°. All four angles are 90°.*

75. Three lines meet at a point. One angle is 40°, the vertically opposite is also 40°. Another angle is 70°. Find the angle adjacent to the 70°.
   - **A) 70°** | B) 100° | C) 110° | D) 140°
   - *With 3 lines at a point: 6 angles. The vertically opposite angle to 70° is also 70°. Remaining 2 angles = (360 − 80 − 140) ÷ 2 = 70° each.*

76. Two lines cross. Angle A = 55°. Angle B is adjacent to A. Angle C is vertically opposite to B. Find C.
   - A) 55° | B) 65° | C) 115° | **D) 125°**
   - *B = 180 − 55 = 125°. C is vertically opposite to B, so C = 125°.*

### VERTICALLY OPPOSITE ANGLES (Q77–108)

77. Two straight lines intersect. If one angle is x° and the adjacent angle is (2x)°, find x.
   - A) 45 | B) 50 | C) 55 | **D) 60**
   - *x + 2x = 180. 3x = 180. x = 60.*

78. Two straight lines cross. The angles formed are x°, y°, x° and y°. If x − y = 30°, find x.
   - A) 95° | B) 100° | **C) 105°** | D) 110°
   - *x + y = 180 and x − y = 30. Adding: 2x = 210. x = 105°.*

79. Two lines intersect. One angle is 3a° and the vertically opposite is (a + 50)°. Find a.
   - A) 20 | **B) 25** | C) 30 | D) 35
   - *3a = a + 50. 2a = 50. a = 25.*

80. Two lines cross. An angle is (5x − 20)° and its vertically opposite angle is (3x + 16)°. Find x.
   - A) 14 | B) 16 | **C) 18** | D) 20
   - *5x − 20 = 3x + 16. 2x = 36. x = 18.*

81. Two straight lines cross. One angle is 2y° and the adjacent angle is (y + 60)°. Find y.
   - A) 35 | **B) 40** | C) 45 | D) 50
   - *2y + y + 60 = 180. 3y = 120. y = 40.*

82. Two lines cross at a point. One angle is 48°. How many of the four angles are acute?
   - A) 1 | **B) 2** | C) 3 | D) 4
   - *Angles: 48°, 132°, 48°, 132°. Two are acute (48°).*

83. Two intersecting lines form an angle of 90°. What can you say about the lines?
   - A) They are parallel | **B) They are perpendicular** | C) They are curved | D) They are skew
   - *Lines meeting at 90° are perpendicular.*

84. Two lines intersect. One angle is (x + 35)° and the vertically opposite angle is (2x + 5)°. Find x.
   - A) 25 | **B) 30** | C) 35 | D) 40
   - *x + 35 = 2x + 5. 30 = x. x = 30.*

85. At an intersection, the angle between two roads is 65°. What is the obtuse angle at the same intersection?
   - A) 105° | B) 110° | **C) 115°** | D) 125°
   - *180° − 65° = 115°.*

86. Two straight lines intersect forming angles (4p)° and (p + 45)°. If they are adjacent, find p.
   - A) 25 | **B) 27** | C) 30 | D) 35
   - *4p + p + 45 = 180. 5p = 135. p = 27.*

87. Two lines cross. One angle is (3m − 12)° and the adjacent angle is (2m + 7)°. Find the value of the larger angle.
   - A) 81° | B) 93° | **C) 99°** | D) 111°
   - *(3m − 12) + (2m + 7) = 180. 5m − 5 = 180. 5m = 185. m = 37. Angles: 3(37) − 12 = 99° and 2(37) + 7 = 81°. The larger angle is 99°.*

88. Lines AB and CD intersect at O. Angle AOC = 125°. Find angle BOD.
   - A) 55° | B) 65° | **C) 125°** | D) 235°
   - *Angle BOD is vertically opposite to angle AOC. So angle BOD = 125°.*

89. Lines PQ and RS intersect at O. Angle POR = 47°. Find angle QOS.
   - A) 43° | **B) 47°** | C) 133° | D) 313°
   - *Angle QOS is vertically opposite to angle POR. So angle QOS = 47°.*

90. Lines AB and CD cross at O. Angle AOC = (2x + 14)° and angle BOD = (3x − 16)°. Find angle AOC.
   - A) 60° | B) 68° | **C) 74°** | D) 78°
   - *Vertically opposite: 2x + 14 = 3x − 16. x = 30. Angle AOC = 2(30) + 14 = 74°.*

91. Two lines intersect. If one angle is twice the vertically opposite angle, this is:
   - A) Always true | B) Only if both are 90° | **C) Impossible** | D) Only for right angles
   - *Vertically opposite angles are always equal. One cannot be twice the other (unless both are 0°, which isn't a real intersection).*

92. At a road junction, the acute angle between two roads is 38°. Find the reflex angle at the junction.
   - A) 142° | B) 218° | **C) 322°** | D) 342°
   - *Reflex angle = 360° − 38° = 322°.*

93. Two lines intersect. Three of the angles are 55°, 125°, and 55°. Find the fourth angle.
   - A) 55° | B) 105° | C) 115° | **D) 125°**
   - *Total = 360°. Fourth angle = 360 − 55 − 125 − 55 = 125°.*

94. Lines intersect at O forming angles p°, q°, p° and q°. If p = 3q, find p.
   - A) 120° | B) 130° | **C) 135°** | D) 140°
   - *p + q = 180. 3q + q = 180. 4q = 180. q = 45. p = 135°.*

95. Two straight lines cross. The sum of a pair of adjacent angles is:
   - A) 90° | **B) 180°** | C) 270° | D) 360°
   - *Adjacent angles on a straight line always sum to 180°.*

96. Two lines intersect. One of the angles is x°. Express the adjacent angle in terms of x.
   - A) x° | B) (90 − x)° | **C) (180 − x)°** | D) (360 − x)°
   - *Adjacent angles on a straight line sum to 180°. Adjacent = (180 − x)°.*

97. Two straight lines intersect at right angles. All four angles are:
   - A) 45° each | B) 60° each | **C) 90° each** | D) 180° each
   - *If lines are perpendicular, all four angles at the intersection are 90°.*

98. Two lines cross. One angle is (6x − 30)° and its vertically opposite angle is (4x + 10)°. Find the angle.
   - A) 80° | B) 86° | **C) 90°** | D) 96°
   - *6x − 30 = 4x + 10. 2x = 40. x = 20. Angle = 6(20) − 30 = 90°.*

99. A transversal crosses two parallel lines. A corresponding angle is 70°. Find the other corresponding angle.
   - **A) 70°** | B) 80° | C) 100° | D) 110°
   - *Corresponding angles are equal when lines are parallel. The answer is 70°.*

100. A transversal crosses two parallel lines. An alternate angle is 55°. Find the other alternate angle.
   - A) 35° | **B) 55°** | C) 125° | D) 145°
   - *Alternate angles are equal when lines are parallel. The answer is 55°.*

101. A transversal crosses two parallel lines. One co-interior angle is 65°. Find the other.
   - A) 65° | B) 105° | **C) 115°** | D) 125°
   - *Co-interior angles sum to 180°. Other = 180° − 65° = 115°.*

102. Parallel lines are cut by a transversal. One angle is 110°. The corresponding angle is:
   - A) 70° | B) 80° | C) 100° | **D) 110°**
   - *Corresponding angles are equal: 110°.*

103. Parallel lines are cut by a transversal. One angle is 130°. The alternate angle is:
   - A) 50° | B) 60° | **C) 130°** | D) 140°
   - *Alternate angles are equal: 130°.*

104. Parallel lines cut by a transversal. Angle a = 75° (co-interior with angle b). Find b.
   - A) 75° | B) 95° | **C) 105°** | D) 115°
   - *Co-interior angles sum to 180°. b = 180° − 75° = 105°.*

105. Lines AB ∥ CD. A transversal makes an angle of 48° with AB. The corresponding angle with CD is:
   - A) 42° | **B) 48°** | C) 132° | D) 138°
   - *Corresponding angles: 48°.*

106. Lines AB ∥ CD. A transversal makes an angle of 62° with AB. The alternate angle at CD is:
